Su3-Tou5 Heng5-Toan7

Te7 1 ChiuN

1) Chhin-ai3 e5 The5-o-hui-lo5 a3:
Ti7 goa2 e5 thau5 chit8 pun2 chheh, goa2 u7 sia2 Ia5-sou chu7 khai-si2 I e5 kang-chok i2-lai5 sou2 cho3, sou2 ka3-si7 it-chhe3 e5 tai7-chi3,  2) it-tit8 kau3 siu7 geng5-chiap khi3 thiN-teng2 hit jit8. Siu7 geng5-chiap i2-cheng5, I eng7 Seng3 Leng5 e5 tai7-leng5 ka3-si7 I sou2 keng2-soan2 e5 Su3-tou5.  3) I siu7-lan7 liau2-au7, si3-chap8 jit8 e5 tiong-kan, hian2-hian7 chin-che7 pai2 hou7 in khoaN3, eng7 chiong2-chiong2 e5 hong-hoat lai5 cheng3-beng5 I khak-sit8 teh oah8, ia7 kap in kong2-khi2 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok e5 tai7-chi3.  4) In chu7-chhan e5 si5, Ia5-sou hoan-hu3 in kong2: 몮M7-thang li7-khui Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, tioh8 tan2-hau7 Thian-hu7 sou2 eng3-un2 e5, chiu7-si7 Goa2 bat ka7 lin2 kong2 koe3 e5 in-su3.  5) Iok-han7 eng7 chui2 ka7 lang5 se2-le2, tan7-si7 koh bo5 kui2 jit8, lin2 ia7 e7 tit-tioh8 Seng3 Leng5 e5 se2-le2.몯

Ia5-sou seng-thian:
	6) In kap Ia5-sou chu7-chip8 e5 si5, mng7 I kong2: 몮Chu2 a3, Li2 boeh chai7 chit e5 si5 lai5 hoe5-hok8 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Ong5-kok si7 bo5?몯  7) Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2: 몮Si5-khek kap jit8-ki5, si7 Thian-hu7 ka-ti7 e5 koan5-peng3 sou2 teng7 e5, m7-si7 lin2 sou2 e7-tang3 chai-iaN2 e5.  8) Tan7-si7 Seng3 Leng5 kang3 loh8-lai5 lin2 mui2 chit8 e5 lang5 e5 si5, lin2 it-teng7 e7 tit-tioh8 tai7-leng5; peng7-chhiaN2 chai7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, choan5 Iu5-thai3 kap Sat-ma2-li7-a, it-tit8 kau3 thiN-piN hai2-kak, lin2 e7 lai5 ui7 Goa2 cho3 kian3-cheng3.몯  9) Chiah-e5 oe7 kong2 liau2-au7, chai7 in e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5, I chiu7 siu7 geng5-chiap seng-thian, u7 chit8 phian3 hun5 ka7 I chiap-khi3, in chiu7 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 I.
	10) In iau2 teh khoaN3 I seng-thian e5 si5, hut-jian5-kan u7 nng7 e5 chheng7 peh8-saN e5 lang5 lai5 khia7 ti7 in e5 piN-a,  11) tui3 in kong2: 몮Ka-li7-li7-lang5 a3, lin2 an3-choaN2 khia7 ti7 chia teh khoaN3 thiN? Li7-khui lin2 siu7 geng5-chiap seng-thian chit ui7 Ia5-sou, chhin-chhiuN7 lin2 khoaN3-kiN3 I seng-thian an2-ne, I ia7 an2-ne koh-chai3 tng2-lai5.몯

Iu5-tai7 e5 hou7-ke3-chia2:
	12) Jian5-au7 hiah-e5 Su3-tou5 chiu7 tui3 chit8 e5 kio3-cho3 Kan-na2-soaN hia tng2-khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2. Hit e5 soaN li7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 tai7-iok u7 poaN3 eng-li2 hng7. (몮PoaN3 eng-li2 hng7 si7 chai7 An-hioh-jit8 u7 in2-chun2 lang5 kiaN5 e5 lou7-theng5.")  13) In jip8-khi3 chhi7-lai7, chiu7 peh khit-khi3 in teh toa3 hit keng chhu3 e5 lau5-teng2 e5 pang5-keng. Hiah-e5 lang5 chiu7-si7 Pi2-tek, Iok-han7, Nga2-kok, An-tek-lek8, Hui-lek8 kap To-ma2, Pa-to-lo5-mai2 kap Ma2-thai3, A-lek8-hui e5 kiaN2 Nga2-kok, Se-lo5-ti2-tong2 e5 Se-bun5, kap Nga2-kok e5 kiaN2 Iu5-tai7.  14) Chiah-e5 lang5 chiu7 kap kui2-na7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, pau-ham5 Ia5-sou e5 bo2-chhin Ma2-li7-a i2-kip8 Ia5-sou e5 hiaN-ti7, cho3-hoe2 it-sim it-i3 ke3-siok8 ki5-to2.
	15) Bo5 kui2 jit8 au7, tai7-iok u7 chit8 pah ji7-chap8 e5 teh chu7-hoe7 e5 si5, Pi2-tek chiu7 khia7 khi2-lai5 tui3 hiah-e5 sin3-tou5 kong2:  16) 몮HiaN-ti7 a3, Seng3 Leng5 chioh Tai7-pit8 e5 chhui3, chai7 Seng3-keng-siong7 i7-gian5 Iu5-tai7 e7 chhoa7 lang5 lai5 liah8 Ia5-sou. Chiah-e5 oe7 eng-kai tioh8 eng3-giam7.  17) Iu5-tai7 pun2-lai5 si7 goan2 chit tin7 e5 chit8 e5, ia7 u7 tit-tioh8 kap goan2 cho3-hoe2 kang-chok e5 chit-hun7.몯
	18) (Iu5-tai7 eng7 i cho3 put-gi7 lai5 tit-tioh8 e5 chiN5-chai5 be2 chit8 te3 te7, to3-thau5-chai loh8-khi3 si2 toa3 hia; pak-tou2 piak-khui, tng5-a2-tou7 long2 lau5 chhut-lai5.  19) Toa3 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 lang5 long2 chai-iaN2 chit hang7 tai7-chi3, sou2-i2 chiau3 in te7-hng e5 oe7 chiong hit te3 te7 kio3-cho3 A-kek-tai7-ma2, i3-su3 chiu7-si7 몮Hoeh te7.몯)
20) 몮In-ui7 Si-phian e5 chheh u7 sia2 kong2: 몬Tioh8 hou7 i e5 chhu3 hong-hoe3, Tioh8 hou7 hit keng bo5 lang5 khia7-khi2.몭 Ia7 u7 sia2 kong2: 몬Tioh8 hou7 pat8-lang5 lai5 tai7-the3 i e5 chit-ui7.몭몯
	21-22) 몮Sou2-i2 tioh8 tui3 hiah-e5 thau5 kau3 boe2 kap lan2 cho3-tin7 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan, soan2 chit8 e5 lai5 kap goan2 tau3-tin7 lai5 cho3 Chu2 Ia5-sou hok8-hoat8 e5 kian3-cheng3-jin5. Hit e5 lang5 eng-kai tioh8 tui3 Iok-han7 e5 se2-le2 khai-si2, it-tit8 kau3 Ia5-sou li7-khui lan2, siu7 geng5-chiap seng-thian hit jit8 ui5-chi2, long2 u7 kap goan2 cho3-tin7 e5.몯  23) Sou2-i2 in chiu7 the5-mia5 nng7 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 kio3-cho3 Pa-sat-pa, ia7 chheng-hou cho3 Iu5-su-tou e5 Iok-sek, i2-kip8 Ma2-the5-a.  24) In chiu7 ki5-to2 kong2: 몮Chu2 a3, Li2 chai-iaN2 cheng3-lang5 e5 sim. Kiu5 Li2 chi2-si7 chit nng7 e5 tiong-kan e5 tah chit8 e5 si7 Li2 keng2-soan2 e5,  25) boeh lai5 hou7 i cho3 Su3-tou5 hok8-bu7, lai5 chiap Iu5-tai7 e5 chit-hun7, in-ui7 Iu5-tai7 hong3-khi3 chit e5 chit-hun7, khi3 kiaN5 i ka-ti7 e5 lou7.몯  26) Jian5-au7, in chiu7 eng7 nng7 e5 mia5 cho3 khau-a2 lai5 thiu, khi3 thiu-tioh8 Ma2-the5-a; i chiu7 ka-jip8 khi3 hit tin7 chap8-it e5 Su3-tou5 e5 lai7-bin7.

Te7 2 ChiuN

Seng3 Leng5 e5 kang3-lim5:
	1) Gou7-sun5-cheh hit jit8 chit8-e7 kau3, cheng3-lang5 long2 chu7-chip8 cho3-hoe2 e5 si5,  2) hut-jian5-kan chhin-chhiuN7 thau3 toa7 hong e5 siaN tui3 thiN-teng2 lai5, chhiong-moa2 in teh che7 hit keng chhu3.  3) In chiu7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 hang7 chhin-chhiuN7 hoe2-chih8 e5 mih8-kiaN7 chhut-hian7, thoaN3-khui khi3, theng5 toa3 in mui2 chit8 e5 lang5 e5 teng2-bin7.  4) In chiu7 long2 chhiong-moa2 Seng3 Leng5, chiau3 Seng3 Leng5 siuN2-su3 hou7 in e5 leng5-lek8, khai-si2 kong2 pat8 kok e5 oe7-gi2.
	5) Hit e5 si5 u7 chit8 koa2 tui3 se3-kai3 kok kok lai5 e5 khian5-seng5 e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5, toa3 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.  6) In chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 chit e5 siaN, kui toa7 tin7 lang5 long2 chu7-chip8 oa2-lai5. In-ui7 Su3-tou5 teh kong2 e5 oe7-gi2, hou7 mui2 chit8 e5 teh thiaN e5 lang5, thiaN-tioh8 na2 chhin-chhiuN7 teh kong2 in e5 hong-gian5, in chiu7 toa7 tioh8-kiaN.  7) In tioh8-kiaN kam2-kak ki5-koai3, kong2: 몮Li2 khoaN3, chiah-e5 teh kong2-oe7 e5, kam2 m7-si7 long2 si7 Ka-li7-li7-lang5?  8) Si7 an3-choaN2 lan2 mui2 chit8 e5 lang5, na2 e7 long2 thiaN-kiN3 in teh kong2 lan2 ka-ti7 e5 hong-gian5?  9) Lan2 tui3 PhaN3-the5-a, Bi2-thai3, I2-lan5; tui3 Bi2-sou2-pho-tai7-bi2, Iu5-thai3 kap Ka-phaN3-to-ka; tui3 Pun2-tou kap A-se-a,  10) tui3 Hut-lu7-ka kap Pong5-hui-li7-a, tui3 Ai-kip8 kap oa2 Kou2-li7-nai7 e5 Lu7-pi2-a te7-khu; i2-kip8 tui3 Lo5-ma2 lai5 e5;  11) bo5-lun7 si7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 a2-si7 kai2-chong lai5 jip8 Iu5-thai3-kau3 e5 lang5; u7-e5 si7 tui3 Kek-li7-ti2 kap A-lat-pek lai5 e5 --- lan2 tai7-ke na2 e7 long2 thiaN in eng7 lan2 e5 hong-gian5 teh kong2 Siong7-chu2 sou2 cho3 ui2-tai7 e5 tai7-chi3!몯  12) Tai7-ke to tioh8-kiaN bok8-beng5 ki5-biau7, hou7-siong mng7 kong2: 몮Che si7 sim2-mih tai7-chi3?몯  13) Tan7-si7 ia7 u7 lang5 thi2-chhio3 in kong2, 몮Chiah-e5 lang5 teh chiu2-chui3!몯

Pi2-tek e5 kang2-to7:
	14) Pi2-tek chiu7 kap chap8-it ui7 Su3-tou5 khia7 khi2-lai5, toa7 siaN tui3 kun5-chiong3 kong2: 몮Iu5-thai3-lang5 kap toa3 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 it-chhe3 e5 lang5 a3! Lin2 tioh8 chai-iaN2 chit hang7 tai7-chi3, tioh8 chu3-i3 thiaN goa2 e5 oe7.  15) Lin2 siuN7 kong2 chiah-e5 lang5 teh chiu2-chui3, ki5-sit8 in m7-si7 teh chiu2-chui3; in-ui7 chim2-ma2 chiah chai2-khi2-si5 e5 kau2 tiam2 nia7-nia7.  16) Che chiaN3-si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 tai7-gian5-jin5 Iok-jiN2 sou2 kong2 e5:
17) 몬Siong7-chu2 kong2: Che chiu7-si7 chiong-lai5 u7 chit8 e5 si5, Goa2 sou2 boeh cho3 e5; Goa2 boeh chiong Goa2 e5 Seng3 Leng5 koan3 hou7 it-chhe3 e5 lang5; Hou7 lin2 e5 cha-pou-kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2 e7 the3 Goa2 kong2-oe7, Lin2 e5 siau3-lian5-lang5 e7 khoaN3-kiN3 i7-siong7, Lin2 e5 lau7-lang5 e7 tit-tioh8 thok-bang7.  18) Tioh8, chai7 hiah-e5 jit8-chi2, Goa2 ia7 boeh chiong Goa2 e5 Seng3 Leng5, Koan3 hou7 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 kap li2-pi7; in chiu7 e7 the3 Goa2 kong2-oe7.  19) Goa2 boeh toa3 thiN-teng2 hian2-si7 ki5-biau7 e5 tai7-chi3, Toa3 te7-siong7 hian2-si7 sin5-chek; e7 u7 hoeh kap hoe2 kap ian-bu7;  20) Jit8-thau5 e7 piN3-cho3 ou-am3, Goeh8-niu5 e7 chhin-chhiuN7 hoeh hiah-nih8 ang, Chu2 ui2-tai7 eng5-iau7 e5 jit8-chi2 lai5-lim5 i2-cheng5, e7 an2-ne.  21) Hit e5 si5, na7 hou-kiu5 Chu2 e5 mia5 e5, long2 e7 tit-tioh8 kiu3.몭몯
	22) 몮I2-sek-liat-lang5 a3, chhiaN2 thiaN goa2 kong2 koan-he7 Na2-sat-lek8-lang5 Ia5-sou chiah-e5 oe7! Siong7-chu2 thong-koe3 I, chai7 lin2 e5 tiong-kan hian2-si7 tai7-leng5, ki5-su7  kap sin5-chek, lai5 tui3 lin2 cheng3-beng5 I teh un7-heng5 Siong7-chu2 e5 tai7-leng5. Che si7 lin2 ka-ti7 sou2 chai-iaN2 e5.  23) Siong7-chu2 chiau3 i7-teng7 e5 chi2-i3 kap ke3-oe7, chiong Ia5-sou kau hou7 lin2; lin2 chiu7 chioh put-hoat e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2, ka7 I teng3 toa3 sip8-ji7-ke3-teng2, ka7 I sat-hai7.  24) Tan7-si7 Siong7-chu2 kai2-ti5 I si2-bong5 e5 thong3-khou2, hou7 I tui3 si2-lang5 tiong koh-oah8 khi2-lai5; in-ui7 si2-bong5 be7-tang3 ka7 I khong3-che3 tiau5 le7.  25) Tai7-pit8 koan-he7 I e5 tai7-chi3 u7 kong2:
몬Goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 Chu2 si5-siong5 ti7 Goa2 bin7-cheng5, In-ui7 I ti7 Goa2 e5 chiaN3-peng5, goa2 chiah be7 tong7-iau5.  26) Sou2-i2 Goa2 e5 sim chin hoaN-hi2, Goa2 e5 oe7 chhiong-moa2 khoai3-lok8; Iu7-koh Goa2 e5 jiok8-sin e7 chai7 hi-bong7-tiong an-jian5 koe3-jit8.  27) In-ui7 Li2 be7 chiong Goa2 e5 leng5-hun5 pang3-sak toa3 im-kan, Ia7 be7 hou7 Li2 khian5-seng5 e5 lou5-pok8 siu7 hu2-pai7.  28) Li2 i2-keng chi2-si7 Goa2 seN3-mia7 e5 to7-lou7, Li2 e7 hou7 Goa2 chai7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 chhiong-moa2 hi2-lok8.몭몯
	29) 몮HiaN-ti7 a3, goa2 tioh8 than2-pek8 ka7 lin2 kong2 koan-he7 lan2 e5 sian-chou2 Tai7-pit8 e5 tai7-chi3. I si2-khi3 a3, ia7 i2-keng hou7 lang5 bai5-chong3 a3, peng7-chhiaN2 i e5 bong7, kau3 kin-na2-jit8 iau2 u7 ti7 lan2 chia.  30) I si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 tai7-gian5-jin5, ia7 chai-iaN2 Siong7-chu2 bat tui3 i hoat-se3 kong2 boeh tui3 i e5 hou7-e3 lip8 chit8 ui7 lai5 che7 toa3 I e5 po2-cho7.  31) Tai7-pit8 khoaN3-chhut Siong7-chu2 sou2 boeh cho3 e5 tai7-chi3; koan-he7 Ki-tok e5 hok8-hoat8, i chiu7 kong2:
몬I bo5 pi7 pang3-sak toa3 im-kan, I e5 jiok8-sin ia7 bo5 hu2-pai7 khi3.몭
32) Siong7-chu2 hou7 chit ui7 Ia5-sou tui3 si2-lang5 tiong koh-oah8 khi2-lai5 a3, goan2 long2 si7 chit e5 su7-sit8 e5 kian3-cheng3-jin5.  33) I i2-keng pi7 the5-ko ti7 Siong7-chu2 e5 chiaN3-peng5, ia7 chiap-siu7 tioh8 Thian-hu7 sou2 eng3-un2 e5 Seng3 Leng5; I chiong chit ui7 Seng3 Leng5 koan3-chu3 hou7 goan2. Chit e5 su7-sit8 chiu7-si7 lin2 hian7-chai7 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 sou2 thiaN-kiN3 e5.  34) Sui-jian5 Tai7-pit8 pun2-sin bo5 seng-thian, tan7-si7 i kong2: 
몬Siong7-chu2 tui3 goa2 e5 Chu2 kong2: Che7 toa3 Goa2 e5 chiaN3-peng5,  35) It-tit8 kau3 Goa2 hou7 Li2 e5 tek8-jin5, cho3 kha-tiam7 lai5 hou7 Li2 khoa3-kha.몭몯
	36) 몮Sou2-i2 choan5 I2-sek-liat8 e5 bin5-chok8 tioh8 khak-sit8 chai-iaN2, lin2 ka7 I teng3 toa3 sip8-ji7-ke3 chit ui7 Ia5-sou, Siong7-chu2 i2-keng hong-lip8 I cho3 Chu2, cho3 Ki-tok a3!몯
	37) Cheng3-lang5 thiaN-kiN3 chiah-e5 oe7, in e5 sim chhin-chhiuN7 hou7 to chhak8-tioh8, chiu7 tui3 Pi2-tek kap ki5-tha e5 Su3-tou5 kong2: 몮HiaN-ti7 a3, goan2 tioh8 an3-choaN2 cho3?몯  38) Pi2-tek ka7 in kong2: 몮Lin2 tioh8 hoe2-kai2. Mui2 chit8 e5 lang5 tioh8 hong7 Ia5-sou Ki-tok e5 mia5 lai5 siu7 se2-le2, lin2 e5 choe7 chiah e7 tit-tioh8 sia3-bian2; lin2 chiu7 e7 tit-tioh8 Siong7-chu2 e5 in-su3, chiu7-si7 Seng3 Leng5.  39) In-ui7 Siong7-chu2 chit e5 eng3-un2 si7 boeh hou7 it-chhe3 Chu2 lan2 e5 Siong7-chu2 sou2 keng2-soan2 e5, chiu7-si7 boeh hou7 lin2 kap lin2 e5 kiaN2-sun, i2-kip8 it-chhe3 oan2-hong e5 lang5.몯
	40) Pi2-tek iau2 koh leng7-goa7 eng7 chin-che7 oe7 cho3 kian3-cheng3, ka7 in bian2-le7 kong2: 몮Lin2 tioh8 kiu3 lin2 ka-ti7 thoat-li7 chit e5 sia5-ok e5 se3-tai7.몯  41) Chiap-siu7 i e5 oe7 e5 lang5, long2 siu7 se2-le2; hit jit8 tai7-iok u7 saN-chheng lang5 ka- jip8 cho3 sin3-tou5.  42) In long2 choan5-sim thiaN Su3-tou5 e5 ka3-si7, hiong2-siu7 sin3-tou5-kan kau-gi5 e5 seng-oah8, peh mi7-pau, ki5-to2.

Sin3-tou5-kan e5 seng-oah8:
	43) Siong7-chu2 thong-koe3 Su3-tou5 cho3 chin-che7 sin5-chek ki5-su7, hou7 cheng3-lang5 to khi2 keng3-ui3 e5 sim.  44) Sin3-tou5 long2 cho3-hoe2 seng-oah8. In sou2 u7 e5 mih8 long2 kong-ke eng7.  45) In be7 in e5 ka-san2 kap sou2-iu2-but8, chiau3 kok lang5 e5 su-iau3 lai5 hun-phoe3.  46) In tak8-jit8 tong5-sim hap8-i3 cho3-hoe2 khi3 seng3-tian7 keng3-pai3, ia7 toa3 in e5 chhu3-lai7 cho3-hoe2 peh mi7-pau, tai7-ke phau7 hoaN-hi2 seng5-khun2 e5 sim-cheng5 chiah8-png7,  47) chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2, ia7 tit-tioh8 cheng3-lang5 e5 jin5-bong7. Chu2 chiu7 chiong I sou2 boeh kiu3 e5 lang5, jit8-jit8 cheng7-ka cho3 in e5 hoe7-chiong3.

Te7 3 ChiuN

I-ho2 pai2-kha-e5:
	1) U7 chit8 jit8, e7-pou-si5 saN tiam2, chiu7-si7 ki5-to2 e5 si5, Pi2-tek kap Iok-han7 teh boeh khi3 seng3-tian7.  2) U7 chit8 e5 lang5 tu2 hou7 lang5 kng tui3 hia koe3. I chu7 chhut-si3 chiu7 pai2-kha, tak8-jit8 hou7 lang5 kng lai5 khng3 toa3 seng3-tian7 e5 mng5-khau2, hit e5 mng5 kio3-cho3 몮Sui2 e5 mng5몯, toa3 hia hiong3 boeh jip8-khi3 seng3-tian7 e5 lang5 kiu5-khit.  3) I khoaN3-kiN3 Pi2-tek kap Iok-han7 teh-boeh jip8-khi3 seng3-tian7, chiu7 ka7 in kiu5-khit.  4) Pi2-tek kap Iok-han7 kim-kim ka7 i khoaN3, jian5-au7 Pi2-tek kong2: 몮Li2 khoaN3 goan2!몯  5) Hit e5 lang5 chiu7 liah8 in kim-kim khoaN3, teh ki5-thai7 e7-tang3 tui3 in tit-tioh8 sim2-mih.  6) Tan7-si7 Pi2-tek tui3 i kong2: 몮Goa2 ia7 bo5 kim ia7 bo5 gin5, tan7-si7 goa2 boeh chiong goa2 sou2 u7 e5 hou7 li2; goa2 hong7 Na2-sat-lek8-lang5 Ia5-sou Ki-tok e5 mia5, beng7-leng7 li2 khi2-lai5 kiaN5!몯  7) I chiu7 khan i e5 chiaN3-chhiu2, hou7 i khia7 khi2-lai5. I e5 kha kap kha-oan sui5-si5 chiu7 u7 lat8;  8) thiau3 khi2-lai5 khia7 le7, khai-si2 kiaN5-lai5 kiaN5-khi3.  I chiu7 kap in jip8-khi3 seng3-tian7, na2 kiaN5, na2 thiau3, na2 chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2.  9) Cheng3-lang5 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 i teh kiaN5, teh chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2;  10) in chit8-e7 jin7-chhut i chiu7-si7 tiaN7-tiaN7 che7 ti7 seng3-tian7 몮Sui2 e5 mng5몯 hit e5 khit-chiah8, in chiu7 tui3 i sou2 hoat-seng e5 tai7-chi3, moa2-sim tioh8-kiaN kam2-than3.

Pi2-tek chai7 seng3-tian7 kang2-to7:
	11) Hit e5 lang5 ti7 몮Sou2-lo5-bun5 e5 chau2-long5몯 iau2-ku2 ka7 Pi2-tek kap Iok-han7 giu2 tiau5-tiau5 e5 si5, cheng3-lang5 long2 toa7 tioh8-kiaN, chau2 oa2-lai5 in hia.  12) Pi2-tek khoaN3-kiN3 an2-ne chiu7 tui3 hiah-e5 lang5 kong2: 몮I2-sek-liat8-lang5 a3, an3-choaN2 khoaN3-kiN3 an2-ne chiu7 teh tioh8-kiaN, an3-choaN2 liah8 goan2 kim-kim khoaN3? Lin2 siuN7 kong2 goan2 si7 eng7 goan2 e5 koan5-peng3 a2-si7 keng3-khian5 lai5 hou7 i kiaN5 si7 bo5?  23) A-pek-lah8-han2 lan2 e5 chou2-sian e5 Siong7-chu2, i2-keng siuN2-su3 eng5-iau7 hou7 I e5 pok8-jin5 Ia5-sou. Lin2 soah chiong I kau hou7 Pi2-liap8-to. Sui-jian5 Pi2-liap8-to koat-teng7 boeh pang3 I khi3, lin2 toa3 Pi2-liap8-to e5 bin7-cheng5 ka7 I ki7-choat8.  14) Lin2 ki7-choat8 Hit-ui7 sin5-seng3 iu7-koh kong-gi7 e5, tian-to3 iau-kiu5 Pi2-liap8-to ka7 lin2 pang3 chit8 e5 sat-jin5-hoan7.  15) An2-ne lin2 thai5-si2 Hit-ui7 seN3-mia7 e5 Chhong3-cho7-chia2, tan7-si7 Siong7-chu2 hou7 I tui3 si2-lang5 tiong koh-oah8 khi2-lai5, --- iah goan2 chiu7-si7 chit e5 tai7-chi3 e5 kian3-cheng3-jin5.  16) Lin2 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3, lin2 sou2 bat chit e5 pai2-kha-e5, oa2-kho3 Ia5-sou e5 mia5, chiu7-si7 in-ui7 sin3 I e5 mia5, chiu7 hou7 i u7 khui3-lat8; tui3 I e5 mia5 e5 sin3-sim, hou7 chit e5 lang5 chai7 lin2 cheng3-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 oan5-choan5 ho2-khi3.몯
	17) 몮HiaN-ti7 a3, taN goa2 chai-iaN2 lin2 kap lin2 e5 leng2-to7-chia2 tui3 Ia5-sou an2-ne cho3, si7 in-ui7 lin2 m7 chai-iaN2 poaN3 hang7.  18) Tan7-si7 Siong7-chu2 kou2-cha2 chioh I e5 chiong3 tai7-gian5-jin5, soan-pou3 I e5 Ki-tok tioh8 siu7-lan7; I an2-ne lai5 eng3-giam7 I e5 oe7.  19) Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 hoan2-hoe2 lai5 kui-hiong3 Siong7-chu2. An2-ne I chiu7 e7 siau-ti5 lin2 e5 choe7.  20) An2-ne Chu2 e7 siuN2-su3 lin2 an-lok8 e5 si5-ki5, ia7 e7 chhe-phai3 Ia5-sou lai5, chiu7-si7 I i2-keng ui7 lin2 i7-teng7 e5 Ki-tok.  21) Ia5-sou tioh8 lau5 toa3 thiN-teng2 lau5 kau3 theng3-hau7 ban7-but8 keng-sin hit e5 si5-ki5, chiu7-si7 Siong7-chu2 kou2-cha2 chioh I sin5-seng3 e5 tai7-gian5-jin5 sou2 soan-gian5 e5 si5-ki5.  22) In-ui7 Mou5-se u7 kong2: 몬Chu2 Siong7-chu2 e7 tui3 lin2 e5 bin5-chok8-tiong, ka7 lin2 siat-lip8 chit8 ui7 Siong7-chu2 e5 tai7-gian5-jin5; chhin-chhiuN7 siat-lip8 goa2 an2-ne. I sou2 ka7 lin2 kong2 e5, lin2 long2 tioh8 thiaN.  23) Na7 bo5 thiaN Hit-ui7 Siong7-chu2 e5 tai7-gian5-jin5 sou2 kong2 e5 lang5, e7 tui3 Siong7-chu2 e5 chu2-bin5 pi7 keh-li7, pi7 siau-biat8.몭  24)  Tui3 Sat-bou7-jiN2(**ni2) i2-kip8 i2-au7 hiah-e5 Siong7-chu2 e5 tai7-gian5-jin5 na7 kong2 i7-gian5 e5, ia7 long2 u7 kong2-khi2 chiah-e5 jit8-chi2.  25) Lin2 si7 Siong7-chu2 tai7-gian5-jin5 e5 kiaN2-sun, ia7-si7 seng5-siu7 Siong7-chu2 kap lin2 chou2-sian sou2 lip8 e5 iok e5 lang5. Siong7-chu2 tui3 A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2: 몬Te7-siong7 ban7-bin5, long2 e7 tui3 li2 e5 hou7-e3 siu7-tioh8 chiok-hok.몭  26) Siong7-chu2 ui7 lin2 keng2-soan2 I e5 Pok8-jin5, chiu7 tai7-seng chhe-phai3 I lai5-kau3 lin2 chia, ka7 lin2 chiok-hok, hou7 lin2 mui2 chit8 e5 lang5 khi3-sia5 kui cheng3.몯

Te7 4 ChiuN

Pi2-tek kap Iok-han7 siu7 sim2-phoaN3:
	1) Pi2-tek kap Iok-han7 iau2 teh ka7 cheng3-lang5 kong2-oe7 e5 si5, che3-si kap seng3-tian7 e5 siu2-oe7 tiuN2, i2-kip8 Sat-thou2-kai-tong2 e5 lang5 chiu7 lai5 in hia.  2) In chin put-boan2, in-ui7 chit nng7 ui7 Su3-tou5 teh ka3-si7 cheng3-lang5, ia7 kin-ki3 Ia5-sou e5 hok8-hoat8 lai5 soan-kang2 si2-lang5 e5 koh-oah8 khi2-lai5.  3) Sou2-i2 in chiu7 he7-chhiu2 liah8 hit nng7 ui7 Su3-tou5; in-ui7 thiN i2-keng am3 a3, chiu7 ka7 in khau3-liu5 kau3 keh-tng2 jit8.  4) Tan7-si7 thiaN in e5 to7-li2 e5 lang5, u7 chin-che7 lang5 sin3; cha-pou-lang5 long2-chong2 chha-put-to u7 gou7-chheng.
	5) Keh-tng2 jit8, Iu5-thai3 e5 thau5-lang5, tiuN2-lo2 kap keng-hak8-chia2 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 khai-hoe7;  6) che3-si-tiuN2 A-na2, Kai-a-hoat, Iok-han7, A-lek8-san-tai7 i2-kip8 ki5-tha che3-si-tiuN2 chok8-lai7 e5 lang5, ia7 long2 chu7-chip8 ti7 hia.  7) In kio3 hit nng7 ui7 Su3-tou5 khia7 toa3 in bin7-cheng5, mng7 in kong2: 몮Lin2 eng7 sim2-mih koan5, hong7 sim2-mih lang5 e5 mia5 cho3 chit khoan2 tai7-chi3?몯  8) Hit e5 si5, Pi2-tek chhiong-moa2 Seng3 Leng5, tui3 in kong2: 몮Peh-seN3 e5 leng2-to7-chia2 kap tiuN2-lo2 a3,  9) goan2 kin-na2-jit8 na7 ui7-tioh8 tui3 pai2-kha-e5 cho3 ho2-su7, khoaN3 eng7 sim2-mih hoat-tou7 ka7 i i-ho2 khi3 lai5 siu7 sim2-mng7,  10) lin2 cheng3-lang5 kap I2-sek-liat8 e5 peh-seN3 long2 tioh8 chai-iaN2, khia7 ti7 lin2 bin7-cheng5 chit e5 lang5 oan5-choan5 ho2-khi3, si7 hong7 Na2-sat-lek8-lang5 Ia5-sou Ki-tok e5 mia5 i-ho2 e5 --- chit ui7 Ia5-sou si7 lin2 ka7 I teng3 toa3 sip8-ji7-ke3 si2, Siong7-chu2 hou7 I tui3 si2-lang5-tiong koh-oah8 khi2-lai5 e5.  11) Chit ui7 Ia5-sou chiu7-si7 Seng3-keng sou2 kong2 e5:
몬Lin2 chiah-e5 khi2-chhu3 sai-hu7 sou2 tan3-tiau7 e5 chioh8, soah piN3-cho3 chhu3-kak-thau5 e5 ki-chioh8.몭
12) Chi2-u7 tui3 I chiah e7-tang3 tit-tioh8 chin2-kiu3; in-ui7 ti7 thian-ha7, Siong7-chu2 bo5 siuN2-su3 hou7 lang5 pat8 e5 mia5, hou7 lan2 oa2-kho3 hit e5 mia5 lai5 tit-tioh8 kiu3.몯
	13) Chham-hoe7 e5 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 Pi2-tek kap Iok-han7 hiah-nih8 toa7 taN2, ia7 chai-iaN2 in si7 bo5 siu7 kau3-iok8 e5 phou2-thong-lang5, long2 chin tioh8-kiaN; ia7 e7-jin7-tit in si7 kap Ia5-sou cho3-tin7 e5.  14) Peng7-chhiaN2 khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 hou7 in i-ho2 khi3 e5 lang5 khia7 ti7 in e5 piN-a, chiu7 kio3 Pi2-tek kap Iok-han7 li7-khui hoe7-gi7-thiaN, chiah hou7-siong tho2-lun7 kong2:  16) 몮Lan2 tioh8 an3-choaN2 lai5 chhu2-li2 chiah-e5 lang5? In-ui7 toa3 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 mui2 chit8 e5 lang5, long2 chai-iaN2 in cho3 chit e5 tek8-piat8 e5 sin5-chek, lan2 ia7 bo5 seng5-jin7 be7-eng7-tit.  17) Tan7-si7 ui7 boeh hong5-chi2 chit hang7 tai7-chi3 chai7 bin5-kan m7-thang thoan5-iong5 khah khoah khi3, lan2 tioh8 keng2-kai3 in mai3 koh kho3 Ia5-sou e5 mia5 lai5 ka7 lang5 kong2 to7-li2.몯  18) In chiu7 koh kio3 in jip8-khi3, kim3-chi2 in chhian-ban7 m7-thang eng7 Ia5-sou e5 mia5 kong2-oe7 a2-si7 ka3-si7 lang5.  19) Tan7-si7 Pi2-tek kap Iok-han7 in3-tap in kong2: 몮Chai7 Siong7-chu2 e5 gan2-tiong, sun7-chiong5 lin2 a2-si7 sun7-chiong5 Siong7-chu2, tah chit8 hang7 khah tioh8, lin2 ka-ti7 phoaN3-toan3 khoaN3-bai7 le3;  20) in-ui7 goan2 ka-ti7 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3, sou2 thiaN-kiN3 e5 tai7-chi3, bo5 kong2 be7-eng7-tit. 몯21) Hiah-e5 lang5 chhoe7 bo5 li2-iu5 thang lai5 heng5-hoat8 in, iu7-koh in-ui7 bin5-chiong3 khoaN3-kiN3 sou2 hoat-seng e5 tai7-chi3 long2 teh chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2, chiu7 koh chit8 pai2 giam5-keh ka7 in keng2-ko3 liau2-au7, pang3 in chhut-khi3.  22) Cheng3-lang5 an2-ne teh chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2, si7 in-ui7 hou7 sin5-chek lai5 i-ho2 khi3 chit e5 lang5, i2-keng si3-chap8 goa7 hoe3 a3.

Sin3-tou5 e5 ki5-to2:
	23) Pi2-tek kap Iok-han7 siu7 sek-hong3 liau2-au7, chiu7 tng2-khi3 in e5 hoe7-iu2 hia, chiong che3-si-tiuN2 kap tiuN2-lo2 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, ka7 in po3-ko3.  24) In chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 an2-ne, chiu7 it-sim it-i3 toa7-siaN tui3 Siong7-chu2 ki5-to2 kong2: 몮Choan5-leng5 e5 Chu2-chaiN2, Li2 si7 thiN-te7, toa7-hai2 i2-kip8 u2-tiu7 ban7-but8 e5 Cho7-but8-chu2!  25) Li2 eng7 Seng3 Leng5 chioh Li2 e5 lou5-pok8, goan2 e5 chou2-sian Tai7-pit8 e5 chhui3 kong2:
몬Ban7-kok ui7 sim2-mih toa7 siu7-khi3, Ban7-bin5 ui7 sim2-mih ke3-bou5 khong-tong7 e5 tai7-chi3?  26) Se3-siong7 e5 kun-ong5 chun2-pi7 peng-be2, Thong2-ti7-chia2 lian5-hap8 cho3-hoe2, Tui3-tek8 Chu2 kap I e5 Bi2-sai3-a.몭
27) Ko2-jian5 Hi-lut8, Pun2-tiu Pi2-liap8-to, kap Goa7-pang-lang5 i2-kip8 I2-sek-liat8-lang5 chu7-chip8 chai7 chit e5 tou-chhi7, kong-kek Li2 sou2 boah-iu5 e5 seng3-kiat e5 lou5-pok8 Ia5-sou.  28) In seng5-chiu7 it-chhe3 Li2 e5 chhiu2 kap chi2-i3 sou2 su7-sian ke3-oe7 tioh8 sit8-hian7 e5 tai7-chi3.  29) Chu2 a3, taN kiu5 Li2 kam3-chhat in e5 khiong2-hat, ia7 siuN2-su3 Li2 e5 pok8-jin5 ho2-taN2 soan-kang2 Li2 e5 chin-to7.  30) Kiu5 Li2 chhun-chhiu2 chhut-lai5 i-peN7, ia7 iong7 Li2 seng3-kiat e5 lou5-pok8 Ia5-sou e5 mia5 lai5 cho3 ki5-su7 sin5-chek.몯  31) In ki5-to2 soah e5 si5, chu7-hoe7 hit e5 sou2-chai7 chiu7 io5-tang7; in chiu7 long2 chhiong-moa2 Seng3 Leng5, ho2-taN2 khai-si2 soan-kang2 Siong7-chu2 e5 to7-li2.

Sin3-tou5 e5 kiong7-tong5 seng-oah8:
	32) Chiong3 sin3-tou5 long2 it-sim it-i3. Bo5 lang5 kong2 i sou2 u7 e5 mih8 si7 i ka-ti7 e5. In sou2 u7 e5 mih8 it-chhe3 long2 si7 kong-ke e5.  33) Su3-tou5 eng7 toa7 koan5-leng5 lai5 ka7 Chu2 Ia5-sou e5 hok8-hoat8 cho3 kian3-cheng3, Siong7-chu2 ia7 toa7-toa7 siuN2-su3 in-tian2 hou7 in tai7-ke.  34) In e5 tiong-kan bo5 chit8 e5 u7 khiam3-khoeh sim2-mih; in-ui7 u7 chhan5-hng5 a2-si7 u7 chhu3-theh8 e5, long2 be7 tiau7, chiong hiah-e5 be7 khi3 sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 chiN5 theh8-lai5,  35) kau hou7 Su3-tou5; chiau3 kok-lang5 e5 su-iau3 hun-phoe3 hou7 in.
	36) U7 chit8 e5 ti7 Ku-pi2-lou7 chhut-si3 e5 Li7-bi7-chok8 e5 lang5, mia5 kio3-cho3 Iok-sek, Su3-tou5 kio3 i cho3 Pa-na2-pa (I3-su3 chiu7-si7 몮An-ui3-chia2몯).  37) I ia7 be7 ka-ti7 e5 chhan5-hng5, chiong chiN5 theh8 lai5 kau hou7 Su3-tou5.

Te7 5 ChiuN

A-na2-ni5-a kap Sat-hui-lat:
	1) U7 chit8 e5 lang5 mia5 kio3-cho3 A-na2-ni5-a, kap i e5 bou2 Sat-hui-lat be7 chit8 te3 thou2-te7,  2) kap in bou2 chham-siong5, chiong be7 thou2-te7 e5 chiN5 lau5 chit8 pou7-hun7 khi2-lai5, chhun e5 chiah theh8-lai5 kau hou7 Su3-tou5.  3) Pi2-tek ka7 i kong2: 몮A-na2-ni5-a, li2 an3-choaN2 hou7 Sat-tan3 lai5 khong3-che3 li2 e5 sim, hou7 li2 lai5 khi-phian3 Seng3 Leng5, chiong be7 thou2-te7 e5 chiN5 lau5 chit8 pou7-hun7 khi2-lai5?  4) Thou2-te7 iau2-boe7 be7 si7 li2 e5; be7 liau2-au7 li2 u7 koan5 thang sui5-i3 chhu2-li2 chiah-e5 chiN5. Li2 si7 an3-choaN2 sim-lai7 ke3-bou5 lai5 cho3 chit khoan2 tai7-chi3? Li2 an2-ne cho3 m7-si7 khi-phian3 lang5 ---si7 khi-phian3 Siong7-chu2!몯  5) A-na2-ni5-a chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 chiah-e5 oe7 chiu7 lek loh8-khi3, soah si2-khi3; thiaN-tioh8 chit hang7 tai7-chi3 e5 lang5, long2 toa7 tioh8-kiaN.  6) U7 chit8-koa2 siau3-lian5-lang5 chiu7 kiaN5 oa2-lai5, chiong i e5 si-the2 pau khi2-lai5, kng chhut-khi3 bai5-chong3.
	7) Chha-put-to saN tiam2-cheng au7, in thai3-thai3 jip8-lai5, iau2 m7 chai-iaN2 sou2 hoat-seng e5 tai7-chi3.  8) Pi2-tek ka7 i kong2: 몮Li2 ka7 goa2 kong2, che si7 lin2 be7 thou2-te7 e5 long2-chong2 e5 chiN5 si7 bo5?몯 I in3 kong2: 몮Si7, long2-chong2 chiu7-si7 chiah-e5 chiN5.몯  9) Pi2-tek chiu7 tui3 i kong2: 몮Lin2 an3-choaN2 chhoan3-thong lai5 chhi3-tham3 Chu2 e5 Seng3 Leng5? Li2 khoaN3 bai5-chong3 lin2 tiong7-hu e5 lang5 tu2-tu2 kiaN5 tng2-lai5 kau3 mng5-khau2 a3, in ia7 boeh ka7 li2 kng chhut-khi3!몯  10) I chiu7 chek-si5 lek loh8-khi3 Pi2-tek e5 bin7-cheng5, si2-khi3. Hiah-e5 siau3-lian5-lang5 jip8-lai5, khoaN3-kiN3 i si2-khi3 a3, chiu7 kng i chhut-khi3 bai5-chong3 toa3 in tiong7-hu e5 piN-a.  11) Choan5 kau3-hoe7 kap thiaN-kiN3 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 e5 lang5, long2 toa7 tioh8-kiaN.

Sin5-chek kap ki5-su7:
	12) Su3-tou5 ti7 cheng3-lang5 e5 tiong-kan cho3 chin-che7 sin5-chek kap ki5-su7. Sin3-tou5 si5-siong5 tong5-sim hap8-i3 lai5 chu7-chip8 toa3 Sou2-lo5-bun5 e5 chau2-long5.  13) I2-goa7 e5 lang5, sui-jian5 bo5 lang5 kaN2 khi3 kap in cho3-hoe2, m7-ku2 tai7-ke long2 chin chun-tiong7 in.  14) Sin3 Chu2 e5 lang5, bo5-lun7 cha-pou-e5 cha-bou2-e5, lu2 lai5 lu2 che7.  15) Soah u7 lang5 chiong peN7-lang5 kng chhut-lai5 ke-a2-lou7, khng3 toa3 bin5-chhng5-teng2 a2-si7 chhng5-phou-teng2, thang hou7 Pi2-tek tui3 hia koe3 e5 si5, siong7-bo5 i e5 iaN2 e7 jia-tioh8 kui2-e5-a2 lang5.  16) Ia7 u7 chit8 toa7 tin7 lang5 tui3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 chiu-ui5 e5 hiong-tin3, chhoa7 peN7-lang5 kap hou7 sia5-sin5 tiN5-sin e5 lang5 lai5; in long2 hou7 i i-ho2 khi3.

Su3-tou5 siu7 pek-hai7:
	17) Che3-si-tiuN2 i2-kip8 kap i tau3-tin7 e5 cheng3-lang5, chiu7-si7 Sat-thou2-kai-tong2 e5 lang5, long2 hui-siong5 chit-tou3 Su3-tou5, chiu7 he7-chhiu2 liah8 Su3-tou5.  18) In liah8 Su3-tou5 khi2-lai5, ka7 in koaiN loh8-khi3 kong-ka e5 kaN-gak8.  19) Tan7-si7 hit am3 Chu2 e5 thian-sai3 lai5 khui kaN-gak8 e5 mng5, chhoa7 in chhut-lai5, ka7 in kong2:  20) 몮Lin2 khi3 khia7 toa3 seng3-tian7 lai7, chiong chit e5 chin2-kiu3 e5 sin3-sek long2 kong2 hou7 cheng3-lang5 thiaN.몯  21) Su3-tou5 thiaN i e5 oe7, thiN-boeh-kng e5 si5, in chiu7 jip8-khi3 seng3-tian7, khai-si2 ka3-si7 lang5.
	Che3-si-tiuN2 i2-kip8 kap i tau3-tin7 e5 lang5 chit8-e7 kau3, chiu7 tiau3-chip8 it-chhe3 I2-sek-liat8-lang5 e5 tiuN2-lo2 lai5 khui kong-gi7-hoe7; jian5-au7 chhe khi3 kaN-gak8 chhoa7 Su3-tou5 lai5.  22) Tan7-si7 siu2-oe7 kau3 hia e5 si5, bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 Su3-tou5 ti7 kaN-gak8-lai7; in chiu7 tng2-khi3 tui3 kong-gi7-hoe7 po3-ko3. kong2:  23) 몮Goan2 kau3 kaN-gak8 e5 si5, khoaN3-kiN3 kaN-gak8 so2 tiau5-tiau5, khan3-siu2 ia7 khia7 ti7 mng5-goa7 teh kou3; tan7-si7 goan2 chit8-e7 khui-mng5, bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 poaN3 e5 lang5 ti7 lai7-bin7.몯  24) Seng3-tian7 e5 siu2-oe7-tiuN2 kap che3-si-tiuN2 thiaN-kiN3 chiah-e5 oe7, kam2-kak chin ki5-koai3, m7-chai su7-cheng5 boeh an3-choaN2 ian2-pian3.  25) Hit e5 si5 u7 chit8 e5 lang5 jip8-lai5 ka7 in kong2: 몮Lin2 liah8 jip8-khi3 koaiN ti7 kaN-gak8 e5 lang5, chim2-ma2 khia7 ti7 seng3-tian7 lai7 teh ka3-si7 lang5!몯  26) Siu2-oe7-tiuN2 chiu7 kap i e5 pou7-ha7 khi3 chhoa7 Su3-tou5 tng2-lai5, m7-kaN2 eng7 kiong5-ngeN7 e5 chhiu2-toaN7, in-ui7 in kiaN-liau2 hou7 cheng3-lang5 eng7 chioh8-thau5 tim3.
	27) In chhoa7 Su3-tou5 jip8-lai5, hou7 in khia7 toa3 kong-gi7-hoe7 e5 bin7-cheng5, che3-si-tiuN2 chiu7 mng7 in kong2:  28) 몮Goan2 giam5-kim3 lin2 m7-thang eng7 Chit e5 mia5 ka3-si7 lang5, tan7-si7 lin2 tian-to3 chiong lin2 e5 ka3-si7 thoan5-khui choan5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, siuN7-boeh hou7 Chit e5 lang5 si2-bong5 e5 chek-jim7 kui hou7 goan2!몯  29) Pi2-tek kap ki5-tha e5 Su3-tou5 in3-tap kong2: 몮Goan2 sun7-chiong5 Siong7-chu2 pi2 sun7-chiong5 lang5 khah tiong7-iau3.  30) Lin2 ka7 I teng3-si2 toa3 sip8-ji7-ke3-teng2 e5 Ia5-sou, lan2 e5 chou2-sian e5 Siong7-chu2 i2-keng hou7 I koh-oah8 khi2-lai5 a3.  31) Siong7-chu2 iu7 ka7 I the5-seng toa3 I e5 chiaN3-chhiu2-peng5, hou7 I cho3 Siu2-leng2, cho3 Kiu3-chu2, hou7 I2-sek-liat8-lang5 u7 hoe2-kai2 e5 ki-hoe7, ia7 hou7 in e5 choe7 e7 tit-tioh8 sia3-bian2.  32) Goan2 chiu7-si7 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 e5 kian3-cheng3-jin5. Siong7-chu2 sou2 siuN2-su3 hou7 sun7-chiong5 I e5 lang5 e5 Seng3 Leng5, ia7 ui7 chit hang7 tai7-chi3 cho3-cheng3.
	33) Kong-gi7-hoe7 e5 lang5 thiaN-kiN3 chiah-e5 oe7 chiu7 toa7 siu7-khi3, koat-i3 siuN7 boeh ka7 in sat-hai7.  34) Tan7-si7 in tiong-kan u7 chit8 e5 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5, kio3-cho3 Ka-ma2-liat8, si7 siu7 cheng3-lang5 chun-keng3 e5 Lut8-hoat e5 lau7-su. I chai7 kong-gi7-hoe7-tiong khia7 khi2-lai5, beng7-leng7 lang5 chiam7-si5 chhoa7 Su3-tou5 chhut-khi3 goa7-bin7,  35) chiu7 tui3 tai7-ke kong2: 몮I2-sek-liat8-lang5 a3, lin2 boeh pan7 chiah-e5 lang5, tioh8 chin sio2-sim.  36) I2-cheng5 u7 chit8 e5 lang5 kio3-cho3 Tiu-tai7 chhut-hian7, chu7-chheng i chin ui2-tai7; chha-put-to u7 si3-pah lang5 lai5 toe3 i. I hou7 lang5 thai5-si2, it-chhe3 toe3 i e5 lang5 long2 si3-soaN3 khi3, i e5 ke3-bou5 chiu7 long2 lok8-khong.  37) Au7-lai5 u7 chit8 e5 Ka-li7-li7-lang5 Iu5-tai7, chai7 hou7-khau2 tiau5-cha e5 si5-ki5 chhut-hian7, in2-iu2 chit8 tin7 lang5 lai5 toe3 i, tan7-si7 i ia7 biat8-bong5; toe3 i e5 lang5 ia7 long2 si3-soaN3 khi3.  38) TaN koan-he7 chit e5 an3-kiaN7 goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, m7-thang kan-siap8 chiah-e5 lang5, chhut-chai7 in khi3. In-ui7 in e5 ke3-bou5, in e5 kang-chok na7-si7 tui3 lang5 lai5 e5, it-teng7 e7 sit-pai7;  39) tan7-si7 na7-si7 tui3 Siong7-chu2 lai5 e5, lin2 chiu7 be7-tang3 ka7 in pho3-hoai7. KiaN-liau2 lin2 soah e7 kap Siong7-chu2 cho3 tui3-tek8!몯 Kong-gi7-hoe7 chiu7 thiaN i e5 khoan3-ko3.  40) In kio3 Su3-tou5 jip8-lai5, eng7 piN ka7 in phah, beng7-leng7 in m7-thang koh hong7 Ia5-sou e5 mia5 kong2 to7-li2; jian5-au7 chiah pang3 in chhut-khi3.  41) Su3-tou5 li7-khui kong-gi7-hoe7, moa2-sim hoaN-hi2, kong2 Siong7-chu2 khoaN3 in e7-tat8-tit ui7 Ia5-sou e5 mia5 siu7 bu2-jiok8.  42) In chiu7 tak8-jit8 toa3 seng3-tian7 a2-si7 toa3 jin5-ke, ke3-siok8 ka3-si7 lang5, thoan5 koan-he7 Ia5-sou chiu7-si7 Bi2-sai3-a e5 Hok-im.

Te7 6 ChiuN

Soan2 chhit e5 cho3 chip-su7:
	1) Chai7 chit e5 tiong-kan, in-ui7 bun5-tou5 it-tit8 cheng7-ka khi2-lai5, kong2 Hi-lah8-oe7 e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5 soah tui3 pun2-te7 e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5 phau7 put-peng5. In ke3-kau3 kong2 hun-phoe3 jit8-jit8 e5 chiah8-niu5 e5 si5, bo5 kou3 tioh8 in e5 koaN2-hu7.  2) Chap8-ji7 ui7 Su3-tou5 chiu7 kio3 choan5-the2 e5 bun5-tou5 long2 oa2-lai5, ka7 in kong2: 몮Goan2 hong3-khi3 thoan5 Siong7-chu2 e5 to7-li2, lai5 chiang2-koan2 sian7-sit8 chin bo5 hap8-sek.  3) Sou2-i2 hiaN-ti7 a3, tioh8 tui3 lin2 e5 tiong-kan soan2-chhut chhit e5 ho2 mia5-siaN, chhiong-moa2 Seng3 Leng5 iu7-koh u7 ti3-hui7 e5 lang5, goan2 thang ui2-jim7 in lai5 hu7-chek chit hang7 tai7-chi3.  4) An2-ne goan2 chiu7 e7-tang3 choan5-sim lai5 ki5-to2, lai5 chin7 thoan5-to7 e5 chit-hun7.몯  5) Cheng3-lang5 thiaN-tioh8 Su3-tou5 e5 the5-an3 chin hoaN-hi2; in chiu7 soan2 Su7-the5-hoan2, i si7 chhiong-moa2 sin3-sim kap Seng3 Leng5 e5 lang5, kap Hui-lek8, Pek-lo5-ko-lo5, Ni5-ka-na2, The5-bun5, Pa-bi2-na2, i2-kip8 i2-cheng5 kai2-chong jip8 Iu5-thai3-kau3 e5 An-the5-o-lang5 Ni5-ko-lah.  6) In hou7 chit chhit e5 lang5 khia7 toa3 Su3-tou5 e5 bin7-cheng5, Su3-tou5 chiu7 ki5-to2, ia7 ka7 in an3-chhiu2.
	7) Siong7-chu2 e5 chin-to7 chiu7 lu2 thoan5 lu2 khoah; chai7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 bun5-tou5 ia7 it-tit8 cheng7-ka, ia7 u7 chin-che7 che3-si lai5 sin3-chiong5 chit e5 to7-li2.

Su7-the5-hoan2 pi7 khong3-ko3:
	8) Su7-the5-hoan2 chhiong-moa2 in-hui7 kap leng5-lek8, chai7 bin5-chiong3 e5 tiong-kan cho3 toa7 sin5-chek kap ki5-su7.  9) Tan7-si7 u7 chit8-koa2 kio3-cho3 Chu7-iu5-jin5 e5 hoe7-tng5 e5 lang5, ki5-tiong u7 tui3 Kou2-li7-nai7 kap A-lek8-san-thai3 lai5 e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5. In kap ki5-tha tui3 Ki-li7-ka kap A-se-a lai5 e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5, khai-si2 kap Su7-the5-hoan2 pian7-lun7.  10) Tan7-si7 Seng3 Leng5 siuN2-su3 Su7-the5-hoan2 ti3-hui7, sou2-i2 i teh kong2 e5 si5, cheng3-lang5 long2 be7-tang3 kap i khong3-pian7.  11) In chiu7 sai2-long7 lang5 kong2: 몮Goan2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 i kong2-khi2 hui2-pong3 Mou5-se kap Siong7-chu2 e5 oe7!몯  12) In eng7 chit khoan2 hoat-tou7 lai5 sian3-tong7 bin5-chiong3, tiuN2-lo2 kap keng-hak8-chia2. In lai5 Su7-the5-hoan2 hia, ka7 i liah8 khi2-lai5, thoa i khi3 kong-gi7-hoe7.  13) In chiu7 tho3 chit8-koa2 ke2 cheng3-jin5, kio3 in kong2: 몮Chit e5 lang5 kong2-oe7 tiaN7-tiaN7 kong-kek chit e5 seng3-tian7 kap Mou5-se e5 Lut8-hoat, 14) in-ui7 goan2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 i kong2 chit e5 Na2-sat-lek8-lang5 Ia5-sou boeh hui2-hoai7 chit e5 seng3-tian7, ia7 boeh kai2-pian3 Mou5-se sou2 thoan5 loh8-lai5 hou7 lan2 e5 koan3-le7!몯  15) Hit e5 si5 che7 ti7 kong-gi7-hoe7 e5 lang5, long2 liah8 Su7-the5-hoan2 kim-kim khoaN3, khoaN3-kiN3 i e5 bin7 tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 thian-sai3 e5 bin7.

Te7 7 ChiuN

Su7-the5-hoan2 e5 tap-pian7:
	1) Che3-si-tiuN2 chiu7 mng7 Su7-the5-hoan2 kong2, 몮Su7-sit8 u7-iaN2 an2-ne bo5?몯  2) Su7-the5-hoan2 in3 kong2: 몮Hu7-lo2 hiaN-ti7 a3! ChhiaN2 lin2 thiaN goa2 kong2! Lan2 e5 chou2-sian A-pek-lah8-han2, iau2-boe7 khi3 toa3 Hap-lan5 i2-cheng5, iau2 ti7 Bi2-sou2-pho-tai7-bi2 e5 si5, eng5-iau7 e5 Siong7-chu2 hian2-hian7 hou7 i khoaN3,  3) tui3 i kong2, 몬Li2 tioh8 li7-khui li2 e5 pun2-thou2 kap chhin-chok8, khi3 Goa2 boeh ka7 li2 chi2-si7 e5 te7-hng.몭  4) I chiu7 li7-khui Ka-lek8-ti2-lang5 e5 te7-hng, khi3 toa3 Hap-lan5. A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 lau7-pe7 si2 liau2-au7, Siong7-chu2 hou7 i tui3 hia poaN-lai5 kau3 lin2 hian7-chai7 teh toa3 chit e5 te7-hng.  5) Ti7 chia Siong7-chu2 long2 bo5 chit8 kak-a2 thou2-te7 hou7 i ke3-seng5, lian5 chhun3-thou2 ia7 bo5; hit e5 si5 sui-jian5 i iau2 bo5 kiaN2, tan7-si7 Siong7-chu2 eng3-un2 boeh chiong chit e5 te7-hng siuN2-su3 hou7 i, kap hou7 i e5 kiaN2-sun.  6) Siong7-chu2 an2-ne ka7 i kong2: 몬Li2 e5 kiaN2-sun e7 khi3 toa3 goa7-kok, e7 cho3 lang5 e5 lou5-le7, e7 hou7 lang5 gek8-thai7 si3 pah ni5 ku2.몭  7) Siong7-chu2 iu7-koh kong2, 몬Tan7-si7 goa2 boeh sim2-phoaN3 hou7 in cho3 lou5-le7 hit e5 kok-bin5, jian5-au7 hiah-e5 lou5-le7 e7 tui3 hit kok chhut-lai5, chai7 chit e5 sou2-chai7 lai5 keng3-pai3 goa2.몭  8) Siong7-chu2 chiu7 siuN2-su3 kat-le2 hou7 A-pek-lah8-han2 cho3 beng5-iok e5 ki3-ho7. Sou2-i2 A-pek-lah8-han2 seN I2-sat liau2-au7 te7-peh jit8, chiu7 ka7 i si-heng5 kat-le2; I2-sat ka7 Nga2-kok si-heng5 kat-le2; Nga2-kok ka7 chap8-ji7 ui7 chok8-tiuN2 si-heng5 kat-le2.몯
	9) 몮Chiah-e7 chok8-tiuN2 chit-tou3 Iok-sek, ka7 i be7 khi3 Ai-kip8 cho3 lou5-le7. Tan7-si7 Siong7-chu2 kap i tong5-chai7,  10) kiu3 i thoat-li7 it-chhe3 hoan7-lan7, siuN2-su3 i ti3-hui7, hou7 i tit-tioh8 Ai-kip8-ong5 Hoat-lo2 e5 thiong2-ai3. Hoat-lo2 chiu7 hou7 i cho3 chaiN2-siong3 thong2-ti7 choan5 Ai-kip8 kap koan2-li2 choan5 ong5-chok8.  11) Au7-lai5 ai-kip8 kap Ka-lam5 choan5 te7 hoat-seng ki-hng, in2-khi2 toa7 chai-lan7, lan2 e5 chou2-sian chhoe7 bo5 sim2-mih thang chiah8.  12) Nga2-kok thiaN-kiN3 ti7 Ai-kip8 u7 chiah8-niu5, i chiu7 thau5 chit8 pai2 chhe-phai3 lan2 e5 chou2-sian khi3 hia.  13) Te7-ji7 pai2 e5 si5 Iok-sek kong2-chhut i e5 sin-se3 hou7 i e5 hiaN-ti7 chai-iaN2, Hoat-lo2 ia7 soah chai-iaN2 hiah-e5 lang5 si7 Iok-sek e5 chhin-chok8.  14) Sou2-i2 Iok-sek chiu7 chhe lang5 thong-ti in lau7-pe7 Nga2-kok, chhiaN2 i kap choan5 ka-chok8 chhit-chap8-gou7 e5 lang5 lai5 Ai-kip8.  15) Nga2-kok chiu7 loh8-khi3 Ai-kip8. au7-lai5 i kap lan2 e5 chou2-sian long2 toa3 hia koe3-ong2 khi3.  16) In e5 si-the2 au7-lai5 un7 tng2-lai5 Si-kiam3, chong3 toa3 khah-cha2 A-pek-lah8-han2 eng7 chiN5 tui3 hap(**Hap)-boat e5 kiaN2-sun be2 khi2-lai5 e5 bong7-te7.몯
	17) 몮Siong7-chu2 tui3 A-pek-lah8-han2 sou2 eng3-un2 e5 tai7-chi3, eng3-giam7 e5 si5-ki5 teh-boeh kau3 a3, hit e5 si5 lan2 e5 bin5-chok8 chai7 Ai-kip8 lu2 seN-thoaN3 lu2 che7.  18) Au7-lai5 leng7-goa7 u7 chit8 e5 m7-bat Iok-sek e5 ong5 khi2-lai5 thong2-ti7 Ai-kip8.  19) I eng7 kui2-ke3 hai7 lan2 e5 bin5-chok8, gek8-thai7 lan2 e5 chou2-sian, kiong5-pek in chiong ang-eN-a2 pang3-sak toa3 goa7-bin7 hou7 in si2.  20) Mou5-se chiu7-si7 tu2-tu2 chai7 chit e5 si5 chhut-si3, si7 chit8 e5 chin sui2 e5 ang-eN-a2, chin siu7 Siong7-chu2 e5 thiong2-ai3. Chai7 in lau7-pe7 e5 chhu3-nih8 iuN2-chhi7 saN kou3-goeh8 au7,  21) i pi7 pang3-sak e5 si5, Hoat-lo2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 ka7 i khioh khi2-lai5 cho3 i ka-ti7 e5 kiaN2 iuN2-chhi7.  22) Mou5-se hak8-sip8 ai-kip8-lang5 it-chhe3 e5 hak8-bun7, bo5-lun7 kong2-oe7 a2-si7 cho3-su7 long2 chin u7 chai5-leng5.몯
	23) 몮Mou5-se kau3 si3-chap8 hoe3 e5 si5, koat-i3 siuN7-boeh khi3 hong2-bun7 I2-sek-liat8 tong5-pau.  24) I chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 in tong5-pau e5 chit8 e5, siu7 Ai-kip8-lang5 gek8-thai7, i chiu7 khi3 po2-hou7 i, thai5-si2 hit e5 Ai-kip8-lang5, the3 hit e5 siu7 gek8-thai7 e5 lang5 po3-siu5.  25) (I siuN7-cho3 i e5 tong5-pau e7 liau2-kai2 Siong7-chu2 boeh eng7 i e5 chhiu2 lai5 kai2-kiu3 in, tan7-si7 in be7-tang3 liau2-kai2.)  26) Keh-tng2 jit8, i khoaN3-kiN3 nng7 e5 I2-sek-liat8-lang5 teh oan-ke, siuN7-boeh ka7 in tiau(NNtiau5)-kai2, kong2, 몬Peng5-iu2 a3, lin2 si7 tong5-pau, an3-choaN2 lin2 teh khi-hu7 lai5 khi-hu7 khi3?몭  27) Tan7-si7 hit e5 teh khi-hu7 lang5 e5, ka7 Mou5-se poe2-khui, kong2, 몬Sim2-mih lang5 jim7-beng7 li2 cho3 goan2 e5 siu2-tiuN2, cho3 goan2 e5 phoaN3-koaN?  28) Li2 boeh chhin-chhiuN7 li2 cha-hng thai5-si2 hit e5 Ai-kip8-lang5 an2-ne lai5 ka7 goa2 thai5-si2 si7 bo5?몭  29) Mou5-se thiaN-tioh8 chit ku3 oe7, chiu7 to5-chhut Ai-kip8, khi3 toa3 Bi2-tian5 e5 te7-hng seng-oah8. I toa3 hia seN nng7 e5 hau7-seN.몯
	30) 몮Keng-koe3 si3-chap8 ni5, kin7 Se-nai2-soaN e5 khong3-ia2-tiong u7 chit8 bou5 chhi3-a2 teh toh8-hoe2, u7 chit8 ui7 thian-sai3 ti7 hoe2-iam7-tiong hian2-hian7 hou7 Mou5-se khoaN3.  31) Mou5-se chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 an2-ne, kam2-kak chin ki5-koai3; oa2-khi3 boeh khoaN3 khah chin le3, chiu7 thiaN-kiN3 Chu2 e5 siaN kong2:  32) 몬Goa2 si7 lin2 chou2-sian e5 Siong7-chu2, si7 A-pek-lah8-han2, I2-sat, Nga2-kok e5 Siong7-chu2.몭 Mou5-se kiaN kah phih8-phih8-chhoah, m7-kaN2 khoaN3.  33) Chu2 chiu7 ka7 i kong2: 몬Li2 chheng7 e5 e5 tioh8 thng3 khi2-lai5, in-ui7 li2 teh khia7 e5 sou2-chai7 si7 seng3-te7.  34) Goa2 khak-sit8 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 Goa2 e5 chu2-bin5 ti7 Ai-kip8 sou2 siu7 e5 gek8-thai7, ia7 u7 thiaN-kiN3 in kio3-khou2 e5 siaN, Goa2 chiah loh8-lai5 boeh chin2-kiu3 in. TaN li2 lai5, Goa2 boeh chhe-phai3 li2 khi3 Ai-kip8.몭몯
	35) 몮Chit e5 Mou5-se chiu7-si7 hou7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 chu2-bin5 khi3-choat8 e5. In kong2, 몬Sim2-mih lang5 jim7-beng7 li2 cho3 goan2 e5 siu2-tiuN2, cho3 goan2 e5 phoaN3-koaN?몭 Tan7-si7 Mou5-se chiu7-si7 Siong7-chu2 thong-koe3 ti7 teh toh8-hoe2 e5 chhi3-a2-bou5-tiong hian2-hian7 e5 thian-sai3 chhe-phai3 i lai5 cho3 siu2-tiuN2, cho3 chin2-kiu3-chia2.  36) I chhoa7 hiah-e5 chu2-bin5 to5-chhut Ai-kip8, chai7 Ai-kip8, Ang-hai2 i2-kip8 chai7 khong3-ia2 tiong, si3-chap8 ni5 kan cho3 chin-che7 sin5-chek ki5-su7.  37) Tui3 I2-sek-liat8-lang5 kong2, 몬Siong7-chu2 e7 tui3 lin2 e5 bin5-chok8-tiong, ka7 lin2 siat-lip8 chit8 ui7 Siong7-chu2 e5 tai7-gian5-jin5, chhin-chhiuN7 siat-lip8 goa2 an2-ne.몭 Chit ku3 chiu7-si7 Mou5-se kong2 e5.  38) Chit e5 lang5 chiu7-si7 I2-sek-liat8 bin5-chok8 chai7 khong3-ia2-tiong chu7-hoe7 e5 si5, khi3 Se-nai2-soaN-teng2 kap thian-sai3 kong2-oe7, cho3 thian-sai3 kap lan2 e5 chou2-sian e5 tiong-to7 lai5 thoan5 hou7 lan2.몯
	39) 몮Tan7-si7 lan2 e5 chou2-sian m7-kheng2 hok8-chiong5 i, tian-to3 ka7 i ki7-choat8. In e5 sim long2 siuN7-boeh koh to3-tng2 khi3 Ai-kip8.  40) In tui3 A-lun5 kong2: 몬Li2 tioh8 cho7 chit8-koa2 ngou2-siong7 thang ka7 goan2 chhoa7-lou7, in-ui7 chhoa7 goan2 chhut Ai-kip8 hit e5 Mou5-se, m7-chai u7 hoat-seng sim2-mih tai7-chi3.몭  41) Chai7 hit e5 si5, in chiu7 cho7 chit8 e5 gu5-a2-kiaN2 e5 siong7, ia7 eng7 seng-le2 lai5 pai3 chit e5 ngou2-siong7, ui7 in ka-ti7 sou2 cho7 e5 lai5 ki2-heng5 che3-tian2.  42) Siong7-chu2 chiu7 m7 chhap in, chhut-chai7 in khi3 pai3 jit8-goat8 seng-sin5, tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 tai7-gian5-jin5 e5 chheh u7 sia2 kong2:
몬I2-sek-liat8 e5 chu2-bin5 a3! Lin2 ti7 khong3-ia2 koe3 si3-chap8 ni5, Kam2 bat thai5 cheng-seN kap eng7 seng-le2 lai5 che3-hian3 Goa2?  43) Lin2 kng Mou5-lok8 e5 pou3-phang5, Kap Li2-hoan sin5 e5 chheN, Chiu7-si7 lin2 sou2 cho7 boeh lai5 pai3 e5 ngou2-siong7; Sou2-i2 Goa2 boeh ka7 lin2 koaN2 koe3-khi3 Pa-pi2-lun5 hit peng5.몭몯
	44) 몮Lan2 e5 chou2-sian chai7 khong3-ia2 u7 piau2-si7 Siong7-chu2 lim5-chai7 e5 tiuN3-bou7. Che si7 Siong7-chu2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se, kio3 i chiau3 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 iuN7-sek kian3-cho7 e5.  45) Au7-lai5 lan2 e5 chou2-sian ke3-seng5 chit e5 tiuN3-bou7. In kap Iok-su-a cho3-hoe2 khi3 chiap-koan2 pat8 bin5-chok8 e5 te7-thou2 e5 si5, Siong7-chu2 cho3 sian-hong chiong hiah-e5 bin5-chok8 koaN2 chhut-khi3. Hit e5 si5 ia7 u7 toa3 chit e5 tiuN3-bou7 khi3, it-tit8 an-ti3 kau3 Tai7-pit8 e5 si5-tai7.  46) Tai7-pit8 tit-tioh8 Siong7-chu2 e5 thiong2-ai3, kiu5 Siong7-chu2 in2-chun2 i ui7 Nga2-kok e5 Siong7-chu2 i7-pi7 chit8 keng ki-chu7 e5 sou2-chai7.  47) Tan7-si7 su7-sit8-siong7 ui7 Siong7-chu2 khi2 seng3-tian7 e5, si7 Sou2-lo5-bun5.몯
	48) 몮Ki5-sit8, Chi3-ko-chia2 Siong7-chu2 bo5 toa3 eng7 lang5 e5 chhiu2 sou2 kian3-cho7 e5 pang5-ok; chiu7-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 tai7-gian5-jin5 kong2:
49) 몬Chu2 kong2, thiN si7 Goa2 e5 po2-cho7, Te7 si7 Goa2 e5 kha-tiam7. Lin2 boeh ka7 Goa2 khi2 sim2-mih khoan2 e5 chhu3? Sim2-mih sou2 chai7 boeh hou7 Goa2 hioh-khun3?  50) Che it-chhe3 kam2 m7-si7 Goa2 chhin-chhiu2 chhong3-cho7 e5?몭몯
	51) 몮Lin2 an3-choaN2 chiah-nih8 kou3-chip! Tui3 Siong7-chu2 e5 chin-li2, lin2 sim-koaN an3-choaN2 chiah bo5 sin3-sim, lin2 e5 hiN7-a2 an3-choaN2 long2 bo5 boeh thiaN? Lin2 tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 lin2 chou2-sian, lin2 ia7 siong5-siong5 hoan2-khong3 Seng3 Leng5!  52) Kam2 u7 chit8 ui7 Siong7-chu2 e5 tai7-gian5-jin5 bo5 hou7 lin2 e5 chou2-sian pek-hai7 tioh8? Hiah-e5 i7-gian5 hit ui7 Kong-gi7-e5 teh-boeh lai5 e5 lang5, lin2 e5 chou2-sian ia7 ka7 in hai7-si2. TaN oaN7 lin2 lai5 chhut-be7 Hit-ui7, bou5-sat Hit-ui7.  53) Lin2 si7 thong-koe3 thian-sai3 nia2-siu7 tioh8 Siong7-chu2 Lut8-hoat e5 lang5, siong7-chhiaN2 bo5 chun-siu2!몯

Ka7 Su7-the5-hoan2 tim3 chioh8-thau5:
	54) In thiaN-kiN3 Su7-the5-hoan2 kong2 chiah-e5 oe7 chiu7 toa7 siu7-khi3, khi3 kah ka7-ge5 chhiat-khi2.  55) Tan7-si7 Su-the5-hoan2 chhiong-moa2 Seng3 Leng5, giah8-thau5 khoaN3 thiN, khoaN3-kiN3 Siong7-chu2 e5 eng5-iau7, ia7 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-sou khia7 ti7 Siong7-chu2 e5 chiaN3-peng5.  56) I chiu7 kong2, 몮Li2 khoaN3, goa2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 thiN khui-khui, Jin5-chu2 khia7 ti7 Siong7-chu2 e5 chiaN3-peng5!몯  57) Cheng3-lang5 toa7-siaN hoah khi2-lai5, tui3 hiN7-a2 ng-le, cho3 chit8-e7 chhih8 oa2-khi3 i hia.  58) In ka7 i thoa chhut-khi3 siaN5-goa7, eng7 chioh8-thau5 ka7 i tim3. Hiah-e5 cho3 cheng3-jin5 e5, chiong in ka-ti7 e5 goa7-saN khng3 toa3 chit8 e5 siau3-lian5-lang5, mia5 kio3-cho3 So3-lo5 e5 bin7-cheng5.  59) In ke3-siok8 eng7 chioh8-thau5 teh tim3 Su7-the5-hoan2 e5 si5, Su7-the5-hoan2 chiu7 hou-kiu5 Chu2 kong2, 몮Chu2 Ia5-sou, chhiaN2 chiap-siu7 goa2 e5 leng5-hun5!몯  60) I kui7 loh8-khi3, toa7 siaN hou-hiam3 kong2, 몮Chu2 a3, chit e5 choe7 m7-thang kui hou7 in!몯 I kong2 soah chiu7 si2-khi3.
	So3-lo5 ia7-si7 chan3-tong5 bou5-sat Su7-the5-hoan2 e5 chit8 e5.

Te7 8 ChiuN

So3-lo5 pek-hai7 kau3-hoe7:
	1) Tui3 hit jit8 khi2, ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 kau3-hoe7 khai-si2 siu7 toa7 pek-hai7; Su3-tou5 i2-goa7 it-chhe3 e5 sin3-tou5, long2 hun-soaN3 khi3 Iu5-thai3 kap Sat-ma2-li7-a Seng2 e5 kok te7-hng.  2) U7 chit8-koa2 khian5-seng5 e5 lang5 bai5-chong3 Su7-the5-hoan2, ui7 i siong-sim toa7 siaN thi5-khau3.
	3) Tan7-si7 So3-lo5 siuN7-boeh hui2-biat8 kau3-hoe7; chhim-jip8 chit8 hou7 koe3 chit8 hou7, bo5 hun cha-pou cha-bou2, thoa sin3-tou5 chhut-lai5, ka7 in koaiN-loh8 kaN-gak8.

Hok-im thoan5 khi3-kau3 Sat-ma2-li7-a:
	4) Hiat-e5 hun-soaN3 khi3 e5 sin3-tou5, chiu7 chit8-si3-ke3 khi3 thoan5 to7-li2.  5) Hui-lek8 khi3 Sat-ma2-li7-a e5 chit8 e5 siaN5-chhi7, tui3 hia e5 lang5 soan-iong5 Ki-tok.  6) Kun5-chiong3 thiaN-kiN3 Hui-lek8 sou2 kong2 e5, khoaN3-kiN3 i sou2 cho3 e5 sin5-chek, chiu7 it-sim it-i3 thiaN-chiong5 i sou2 kong2 e5 oe7.  7) In-ui7 u7 chin-che7 lang5 hou7 sia5-sin5 hu7-sin, hiah-e5 sia5-sin5 toa7 hoah chit8 siaN chiu7 tui3 hiah-e5 lang5 chau2 chhut-lai5; u7 chin-che7 poan3-sui7-e5, pai2-kha-e5 ia7 hou7 i i-ho2 khi3.  8) Thong siaN5-chhi7 e5 lang5 long2 toa7 hoaN-hi2.
	9) Tan7-si7 ti7 chit e5 siaN5-chhi7 u7 chit8 e5 lang5, mia5 kio3-cho3 Se-bun5, chai7-lai5 eng7 sia5-sut8 lai5 be5-hek8 Sat-ma2-li7-a-lang5, chu7-chheng i chin ui2-tai7.  10) Chhi7-lai7 kok kai-kip e5 lang5 long2 thiaN-chiong5 i. In kong2, 몮I chiu7-si7 hit e5 kio3-cho3 tui3 Siong7-chu2 lai5 e5 몬Tai7-leng5-chia2.몭몯  11) In long2 thiaN-chiong5 i, si7 in-ui7 in kau3 taN chin ku2 e5 tiong-kan, long2 siu7 i e5 sia5-sut8 sou2 be5-hek8.  12) Tan7-si7 in chit8-e7 sin3 Hui-lek8 sou2 thoan5 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok e5 Hok-im, kap Ia5-sou Ki-tok e5 mia5, bo5-lun7 cha-pou cha-bou2, long2 lai5 siu7 se2-le2.  13) Lian5 Se-bun5 pun2-sin ia7 lai5 sin3; siu7 se2-le2 liau2-au7 si2-chiong kin-sui5 Hui-lek8, khoaN3-kiN3 i sou2 cho3 e5 ki5-su7 kap sin5-chek, chin kam2-than3.
	14) Ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 Su3-tou5, thiaN-kiN3 Sat-ma2-li7-a-lang5 chiap-siu7 Siong7-chu2 e5 to7-li2, chiu7 chhe-phai3 Pi2-tek kap Iok-han7 khi3 in hia.  15) Chit nng7 ui7 Su3-tou5 chit8-e7 kau3, chiu7 ui7 hiah-e5 sin3-tou5 ki5-to2, hou7 in thang nia2-siu7 Seng3 Leng5.  16) In-ui7 in tu2-tu2 chiah hong7 Chu2 Ia5-sou e5 mia5 siu7 se2-le2, sou2-i2 Seng3 Leng5 iau2-boe7 kang3-lim5 lai5 ti7 in jim7-ho5 lang5.  17) Pi2-tek kap Iok-han7 chit8-e7 ka7 in an3-chhiu2, in chiu7 nia2-siu7 Seng3 Leng5.
	18) Se-bun5 khoaN3-kiN3 Su3-tou5 ka7 in an3-chhiu2, hou7 in nia2-siu7 Seng3 Leng5, i chiu7 hian3-chiN5 hou7 Pi2-tek kap Iok-han7,  19) kong2, 몮ChhiaN2 lin2 ia7 hou7 goa2 chit e5 koan5-peng3, thang hou7 goa2 ka7 i an3-chhiu2 e5 lang5, long2 e7-tang3 nia2-siu7 Seng3 Leng5.몯  20) Tan7-si7 Pi2-tek in3 i kong2: 몮Li2 e5 chiN5 tioh8 kap li2 cho3-hoe2 biat8-bong5! In-ui7 li2 siuN7-cho3 u7 chiN5 chiu7 e7-tang3 be2 Siong7-chu2 e5 in-su3!  21) Goan2 e5 kang-chok bo5 li2 e5 hun7, kap li2 bo5 koan-he7, in-ui7 tui3 Siong7-chu2 khoaN3 khi2-lai5, li2 e5 sim si7 put-cheng3 e5.  22) Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 hoe2-kai2, pang3-sak chit e5 sia5-liam7, ki5-kiu5 Chu2, Chu2 bo5 tiaN7-tioh8 e7 sia3-bian2 li2 sim-lai7 chit khoan2 e5 siuN7-hoat.  23) In-ui7 goa2 khoaN3-chhut li2 siu7 khou2-taN2 e5 tiong3-tok8, siu7 sia5-ok e5 khu-sok.몯  24) Se-bun5 in3 kong2, 몮ChhiaN2 ui7 goa2 ki5-kiu5 Chu2, hou7 goa2 long2 be7 tu2-tioh8 li2 sou2 kong2 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3.몯
	25) Pi2-tek kap Iok-han7 cho3 kian3-cheng3, soan-kang2 Chu2 e5 to7-li2 liau2-au7, in chiu7 tng2-khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, chai7 Sat-ma2-li7-a e5 chin-che7 hiong-chhoan, ian5-lou7 thoan5 Hok-im.

Hui-lek8 kap Ai-the5-o-pek e5 thai3-kam3:
	26) U7 chit8 ui7 Chu2 e5 thian-sai3 ka7 Hui-lek8 kong2: 몮Khi2-lai5, tui3 lam5-peng5 khi3, tui3 hit tiau5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 thau3-kau3 Ka-sat e5 lou7 khi3몯 (Chit tiau5 si7 thau3-koe3 khong3-ia2 e5 lou7.)  27) Hui-lek8 khi2-lai5 chiu7 chhut-hoat khi3. Hit e5 si5, tu2 u7 chit8 e5 Ai-the5-o-pek e5 thai3-kam3 teh-boeh tng2-khi3 in chhu3 e5 tou5-tiong. Chit e5 lang5 si7 teh koan2-li2 Ai-the5-o-pek e5 Li2-ong5 Kan-tai7-ki e5 chai5-cheng3 e5 toa7-koaN.  28) I khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 tiau5-seng3 liau2-au7, tu2 boeh tng2-khi3, che7 ti7 chhia-lai7 teh thak8 tai7-gian5-jin5 I2-sai3-a e5 chheh.  29) Seng3 Leng5 ka7 Hui-lek8 kong2, 몮Li2 kiaN5 oa2-khi3 toe3 hit tiuN chhia.몯  30) Hui-lek8 chiu7 chau2 oa2-khi3 thai3-kam3 hia, thiaN-kiN3 i teh thak8 tai7-gian5-jin5 I2-sai3-a e5 chheh, chiu7 mng7 i kong2, 몮Li2 teh thak8 e5, li2 chai-iaN2 i3-su3 bo5?몯  31) Thai3-kam3 in3 kong2, 몮Bo5 lang5 ka7 goa2 soat-beng5, goa2 na2 e7-tang3 beng5-pek8?몯 I chiu7 chhiaN2 Hui-lek8 peh khit-khi3 chhia-teng2, kap i cho3-hoe2 che7.  32) I teh thak8 hit toaN7 Seng3-keng chiu7-si7 an2-ne:
몮I chhin-chhiuN7 boeh hou7 lang5 khan-khi3 thai5 e5 iuN5, I chhin-chhiuN7 teh hou7 lang5 chian2-mng5 e5 si5, long2 bo5 chhut-siaN e5 iuN5-a2-kiaN2. I long2 bo5 kong2 kah chit8 ku3 oe7.  33) I siu7 khut-jiok8 e5 si5, bo5 lang5 the3 I pian7-hou7. sim2-mih lang5 e7-tang3 biau5-sut8 I e5 hou7-tai7? In-ui7 I ti7 te7-siong7 e5 seN3-mia7 kau3 chiong-kiok8 a7.몯
	34) Thai3-kam3 ka7 Hui-lek8 kong2: 몮ChhiaN2 mng7 li2, tai7-gian5-jin5 kong2 chiah-e5 oe7, si7 chi2 sim2-mih lang5? Si7 chi2 i ka-ti7 a2-si7 chi2 pat8-lang5?몯  35) Hui-lek8 chiu7 khui-chhui3, tui3 hit toaN7 Seng3-keng khai-si2, ka7 i thoan5 koan-he7 Ia5-sou e5 Hok-im.  36) In tui3 hit tiau5 lou7 khi3, khi3-kau3 chit8 e5 u7 chui2 e5 sou2-chai7, thai3-kam3 chiu7 ka7 i kong2: 몮Ti7 chia u7 chui2! Goa2 boeh siu7 se2-le2 u7 sim2-mih chou2-gai7 bo5?몯  ( 37) Hui-lek8 ka7 i kong2, 몮Li2 na7 u7 choan5-sim siong-sin3, chiu7 e7-eng7-tit.몯 I in3 kong2, 몮Goa2 u7; goa2 sin3 Ia5-sou Ki-tok si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 KiaN2.몯  38) Thai3-kam3 chiu7 beng7-leng7 theng5-chhia. Hui-lek8 kap thai3-kam3 nng7 e5 cho3-hoe2 loh8-khi3 chui2-nih8, Hui-lek8 chiu7 ka7 i se2-le2.  39) In tui3 chui2 khi2-lai5 e5 si5, Chu2 e5 Seng3 Leng5 chiu7 ka7 Hui-lek8 chhoa7 chau2-khi3. Thai3-kam3 bo5 koh khoaN3-kiN3 i a3, chiu7 hoaN-hoaN-hi2-hi2 ke3-siok8 li2-heng5.  40) Au7-lai5 Hui-lek8 ti7 A-so2-tou chhut-hian7; i tui3 hia keng-koe3 kok siaN5-chhi7 soan-thoan5 Hok-im, it-tit8 khi3-kau3 Kai-sat-li7-a.

Te7 9 ChiuN

So3-lo5 kui Chu2: (Heng5-toan7 22:6-16; 26:12-18)
	1) So3-lo5 iau2-ku2 it-tit8 khiong2-hat boeh thai5-si2 Chu2 e5 bun5-tou5. I khi3 kiN3 che3-si-tiuN2,  2) Kiu5 i sia2 phe hou7 Tai7-ma2-sek Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 kok hoe7-tng5, siu7-koan5 hou7 i na7 tu2-tioh8 sin3-hong7 Chu2 e5 Chin-to7 e5 lang5, bo5-lun7 lam5-li2, i chiu7 e7-tang3 ka7 in pak8 khi2-lai5, liah8 in tng2-khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.
	3) I chhut-hoat khi3, teh-boeh kau3 Tai7-ma2-sek e5 si5, hut-jian5-kan, tui3 thiN-teng2 u7 chit8 e5 chin kiong5 e5 kng chio3-sia7 loh8-lai5 i e5 chiu-ui5.  4) I chiu7 poah8-to2 loh8-khi3 thou5-kha, thiaN-kiN3 u7 chit8 e5 siaN ka7 i kong2, 몮So3-lo5, So3-lo5, li2 an3-choaN2 pek-hai7 Goa2?몯  5) I mng7 kong2, 몮Chu2 a3, Li2 si7 sim2-mih lang5?몯 Hit e5 siaN in3 i kong2, 몮Goa2 chiu7-si7 li2 sou2 pek-hai7 e5 Ia5-sou.  6) TaN khi2-lai5, jip8-khi3 siaN5-chhi7. Li2 sou2 tioh8-ai3 cho3 e5, khi3-kau3 hia chiu7 e7 siu7 chi2-si7.몯  7) So3-lo5 e5 tang5-phoaN7 tiam7-tiam7 khia7 le7, bo5 kong2 kah chit8 ku3 oe7. In u7 thiaN-kiN3 siaN, tan7-si7 long2 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 iaN2.  8) So3-lo5 tui3 thou5-kha peh khi2-lai5, bak8-chiu peh-khui e5 si5, long2 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 poaN3 hang7.  In chiu7 khan i e5 chhiu2, chhoa7 i jip8-khi3 Tai7-ma2-sek.  9) I ti7 hia saN jit8 ku2 bak8-chiu bo5 khoaN3-kiN3. Hit e5 tiong-kan bo5 chiah8 sim2-mih, ia7 bo5 lim sim2-mih.
	10) Ti7 Tai7-ma2-sek u7 chit8 e5 bun5-tou5 mia5 kio3-cho3 A-na2-ni5-a. Chu2 chai7 i7-siong7 tiong hian2-hian7, ka7 i kio3, 몮A-na2-ni5-a.몯 I in3 kong2, 몮Chu2 a3, goa2 ti7 chia.몯  11) Chu2 ka7 i kong2: 몮Li2 tui3 hit tiau5 Tit8-ke khi3, khi3 hong2-bun7 Iu5-tai7 e5 ka-teng5, chhoe7 chit8 e5 Tai7-sou3-lang5 kio3-cho3 So3-lo5. Li2 e7 khoaN3-kiN3 i teh ki5-to2.  12) I chai7 I7-siong7-tiong u7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 e5 kio3-cho3 A-na2-ni5-a e5 lang5 jip8-lai5, ka7 i an3-chhiu2, hou7 i koh u7 khoaN3-kiN3.몯  13) A-na2-ni5-a in3 kong2: 몮Chu2 a3, goa2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 chin-che7 lang5 ka7 goa2 kong2 chit e5 lang5 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, tui3 Li2 e5 chu2-bin5 cho3 loa7-che7 ok-tok8 e5 tai7-chi3.  14) Peng7-chhiaN2 i lai5 Tai7-ma2-sek, Che3-si-tiuN2 u7 siu7-koan5 hou7 i lai5 liah8 it-chhe3 hou-kiu5 Li2 e5 mia5 e5 lang5.몯  15) Chu2 chiu7 tui3 A-na2-ni5-a kong2: 몮Li2 khi3. I si7 Goa2 keng2-soan2 lai5 su7-hong7 Goa2 e5, boeh po3-iong5 Goa2 e5 mia5 hou7 Goa7-pang-lang5 kap in e5 kun-ong5 i2-kip8 I2-sek-liat8-lang5 chai-iaN2.  16) Goa2 ia7 boeh chi2-si7 i ui7 Goa2 e5 mia5, i tioh8 siu7 loa7-che7 khou2-lan7.몯
	17) A-na2-ni5-a chiu7 khi3, jip8-khi3 hit keng chhu3, ka7 So3-lo5 an3-chhiu2, kong2: 몮HiaN-ti7 So3-lo5, Chu2 chiu7-si7 li2 boeh lai5 e5 tou5-tiong hian2-hian7 hou7 li2 khoaN3 e5 Ia5-sou, chhe-phai3 goa2 lai5 boeh hou7 li2 e5 bak8-chiu koh u7 khoaN3-kiN3, ia7 boeh hou7 li2 chhiong-moa2 Seng3 Leng5.몯  18) Sui5-si5 chiu7 u7 na2 chhin-chhiuN7 hi5-lan5 e5 mih8 tui3 So3-lo5 e5 bak8-chiu lak loh8-lai5, i chiu7 koh u7 khoaN3-kiN3. I chiu7 khia7 khi2-lai5 nia2-siu7 se2-le2.  19) Chiah8-pa2 liau2-au7, the2-lek8 chiu7 koh hok8-goan5.

So3-lo5 chai7 Tai7-ma2-sek thoan5 Hok-im:
	So3-lo5 kap ti7 Tai7-ma2-sek e5 bun5-tou5 cho3-hoe2 toa3 kui2-na7 jit8.  20) I sui5-si5 chiu7 khi3 kok hoe7-tng5, khai-si2 soan-iong5 Ia5-sou, kong2, 몮I si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 KiaN2.몯  21) ThiaN-kiN3 e5 lang5 long2 tioh8-kiaN, mng7 kong2, 몮Ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 sat-hai7 hou-kiu5 chit e5 mia5 e5, kam2 m7-si7 chit e5 lang5? I lai5 chia e5 bok8-tek, kam2 m7-si7 boeh liah8 in tng2-khi3 kau hou7 che3-si-tiuN2?몯
	22) Tan7-si7 So3-lo5 lu2 thoan5 lu2 u7 lek8-liong7. I cheng3-beng5 Ia5-sou si7 bi2-sai3-a, lai5 hou7 hiah-e5 toa3 ti7 Tai7-ma2-sek e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5 bo5 pian7-pok e5 i5-te7.
	23) Koe3-liau2 chin-che7 jit8, Iu5-thai3-lang5 cho3-hoe2 ke3-bou5 boeh sat-hai7 So3-lo5;  24) tan7-si7 in e5 ke3-bou5 hou7 So3-lo5 chai-iaN2. In me5-jit8 toa3 siaN5-mng5 tng-tan2 boeh sat-hai7 i.  25) Tan7-si7 u7 chit8 am3, So3-lo5 e5 bun5-tou5 hou7 i che7 toa3 na5-a2 lai7, tui3 siaN5-chhiuN5-teng2 ka7 i lui7 loh8-khi3.

So3-lo5 khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2:
	26) So3-lo5 khi3-kau3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, siuN7-boeh ka-jip8 bun5-tou5 e5 thoan5-the2; tan7-si7 in long2 tui3 i phau7 kiaN-sim, m7 sin3 i ia7-si7 chit8 e5 bun5-tou5.  27) Tan7-si7 Pa-na2-pa lai5 ka7 i pang-bang5, chhoa7 i khi3 kiN3 Su3-tou5, ka7 in soat-beng5 So3-lo5 ti7 lou7-nih8 an3-choaN2 khoaN3-kiN3 Chu2, Chu2 ka7 i kong2 sim2-mih oe7, i2-kip8 i ti7 Tai7-ma2-sek loa7-nih8 ho2-taN2 hong7 Ia5-sou e5 mia5 thoan5-to7.  28) Chit e5 si5 khi2, So3-lo5 chiu7 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, kap bun5-tou5 cho3-hoe2 chhut-jip8, hong7 Chu2 e5 mia5 ho2-taN2 thoan5-to7.  29) I ia7 kap kong2 Hi-lah8-oe7 e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5 tam5-lun7 pian7-pok, in soah siuN7-boeh ka7 i sat-hai7.  30) HiaN-ti7 chai-iaN2 chit e5 tai7-chi3, chiu7 chhoa7 So3-lo5 loh8-khi3 Kai-sat-li7-a, tui3 hia koh sang3 i tng2-khi3 Tai7-sou3.
	31) Hit e5 si5, choan5 Iu5-thai3, Ka-li7-li7, Sat-ma2-li7-a e5 kau3-hoe7 long2 chin peng5-an, chiam7-chiam7 kian-kou3, sit8-heng5 keng3-ui3 Chu2 e5 seng-oah8, tit-tioh8 Seng3 Leng5 e5 kou2-le7, jin5-sou3 chiu7 it-tit8 cheng7-ka.

Pi2-tek hong2-bun7 Lu7-tai7 kap Iok-phaN3:
	32) Pi2-tek iu5-lek8 kok te7-hng, ia7 u7 khi3 hong2-bun7 toa3 ti7 Lu7-tai7 e5 Siong7-chu2 e5 chu2-bin5.  33) I ti7 hia tu2-tioh8 chit8 e5 lang5, mia5 kio3-cho3 I2-ni5-nga2. I poan3-sui7, peh ni5 ku2 to2 ti7 bin5-chhng5 peh be7 khi2-lai5.  34) Pi2-tek ka7 i kong2: 몮I2-ni5-nga2, Ia5-sou Ki-tok ka7 li2 i-ho2 a3; khi2-lai5 cheng2-li2 li2 e5 bin5-chhng5.몯 I2-ni5-nga2 sui5-si5 chiu7 khi2-lai5.  35) Toa3 ti7 Lu7-tai7 kap Sat-lun5 e5 lang5, long2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 i an2-ne, in chiu7 long2 lai5 kui-hiong3 Chu2.
	36) Ti7 Iok-phaN3 u7 chit8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 sin3-tou5, mia5 kio3-cho3 Tai7-pi2-tai7. (I e5 Hi-lah8-mia5 si7 To-ka, i3-su3 chiu7-si7 Lok8-a2.) I put-si5 cho3 ho2-su7, chin2-che3 san3-lang5.  37) Tu2-tu2 hit e5 si5, i phoa3-peN7 si2-khi3. Lang5 se2 i e5 si-the2, ka7 i khng3 ti7 lau5-teng2 e5 pang5-keng.  38) In-ui7 Lu7-tai7 li7 Iok-phaN3 bo5 loa7 hng7, ti7 Iok-phaN3 e5 bun5-tou5 thiaN-kiN3 Pi2-tek lai5 ti7 Lu7-tai7, in chiu7 chhe nng7 e5 lang5 khi3 khun2-kiu5 i kong2, 몮ChhiaN2 li2 koaN2-kin2 lai5 goan2 chia.몯  39) Pi2-tek chiu7 sui5-si5 peh khi2-lai5, kap in cho3-hoe2 khi3. I chit8-e7 kau3, lang5 chiu7 chhoa7 i khit-khi3 lau5-teng2 e5 pang5-keng. KoaN2-hu7 long2 ui5 toa3 Pi2-tek e5 seng-khu piN teh khau3, theh8 To-ka iau2 teh oah8 e5 si5 cho3 e5 lai7-goa7 saN hou7 i khoaN3.  40) Pi2-tek chiu7 kio3 cheng3-lang5 long2 chhut-khi3, kui7 loh8-khi3 ki5-to2; jian5-au7 oat8 koe3-khi3 tui3 si-the2 kong2, 몮Tai7-pi2-tai7, khi2-lai5!몯 I e5 bak8-chiu chiu7 peh-khui, chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 Pi2-tek chiu7 khi2-lai5 che7.  41) Pi2-tek chhun-chhiu2 khi3 hu5 i khia7 khi2-lai5, jian5-au7 kio3 hiah-e5 sin3-tou5 kap koaN2-hu7 jip8-lai5, chiong koh-oah8 khi2-lai5 e5 To-ka kau hou7 in.  42) Thong Iok-phaN3 long2 chai-iaN2 chit e5 siau-sit, chiu7 u7 chin-che7 lang5 lai5 sin3 Chu2.  43) Pi2-tek ti7 Iok-phaN3 kap chit8 e5 hoan5-phoe5 sai-hu7 Se-bun5 cho3-hoe2 toa3 chin-che7 jit8.

Te7 10 ChiuN

Pi2-tek kap Ko-ni5-liu5:
	1) Ti7 Kai-sat-li7-a u7 chit8 e5 lang5, mia5 kio3-cho3 Ko-ni5-liu5, si7 Lo5-ma2 kun-tui7 I3-tai7-li7-iaN5 e5 lian5-tiuN2.  2) I si7 chit8 e5 keng3-khian5 e5 lang5; i kap choan5-ke e5 lang5 long2 keng3-ui3 Siong7-chu2, khong2-khai3 chin2-che3 Iu5-thai3 e5 san3-chhiah-lang5, put-toan7 teh tui3 Siong7-chu2 ki5-to2.  3) U7 chit8 jit8, e7-pou-si5 chha-put-to saN-tiam2, i chai7 i7-siong7 tiong beng5-beng5 khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 ui7 Siong7-chu2 e5 thian-sai3 jip8-lai5 i hia, ka7 i kio3 chit8 siaN 몮Ko-ni5-liu5!몯  4) I toa7 tioh8-kiaN, liah8 thian-sai3 kim-kim khoaN3, kong2, 몮Chu2 a3, si7 sim2-mih tai7-chi3?몯 Thian-sai3 in3 i kong2: 몮Siong7-chu2 i2-keng chiap-lap8 li2 e5 ki5-to2, ia7 e7-ki3-tit li2 sou2 cho3 e5 chin2-che3.  5) TaN li2 tioh8 chhe-phai3 lang5 khi3 Iok-phaN3, chhiaN2 hit ui7 chheng-hou cho3 Pi2-tek e5 Se-bun5 lai5.  6) I ti7 chit8 e5 hoan5-phoe5 sai-hu7 Se-bun5 e5 chhu3 teh cho3 lang5-kheh. Hit keng chhu3 si7 ti7 hai2-piN.몯  7) Ka7 i kong2-oe7 e5 thian-sai3 khi3 liau2-au7, Ko-ni5-liu5 chiu7 kio3 nng7 e5 chhe-eng7 e5 lang5 i2-kip8 i e5 pou7-siok8 tiong chit8 e5 keng3-khian5 e5 peng-a2 lai5,  8) chiong chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 long2 kong2 hou7 in thiaN, chhe-phai3 in khi3 Iok-phaN3.
	9) Keh-tng2 jit8, in khi3 teh-boeh kau3 Iok-phaN3 e5 si5, chha-put-to tiong-ngou2, Pi2-tek peh khit-khi3 chhu3-teng2 ki5-to2.  10) I pak-tou2 iau, chiu7 siuN7 ai3 chiah8; tan7-si7 in teh ka7 i chun2-pi7 tiong-tau3-tng3 e5 tiong-kan, i soah jip8-sin5 khi3.  11) I khoaN3-kiN3 thiN khui, u7 sim2-mih teh kang3 loh8-lai5, chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 te3 tui3 si3-kak-thau5 tiau3-le3 e5 toa7 te3 pou3, it-tit8 tui7 loh8-lai5 te7-siong7.  12) Lai7-bin7 u7 te2 te7-siong7 kok-chiong2 e5 cheng-seN, thang5-thoa7 kap khong-tiong e5 chiau2-lui7.  13) Hit e5 si5 u7 siaN ka7 i kong2, 몮Pi2-tek, khi2-lai5; thai5 lai5 chiah8.몯  14) Tan7-si7 Pi2-tek kong2, 몮Chu2 a3, chhian-ban7 m7-thang. Goa2 m7-bat chiah8 sim2-mih lah-sap e5, a2-si7 bo5 chheng-khi3 e5.몯  15) Hit e5 siaN te7-ji7 pai2 koh ka7 i kong2: 몮Siong7-chu2 sou2 seng3-hoa3 e5, li2 m7-thang siuN7-cho3 si7 bo5 chheng-khi3 e5.몯  16) An2-ne lian5-lian5 u7 saN pai2, hit te3 toa7 te3 pou3 koh tiau3 tng2-khi3 thiN-teng2.
	17) Pi2-tek tu2 teh siuN7 i sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 chit e5 i7-siong7, siuN7 kah bok8-beng5 ki5-biau7 e5 si5, Ko-ni5-liu5 chhe-phai3 lai5 e5 lang5, i2-keng tham3-thiaN tioh8 Se-bun5 e5 chhu3, lai5 khia7 ti7 mng5-khau2.  18) In toa7 siaN mng7 kong2, 몮U7 chit8 ui7 kio3-cho3 PI2-tek e5 Se-bun5 lai5 toa3 ti7 chia a2 bo5?몯  19) Pi2-tek iau2 teh bek8-siong2 i sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 i7-siong7 e5 si5, Seng3 Leng5 ka7 i kong2: 몮Li2 khoaN3, u7 saN e5 lang5 lai5 boeh chhoe7 li2.  20) Tioh8 koaN2-kin2 loh8-khi3, kap in cho3-hoe2 khi3; m7-thang tiu5-ti5, si7 Goa2 chhe-phai3 in lai5 e5.몯  21) Pi2-tek chiu7 loh8-khi3 kiN3 hiah-e5 lang5, ka7 in kong2: 몮Goa2 chiu7-si7 lin2 teh chhoe7 e5 hit e5 lang5. Lin2 lai5 boeh chhong3 sim2-mih?몯  22) In kong2: 몮Lian5-tiuN2 Ko-ni5-liu5 chhe-phai3 goan2 lai5. I si7 keng3-ui3 Siong7-chu2 e5 gi7-jin5, siu7 choan5 Iu5-thai3-lang5 toa7-toa7 chun-keng3. I siu7 chit8 ui7 seng3 thian-sai3 chi2-si7, boeh chhiaN2 li2 khi3 in chhu3, thang thiaN li2 kang2-to7.  23) Pi2-tek chiu7 chhiaN2 in jip8-khi3, lau5 in toa3 hia koe3-me5.
	Keh-tng2 jit8, Pi2-tek kap in cho3-hoe2 chhut-hoat, kui2-na7 e5 tui3 Iok-phaN3 lai5 e5 hiaN-ti7 ia7 toe3 in khi3.  24) Koh keh-tng2 jit8, in khi3-kau3 Kai-sat-li7-a. Ko-ni5-liu5 liau7-siong2 in e7 lai5, chhiaN2 i e5 chhin-chok8 kap chhin-kin7 e5 peng5-iu2, cho3-hoe2 teh theng3-hau7 i.  25) Pi2-tek tu2 boeh jip8-khi3 e5 si5, Ko-ni5-liu5 chiu7 chhut-lai5 geng5-chiap i, phak loh8-khi3 i e5 kha-cheng5 pai3 i.  26) Tan7-si7 Pi2-tek khan i khi2-lai5, ka7 i kong2, 몮Khi2-lai5, goa2 put-ko3 si7 chit8 e5 lang5.몯  27) Pi2-tek kap i na2 kong2-oe7 na2 kiaN5 jip8-khi3 lai7-bin7, khoaN3-kiN3 chin-che7 lang5 chu7-chip8 ti7 hia.  28) I chiu7 tui3 in kong2: 몮Lin2 ia7 sou2 chai-iaN2, Iu5-thai3-lang5 kap pat8 bin5-chok8 e5 lang5 kau-poe5 a2-si7 lai5-ong2 si7 pi7 kim3-chi2 e5. Tan7-si7 Siong7-chu2 chi2-si7 goa2 bo5-lun7 tui3 sim2-mih lang5, to m7-thang ka7 lang5 khoaN3-cho3 si7 bo5 chheng-khi3 e5, a2-si7 lah-sap e5.  29) Sou2-i2 lin2 chhiaN2 goa2 e5 si5, goa2 bo5 the-si5 chiu7 lai5. TaN goa2 mng7 lin2, lin2 chhiaN2 goa2 lai5 si7 sim2-mih li2-iu5?몯
	30) Ko-ni5-liu5 kong2: 몮Si3 jit8 cheng5, chha-put-to chit e5 si5, e7-pou-si5 saN tiam2, goa2 ti7 chhu3-nih8 teh ki5-to2 e5 si5, hut-jian5-kan u7 chit8 e5 lang5, chheng7 kng iaN3-iaN3 e5 i-hok8 lai5 khia7 toa3 goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5,  31) kong2: 몬Ko-ni5-liu5 a3, Siong7-chu2 chiap-lap8 li2 e5 ki5-to2 a3, ia7 e7-ki3-tit li2 sou2 cho3 e5 chin2-che3.  32) Li2 tioh8 chhe lang5 khi3 Iok-phaN3, chhiaN2 hit ui7 chheng-hou cho3 Pi2-tek e5 Se-bun5 lai5. I ti7 chit8 e5 hoan5-phoe5 sai-hu7 Se-bun5 in chhu3 teh cho3 lang5-kheh. Hit keng chhu3 si7 ti7 hai2-piN.몭  33) Sou2-i2 goa2 sui5-si5 chhe lang5 khi3 chhiaN2 li2 lai5, li2 chin ho2-i3 chiu7 lai5. Hian7-chai7 goan2 long2 chu7-chip8 ti7 Siong7-chu2 e5 bin7-cheng5, boeh thiaN Chu2 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 kong2 it-chhe3 e5 oe7.몯

Pi2-tek e5 kang2-to7:
	34) Pi2-tek chiu7 kong2: 몮Goa2 sit8-chai7 chai-iaN2 Siong7-chu2 tui3 lang5 long2 it-si7 tong5-jin5.  35) Bo5-lun7 sim2-mih bin5-chok8, keng3-ui3 Siong7-chu2, cho3 cheng3-gi7 e5 lang5, long2 e7 siu7 Siong7-chu2 chiap-lap8.  36) Siong7-chu2 thong-koe3 ban7-bin5 e5 Chu2 Ia5-sou Ki-tok, thoan5-pou3 ho5-peng5 e5 Hok-im, chiong chit e5 chin-to7 su3 hou7 I2-sek-liat8-lang5.  37) Lin2 ia7 chai-iaN2 chu7 Iok-han7 thoan5 se2-le2 e5 to7-li2 liau2-au7, tui3 Ka-li7-li7 khai-si2, chai7 Iu5-thai3 choan5-seng2 sou2 hoat-seng e5 tai7-chi3.  38) Lin2 ia7 chai-iaN2 Siong7-chu2 an3-choaN2 hou7 Na2-sat-lek8-lang5 Ia5-sou chhiong-moa2 Seng3 Leng5 kap tai7-leng5. I khi3 kok te7-hng cho3 ho2 tai7-chi3, i-ho2 it-chhe3 siu7 Mou5-kui2 ap-che3 e5 lang5, in-ui7 Siong7-chu2 kap I tong5-chai7.  39) Goan2 chiu7-si7 I chai7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 te7-hng kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 sou2 cho3 e5 tai7-chi3 e5 kian3-cheng3-jin5. In soah ka7 I teng3 toa3 sip8-ji7-ke3-teng2 chhu2-si2.  40) Tan7-si7 te7-saN jit8 Siong7-chu2 hou7 I koh-oah8, hou7 I hian2-hian7;  41) m7-si7 hian2-hian7 hou7 cheng3-lang5 khoaN3, kan-taN hian2-hian7 hou7 Siong7-chu2 su7-sian sou2 keng2-soan2 lai5 ka7 I cho3 kian3-cheng3 e5 lang5 khoaN3. Goan2 chiah-e5 chiu7-si7 Siong7-chu2 hou7 I tui3 si2-lang5 tiong hok8-hoat8 liau2-au7, kap I cho3-hoe2 chiah8, cho3-hoelim2 e5 lang5.  42) I beng7-leng7 goan2 thoan5 Hok-im hou7 cheng3-lang5, cheng3-beng5 I si7 Siong7-chu2 jim7-beng7 I cho3 oah8-lang5 si2-lang5 e5 sim2-phoaN3-koaN.  43) Chiong3 tai7-gian5-jin5 ia7 ka7 I cho3-cheng3 kong2, na7-si7 sin3 Ia5-sou e5 lang5 long2 e7 oa2-kho3 I e5 mia5, tit-tioh8 choe7 e5 sia3-bian2.몯

Goa7-pang-lang5 nia2-siu7 Seng3 Leng5:
	44) Pi2-tek iau2 teh kong2-oe7 e5 si5, Seng3 Leng5 chiu7 kang3-lim5 lai5 ti7 chiah-e5 teh thiaN to7-li2 e5 lang5.  45) Hiah-e5 kap Pi2-tek tui3 Iok-phaN3 cho3-hoe2 lai5 e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 sin3-tou5, khoaN3-kiN3 Siong7-chu2 ia7 siuN2-su3 Seng3 Leng5 e5 in-hui7 hou7 Goa7-pang-lang5, chiu7 toa7 tioh8-kiaN,  46) in-ui7 in thiaN-kiN3 hiah-e5 lang5 jip8-sin5 eng7 ki5-biau7 e5 oe7-gi2 teh chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2 e5 ui2-tai7. Pi2-tek chiu7 kong2:  47) 몮Chiah-e5 lang5 kap goan2 kang7-khoan2, i2-keng nia2-siu7 tioh8 Seng3 Leng5. Sim2-mih lang5 e7 tang3 chou2-chi2 in eng7 chui2 lai5 siu7 se2-le2?몯  48) I chiu7 beng7-leng7 in hong7 Ia5-sou Ki-tok e5 mia5 lai5 siu7 se2-le2. In chiu7 chhiaN2 Pi2-tek kap in koh toa3 hia toa3 kui2-na7-jit8.

Te7 11 ChiuN

Pi2-tek tui3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 kau3-hoe7 e5 po3-ko3:
	1) Su3-tou5 kap toa3 ti7 Iu5-thai3 e5 hiaN-ti7, u7 thiaN-kiN3 kong2 goa7-pang-lang5 ia7 i2-keng chiap-siu7 tioh8 Siong7-chu2 e5 chin-to7 a7.  2) Sou2-i2 Pi2-tek khit-khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 si5, hiah-e5 chu2-tiuN tioh8 ka7 Goa7-pang-lang5 si-heng5 kat-le2 e5 lang5, phe-pheng5 i kong2:  3) 몮Li2 an3-choaN2 jip8-khi3 bo5 siu7 kat-le2 e5 Goa7-pang-lang5 e5 chhu3-nih8 cho3 lang5-kheh, siong7-chhiaN2 kap in cho3-hoe2 chiah8-png7?몯  4) Pi2-tek chiu7 chiong sou2 hoat-seng e5 tai7-chi3, chu7-thau5 kau3-boe2 ka7 in soat-beng5, kong2:
	5) 몮Goa2 ti7 Iok-phaN3 e5 siaN5-chhi7 teh ki5-to2 e5 si5, jip8-sin5 chai7 i7-siong7 tiong khoaN3-kiN3 u7 sim2-mih teh kang3 loh8-lai5, chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 te3 tui3 si3-kak-thau5 tiau3-le3 e5 toa7 te3 pou3, tui3 thiN-teng2 it-tit8 tui7 loh8-lai5 goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5.  6) Goa2 chu3-i3 chit8-e7 khoaN3, ti7 lai7-bin7 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 te7-siong7 e5 cheng-seN, ia2-siu3, thang5-thoa7 kap khong-tiong e5 chiau2-lui7.  7) goa2 ia7 thiaN-kiN3 u7 chit8 e5 siaN ka7 goa2 kong2, 몬Pi2-tek, khi2-lai5; thai5 lai5 chiah8!몭  8) Tan7-si7 goa2 kong2, 몬Chu2 a3, chhian-ban7 m7-thang! Goa2 e5 chhui3 m7-bat chiah8 koe3 sim2-mih lah-sap e5 a2-si7 bo5 chheng-khi3 e5.몭  9) Hit e5 siaN, te7-ji7 pai2 koh tui5 thiN-teng2 ka7 goa2 kong2, '몬Siong7-chu2 sou2 seng3-hoa3 e5, li2 m7-thang siuN7-cho3 si7 bo5 chheng-khi3 e5.몭  10) An2-ne lian5-lian5 u7 saN pai2, chiu7 long2 koh tiau3 tng2-khi3 thiN-teng2.  11) tu2-tu2 hit e5 si5, u7 saN e5 lang5 hou7 lang5 tui3 Kai-sat-li7-a chhe-phai3 lai5 boeh chhoe7 goa2 e5, lai5-kau3 goan2 teh toa3 hit keng chhu3.  12) Seng3 Leng5 kio3 goa2 tioh8 kap in khi3, m7-thang tiu5-ti5. Chit lak8 e5 hiaN-ti7 ia7 kap goa2 cho3-hoe2 khi3 Kai-sat-li7-a, goan2 chiu7 long2 jip8-khi3 Ko-ni5-liu5 in chhu3.  13) I ka7 goan2 kong2 i an2-choaN2 khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 e5 thian-sai3 khia7 ti7 i e5 chhu3-lai7, ka7 i kong2, 몬Li2 chhe-phai3 lang5 khi3 Iok-phaN3, chhiaN2 hit ui7 chheng-hou cho3 Pi2-tek e5 Se-bun5 lai5.  14) I e7 ka7 lin2 kong2 to7-li2, an2-ne li2 kap li2 choan5-ke e5 lang5 chiu7 e7 tit-tioh8 kiu3.몭  15) Goa2 chit8-e7 khai-si2 kong2, Seng3 Leng5 chiu7 kang3-lim5 lai5 in tai7-ke e5 sin-siong7, tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 khi2-chhou kang3-lim5 lai5 lan2 tai7-ke e5 sin-siong7 an2-ne.  16) Goa2 chiu7 siuN7-khi2 Chu2 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, kong2: 몮Iok-han7 si7 eng7 chui2 ka7 lang5 se2-le2, tan7-si7 lin2 e7 siu7 Seng3 Leng5 e5 se2-le2.몭  17) Siong7-chu2 ki3-jian5 siuN2-su3 in-su3 hou7 Goa7-pang-lang5, chhin-chhiuN7 lan2 sin3 Chu2 Ia5-sou Ki-tok e5 si5 siuN2-su3 hou7 lan2 kang7-khoan2, an2-ne goa2 si7 sim2-mih khoan2 e5 lang5, an3-choaN2 e7-tang3 chou2-chi2 Siong7-chu2?몯  18) In thiaN-kiN3 chiah-e5 oe7, chiu7 tiam7-khi3, chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2, kong2, 몮An2-ne khoaN3, Siong7-chu2 ia7 siuN2-su3 hou7 Goa7-pang-lang5 hoan2-hoe2 e5 ki-hoe7, lai5 tit-tioh8 seN3-mia7!몯

Chai7 An-the5-o e5 kau3-hoe7:
	19) Ui7-tioh8 Su7-the5-hoan2 e5 su7-kiaN7 siu7 pek-hai7, si3-soaN3 khi3 hiah-e5 bun5-tou5, chau2 khi3-kau3 Hui-ni5-ki5, Ku-pi2-lou7, An-the5-o kok sou2-chai7. In to3-chhu3 chi2-u7 tui3 Iu5-thai3-lang5 kong2 to7-li2 nia7-nia7.  20) Tan7-si7 bun5-tou5 e5 tiong-kan, u7 kui2-e5-a2 Ku-pi2-lou7-lang5, Kou2-li7-nai7-lang5, in lai5-kau3 An-the5-o, ia7 ka7 Hi-lah8-lang5 thoan5 Chu2 Ia5-sou e5 Hok-im.  21) Chu2 pang-chou7 in, chiu7 u7 chin-che7 lang5 sin3, lai5 kui-hiong3 Chu2.
	22) Chit e5 siau-sit thoan5 lai5-kau3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 kau3-hoe7, in chiu7 chhe-phai3 Pa-na2-pa khi3 An-the5-o.  23) I khi3-kau3 hia, khoaN3-kiN3 Siong7-chu2 loa7-nih8 chiok-hok hia e5 lang5, chiu7 chin hoaN-hi2, peng7-chhiaN2 kou2-le7 in choan5-sim sin3-kho3 Chu2;  24) in-ui7 i si7 chit8 e5 sian7-liong5 e5 lang5, chhiong-moa2 Seng3 Leng5 kap sin3-sim. U7 chin-che7 lang5 hou7 i in2-chhoa7 lai5 kui Chu2.
	25) Jian5-au7 i khi3 Tai7-sou3 chhoe7 So3-lo5,  26) chhoe7-tioh8 liau2-au7, chiu7 chhoa7 i khi3 An-the5-o. Chiok-chiok chit8 ni5 ku2, in nng7 e5 ti7 hia kap kau3-hoe7 e5 lang5 chu7-hoe7, ka3-si7 chin-che7 lang5. Bun5-tou5 siong7 tai7-seng hou7 lang5 chheng-hou cho3 Ki-tok-tou5 e5, si7 ti7 An-the5-o.
	27) Hit tong-si5, u7 kui2-na7 ui7 tai7-gian5-jin5, tui3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 loh8-khi3 An-the5-o.  28) Ki5-tiong u7 chit8 ui7, mia5 kio3-cho3 A-ka-pou3, siu7 Seng3 Leng5 e5 khe2-si7, khia7 khi2-lai5 i7-gian5 choan5 se3-kai3 teh-boeh hoat-seng toa7 ki-hng. (Chai7 Kek-lo2-tiu cho3 hong5-te3 e5 si5-tai7 chin-chiaN3 hoat-seng toa7 ki-hng.)  29) Bun5-tou5 chiu7 koat-i3 boeh chiau3 in kok-lang5 e5 lek8-liong7, kia3 kiu3-che3-phin2 khi3 oan7-chou7 toa3 ti7 Iu5-thai3 Seng2 e5 hiaN-ti7.  30) In chiau3 an2-ne cho3, chiong in sou2 koan-hian3 e5, iu5 Pa-na2-pa kap So3-lo5 keng-chhiu2 kia3 khi3 hou7 kau3-hoe7 e5 tiuN2-lo2.

Te7 12 chiuN

Hi-lut8 pek-hai7 kau3-hoe7:
	1) Hit e5 si5, Hi-lut8-ong5 khai-si2 pek-hai7 kau3-hoe7-tiong kui2-na7 e5 lang5,  2) eng7 to thai5-si2 Iok-han7 e5 a hiaN Nga2-kok.  3) I khoaN3-kiN3 cho3 chit hang7 tai7-chi3 tit-tioh8 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 hoan-sim, chiu7 boeh liah8 Pi2-tek khi2-lai5. (Che si7 chai7 Bo5-kaN3-cheh e5 cheh-ki5 tiong sou2 hoat-seng e5.)  4) Hi-lut8 liah8 Pi2-tek koaiN-loh8 kaN-gak8 liau2-au7, kau hou7 si3 pan e5 peng lun5-liu5 kou3-siu2, mui2 pan u7 si3 e5 peng. Hi-lut8 siuN7-boeh chai7 PoaN5-koe3-cheh au7, ka7 i thoa chhut-lai5 cheng3-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 sim2-phoaN3.  5) Pi2-tek chiu7 an2-ne hou7 lang5 koaiN ti7 kaN-gak8. Hit e5 tiong-kan kau3-hoe7 e5 lang5, put-toan7 jiat8-liat8 ui7 i tui3 Siong7-chu2 ki5-to2.

Pi2-tek chhut-kaN:
	6) Hi-lut8 boeh thoa i chhut-lai5 cheng3-lang5 bin7-cheng5 e5 cheng5 chit8 am3, Pi2-tek hou7 nng7 tiau5 thih-lian7 lian7-le7, khun3 ti7 nng7 e5 peng e5 tiong-kan, ia7 u7 khan3-siu2 ti7 mng5-nih8 teh kou3.  7) Hut-jian5-kan, u7 chit8 ui7 Chu2 e5 thian-sai3 lai5 khia7 toa3 i e5 piN-a, kaN-gak8 lai7 chio3 kah chin kng. Thian-sai3 tah Pi2-tek e5 keng-thau5, ka7 i kio3 chheN2, kong2 몮KoaN2-kin2 khi2-lai5!몯 Thih-lian7 chiu7 tui3 i e5 chhiu2 lak loh8-lai5.  8) Thian-sai3 ka7 i kong2, 몮Khou2-toa3 ha5-le7, e5 chheng7-le7.몯 Pi2-tek chiu7 chiau3 an2-ne cho3. Thian-sai3 iu7-koh kong2, 몮SaN chheng7-le7, toe3 goa2 lai5.몯  9) Pi2-tek chiu7 toe3 i chhut-khi3, m7-chai thian-sai3 sou2 cho3 e5 si7 sit8-chai7 e5; i siuN7-cho3 i si7 teh khoaN3 i7-siong7.  10) In koe3 te7-it koan, iu7 koe3 te7-ji7 koan e5 khan3-siu2-sou2, lai5 kau3 boeh chhut-khi3 siaN5-chhi7 e5 thih-mng5 hia. Hit e5 mng5 chiu7 ka-ti7 khui-khi3. In tui3 hia chhut-khi3, kiaN5 chit8 tiau5 ke-a2 liau2-au7, hut-jian5-kan thian-sai3 chiu7 li7-khui Pi2-tek.
	11) Pi2-tek chiah kak-chheN2 kong2: 몮TaN goa2 chiah chai-iaN2 Chu2 chhe-phai3 I e5 thian-sai3, kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 Hi-lut8 e5 chhiu2 kap Iu5-thai3-lang5 sou2 teh siuN7-boeh cho3 e5 tai7-chi3.몯
	12) I chit8-e7 chai-iaN2 chit e5 cheng5-heng5, chiu7 khi3 Iok-han7 in lau7-bo2 Ma2-li7-a e5 chhu3. (Chit e5 Iok-han7 si7 seN3 Ma2-kho2.) U7 chin-che7 lang5 chu7-chip8 ti7 hia teh ki5-to2.  13) Pi2-tek phah goa7-khau2-mng5 e5 si5, u7 chit8 e5 chhe-eng7 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-na2, kio3-cho3 Lo5-tai7, lai5 mng7 khoaN3 si7 sim2-mih lang5.  14) I jin7-tioh8 Pi2-tek e5 siaN, hoaN-hi2 kah bo5 kou3 khui-mng5, chiu7 chau2 jip8-khi3 ka7 lang5 po3-ko3 kong2 Pi2-tek lai5 khia7 ti7 mng5-khau2.  15) In chiu7 ka7 i kong2, 몮Li2 teh khi2-siau2!몯 Tan7-si7 i kian-chhi5 kong2 khak-sit8 u7-iaN2. In chiu7 kong2, 몮It-teng7 si7 Pi2-tek e5 thian-sai3.몯  16) Hit e5 tiong-kan Pi2-tek iau2 ke3-siok8 teh phah-mng5. In khi3 khui-mng5, chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 i, chiu7 toa7 tioh8-kiaN.  17) Pi2-tek io5-chhiu2 kio3 in tiam7-tiam7, ka7 in soat-beng5 Chu2 an3-choaN2 chhoa7 i tui3 kaN-gak8 chhut-lai5. Iu7-koh kong2, 몮Lin2 chiong chit hang7 tai7-chi3 khi3 po3 hou7 Nga2-kok kap i2-goa7 e5 hiaN-ti7 chai-iaN2.몯 I chiu7 li7-khui hia, khi3 pat8 sou2-chai7.
	18) Kau3 thiN-kng e5 si5, peng-a2 m7-chai Pi2-tek kiu3-keng3 chau2-khi3 tah-ui7, chiu7 loan7-chhau-chhau.  19) Hi-lut8 chiu7 ha7-leng7 in khi3 chhoe7 Pi2-tek, tan7-si7 chhoe7 bo5, chiu7 sim2-mng7 khan2-siu2 e5 peng; sim2-mng7 liau2-au7, beng7-leng7 tioh8 ka7 in chhu2 si2-heng5.
	Jian5-au7 Hi-lut8 li7-khui Iu5-thai3, loh8-khi3 toa3 Kai-sat-li7-a toa3 u7 chit8 toaN7 si5-kan.

Hi-lut8 e5 si2-bong5:
	20) Chhui-lo5 kap Se-tun3 e5 lang5 tek-choe7 tioh8 Hi-lut8, hou7 i chin siu7-khi3; sou2-i2 in chiu7 lian5-hap8 phai3 lang5 khi3 kiN3 Hi-lut8. In tai7-seng be2-siu kiong-lai7 tai7-sin5 Pek-lah-su7-tou, lai5 ka7 Hi-lut8 kiu5-ho5, in-ui7 in e5 kok-lai7 e5 niu5-sit8, si7 siu7 Hi-lut8 e5 leng2-thou2 lai5 teh kiong3-eng3 e5.
	21) Hi-lut8 chiu7 chai7 chi2-teng7 e5 jit8, chheng7 ong5-hok8, che7 toa3 ong5-cho7, tui3 in ian2-kang2.  22) Cheng3-lang5 chiu7 hoah kong2,  몮Che si7 sin5 e5 siaN, m7-si7 lang5 e5 siaN!몯  23) Tan7-si7 Hi-lut8 bo5 kui eng5-iau7 hou7 Siong7-chu2, sou2-i2 Chu2 e5 thian-sai3 chiu7 chek-si5 ka7 i phah-to2 loh8-khi3. I chiu7 hou7 thang5 ka7 si2.
	24) Siong7-chu2 e5 chin-to7 lu2 thoan5 lu2 khoah, lu2 heng-ong7.
	25) Pa-na2-pa kap So3-lo5 oan5-seng5 in e5 oan7-chou7 e5 su3-beng7, chiu7 chhoa7 seN3 Ma2-kho2 e5 Iok-han7, kap in cho3-hoe2 tui3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 tng2-lai5.

Te7 13 ChiuN

Pa-na2-pa kap So3-lo5 siu7 soan2-phai3:
	1) Chai7 An-the5-o e5 kau3-hoe7 tiong, u7 kui2-na7 ui7 tai7-gian5-jin5 kap kau3-su; chiu7-si7 Pa-na2-pa, kio3-cho3 몮Ou-lang5몯 e5 Se-bian7, Kou2-li7-nai7-lang5 Lou7-kiu5, kap Hun-hong e5 ong5 Hi-lut8 cho3-hoe2 siu7 iuN2-chhi7 toa7-han3 e5 Ma2-liam7, i2-kip8 So3-lo5.  2) In teh keng3-pai3 Chu2, teh kim3-chiah8 e5 si5, Seng3 Leng5 ka7 in kong2, 몮Tioh8 ka7 Goa2 hun-phai3 Pa-na2-pa kap So3-lo5, khi3 cho3 Goa2 tiau3 in cho3 e5 kang-chok.몯  3) In kim3-chiah8 ki5-to2 liau2-au7, chiu7 ka7 in nng7 e5 an3-chhiu2, jian5-au7 chhe-phai3 in chhut-hoat.

Chai7 Ku-pi2-lou7:
	4) Pa-na2-pa kap So3-lo5 siu7 Seng3 Leng5 chhe-phai3, loh8-khi3 Se-liu5-ki, tui3 hia che7 chun5 khi3 Ku-pi2-lou7-tou2.  5) In khi3-kau3 Sat-liap8-bi2 e5 si5, chiu7 chai7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 hoe7-tng5 thoan5-kang2 Siong7-chu2 e5 chin-to7. Iok-han7 ia7 cho3-hoe2 ka7 in pang-bang5.
	6) Hit e5 tou2(NNto2) in thau5 kiaN5-kau3 boe2, khi3-kau3 PhaN3-hut, ti7 hia tu2-tioh8 chit8 e5 mou5-sut8-su. I si7 ke2-cho3 sian-ti e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5, mia5 kio3-cho3 Pa-ia5-sou.  7) I si7 chit e5 tou2(NNto2) e5 hian5-beng5 e5 chong2-tok Su7-kiu5 Po2-lo5 e5 sui5-oan5. Chong2-tok tiau3 Pa-na2-pa kap So3-lo5 lai5 boeh thiaN in kang2 Siong7-chu2 e5 chin-to7.  8) Tan7-si7 hit e5 mou5-sut8-su e5 I2-lu7-ma2 (che si7 i e5 Hi-lah8-mia5) chou2-tong3 in nng7 e5, siuN7-boeh hong5-chi2 chong2-tok lai5 sin3 Chu2.  9) Tan7-si7 So3-lo5 --- ia7 kio3-cho3 Po2-lo5 --- chhiong-moa2 Seng3 Leng5; liah8 mou5-sut8-su kim-kim khoaN3,  10) kong2: 몮Li2 chit e5 Mou5-kui2 e5 kiaN2! Li2 si7 it-chhe3 kong-gi7 e5 tek8-jin5; chhiong-moa2 pah-poaN sia5-ok e5 kui2-ke3. Li2 an3-choaN2 iau2-ku2 boeh ong2-khut Chu2 e5 cheng3-to7?  11) TaN Chu2 boeh ka7 li2 he7-chhiu2 a3; li2 e7 chheN-me5, li2 e7 chiam7-si5 lian5 jit8-thau5 ia7 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3.몯 I2-lu7-ma2 e5 bak8-chiu chek-si5 hou7 ou-bu7 ta3 khi2-lai5, bong-lai5 bong-khi3, siuN7-boeh chhoe7 lang5 ka7 i khan-chhiu2 chhoa7-lou7.  12) Chong2-tok khoaN3-kiN3 sou2 hoat-seng e5 tai7-chi3, ia7 thiaN-tioh8 koan-he7 Chu2 e5 to7-li2, toa7-toa7 siu7 kam2-tong7, chiu7 chiaN5-cho3 sin3-tou5.

Chai7 Pi2-se-ti2 e5 An-the5-o:
	13) Po2-lo5 kap i e5 tang5-phoaN7 tui3 PhaN3-hut khui-chun5 lai5-kau3 Pong5-hui-li7-a Seng2 e5 Piat8-ka; tan7-si7 Iok-han7 toa3 hia kap in li7-khui, tng2-khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.  14) In chiu7 tui3 Piat8-ka koh khi3-kau3 Pi2-se-ti2 e5 An-the5-o; chai7 An-hioh-jit8 jip8-khi3 hoe7-tng5 che7.  15) Thak8 Mou5-se e5 Lut8-hoat kap tai7-gian5-jin5 sia2 e5 chheh liau2-au7, hiah-e5 hoe7-tng5-tiuN2 hoan-hu3 lang5 ka7 in kong2: 몮HiaN-ti7 a3, lin2 na7 u7 sim2-mih boeh khoan3-bian2 cheng3-lang5 e5 oe7, chhiaN2 lin2 ka7 cheng3-lang5 kong2.몯  16) Po2-lo5 chiu7 khia7 khi2-lai5, giah8-chhiu2 khi2-lai5 kio3 in tiam7-tiam7 thiaN, chiah khui-chhui3 kong2:
몮I2-sek-liat8 tong5-pau kap it-chhe3 keng3-ui3 Siong7-chu2 e5 lang5 a3, chhiaN2 lin2 thiaN!  17) Chiah-e5 I2-sek-liat8-lang5 e5 Siong7-chu2 keng2-soan2 lan2 e5 chou2-sian, I2-sek-liat8 e5 chu2-bin5 khi3 Ai-kip8 e5 te7-thou2 cho3 chhut-goa7-lang5 teh ki-chu7 e5 tiong-kan, hou7 in chiaN5-cho3 ui2-tai7 e5, iong7 I e5 tai7-leng5 chhoa7 in chau2-chhut Ai-kip8,  18) iu7-koh chai7 khong3-ia2 tiong iuN2-chhi7 in si3-chap8 ni5 ku2.  19) Jian5-au7 hui2-biat8 Ka-lam5 te7-hng e5 chhit e5 bin5-chok8, chiong chit e5 te7-thou2 hou7 in ke3-seng5.  20) Chit e5 ki5-kan tai7-iok u7 si3-pah gou7-chap8 ni5 ku2. Jian5-au7 ui7 in jim7-beng7 su7-su, it-tit8 ke3-siok8 kau3 tai7-gian5-jin5 Sat-bou7-ni2 e5 si5.  21) Au7-lai5 in khun2-kiu5 ai3-boeh chit8 e5 ong5 e5 si5, Siong7-chu2 chiu7 chiong Pian7-nga2-bin2 chi-phai3 tiong Ki-su7 e5 kiaN2 So3-lo5 siuN2-su3 hou7 in, lip8 i cho3 ong5 cho3 si3-chap8-ni5.  22) Siong7-chu2 ka7 So3-lo5 hoe3-ui7 liau2-au7, lip8 Tai7-pit cho3 in e5 ong5; ui7 Tai7-pit8 cho3-cheng3 kong2: 몬Goa2 chhoe7 tioh8 Ia5-se e5 kiaN2 Tai7-pit8. I si7 sun7-chiong5 Goa2 e5 sim e5 lang5. I e7 chun-chiau3 Goa2 e5 i3-su3 cho3 it-chhe3 e5 tai7-chi3.몭  23) Siong7-chu2 chiau3 I e5 eng3-un2, tui3 Tai7-pit8 e5 hou7-e3 ka7 I2-sek-liat8-lang5 siat-lip8 chit8 ui7 Kiu3-chu2, chiu7-si7 Ia5-sou.  24) Ia5-sou lai5-lim5 i2-cheng5, Iok-han7 tui3 it-chhe3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 chu2-bin5 soan-iong5 kong2 tioh8 hoe2-kai2 lai5 siu7 se2-le2.  25) Iok-han7 teh-boeh oan5-seng5 i e5 su3-beng7 e5 si5, tui3 cheng3-lang5 kong2: 몬Lin2 siuN7 goa2 si7 sim2-mih lang5? Goa2 m7-si7 lin2 sou2 teh tan2-hau7 Hit-ui7. Tan7-si7 I ti7 goa2 e5 au7-bin7 teh lai5, goa2 lian5 thau2 I e5 e5-toa3 to be7-kham-tit.몭 몮
	26) 몮Chu-ui7 hiaN-ti7, A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 kiaN2-sun i2-kip8 lin2 it-chhe3 keng3-ui3 Siong7-chu2 e5 lang5 a3. Chit e5 chin2-kiu3 e5 chin-to7 si7 thoan5 hou7 lan2 e5.  27) In-ui7 toa3 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 lang5, kap in e5 koaN-tiuN2 m7-bat I si7 Kiu3-chu2, ia7 bo5 liau2-kai2 mui2 An-hioh-jit8 sou2 thak8 e5 tai7-gian5-jin5 e5 oe7, in chiu7 ka7 Ia5-sou phoaN3-choe7, lai5 eng3-giam7 tai7-gian5-jin5 e5 i7-gian5멖 28) Sui-jian5 in be-tang chhoe7-chhut li2-iu5 lai5 ka7 I teng7 si2-choe7, in kiu5 Pi2-liap8-to tioh8 ka7 I chhu2 si2-heng5.  29) In sit8-heng5 Seng3-keng sou2 ki3-chai3 koan-he7 I it-chhe3 e5 tai7-chi3 liau2-au7, chiu7 tui3 sip8-ji7-ke3 ka7 I pang3 loh8-lai5, khng3 toa3 bong7-lai7.  30) Tan7-si7 Siong7-chu2 hou7 I tui3 si2-lang5 tiong koh-oah8 khi2-lai5.  31) I kui2-na7 jit8 kan, hian2-hian7 hou7 hiah-e5 tui3 Ka-li7-li7 kap I cho3-hoe2 khi2-lai5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 lang5 khoaN3. TaN chiah-e5 lang5 chai7 I2-sek-liat8-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 teh ka7 Ia5-sou cho3 kian3-cheng3.  32) Goan2 lai5 chia si7 boeh ka7 lin2 po3 ho2 siau-sit: chiu7-si7 Siong7-chu2 tuil3an e5 chou2-sian sou2 eng3-un2 e5 tai7-chi3.  33) I i2-keng hou7 Ia5-sou koh-oah8 khi2-lai5, lai5 ka7 lan2 chiah-e5 cho3 in e5 hou7-e3 e5, oan5-seng5 I e5 eng3-un2 a3. Chhin-chhiuN7 Si-phian te7-ji7 phian ia7 u7 ki3-chai3 kong2:
몬Li2 si7 Goa2 e5 KiaN2, Goa2 kin-na2-jit8 seN Li2.몬
34) Siong7-chu2 hou7 I tui3 si2-lang5 tiong koh-oah8 khi2-lai5, be7 koh-chai3 hou7 I hu2-pai7 khi3. Koan-he7 chit hang7 tai7-chi3, Siong7-chu2 kong2:
몬Goa2 boeh chiong tui3 Tai7-pit8 sou2 eng3-un2 hit e5 seng3-kiat koh khak-sit8 e5 chiok-hok, siuN2-su3 hou7 lin2.몭
35) Ti7 Si-phian e5 leng7-goa7 chit8 sou2-chai7, I ia7 u7 kong2,
몬Li2 be7 hou7 Li2 e5 Seng3-chia2 hu2-pai7 khi3.몭
36) In-ui7 Tai7-pit8 chai7-se3 chun-heng5 Siong7-chu2 e5 chi2-i3, si2 liau2-au7 pi7 bai5-chong3 ti7 i e5 chou2-sian e5 piN-a, ia7 hu2-pai7 khi3.  37) Tan7-si7 Siong7-chu2 tui3 si2-lang5-tiong hou7 I koh-oah8 khi2-lai5 Hit-ui7, bo5 keng-giam7 tioh8 hu2-pai7.  38) Sou2-i2 chu-ui7 hiaN-ti7 a3, lin2 tioh8 chai-iaN2, sia3-choe7 e5 to7-li2 si7 thong-koe3 chit ui7 Ia5-sou thoan5 lai5 hou7 lin2 e5; lin2 kho3 Mou5-se e5 Lut8-hoat ia7 be7-tang3 tit-tioh8 sia3-choe7.  39) Na7 sin3 I e5 lang5, it-chhe3 e5 choe7 long2 e7 tit-tioh8 sia3-bian2.  40) Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 kin2-sin7, lin2 chiah be7 khi3 tu2-tioh8 tai7-gian5-jin5 sou2 kong2 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3, chiu7-si7 kong2:
41) 몬KhoaN3-bai7 le3! Lin2 chiah-e5 gau biau2-si7 lang5 e5, Tioh8 kiaN-hiaN5, tioh8 biat8-bong5; In-ui7 chai7 lin2 e5 si5-jit8, Goa2 boeh cho3 chit8 hang7 tai7-chi3. Ka2-su2 u7 lang5 ka7 lin2 soeh-beng5, Lin2 ia7 bo5 boeh sin3.몭
42) Po2-lo5 kap Pa-na2-pa teh-boeh tui3 hoe7-tng5 chhut-khi3 e5 si5, cheng3-lang5 chhiaN2 in au7 An-hioh-jit8 koh lai5 kong2 chiah-e5 to7-li2 hou7 in thiaN.  43) San3-hoe7 liau2-au7, u7 chin-che7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 kap kai2-chong lai5 jip8 Iu5-thai3-kau3 hiah-e5 khian5-seng5 e5 Goa7-pang-lang5, toe3 Po2-lo5 kap Pa-na2-pa chhut-khi3. In nng7 e5 Su3-tou5 chiu7 kap in tam5-oe7, khoan3-bian2 in tioh8 kho3 Siong7-chu2 e5 in-tian2 ke3-siok8 seng-oah8.
