	44) Au7 An-hioh-jit8, chha-put-to thong siaN5-chhi7 e5 lang5, long2 chu7-chip8 lai5 boeh thiaN Chu2 e5 chin-to7.  45) Tan7-si7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 lang5 hiah che7, in moa2-sim khi2 chit-tou3; pian7-pok Po2-lo5 kong2 e5 oe7, iu7-koh ka7 i hui2-pong3.  46) Po2-lo5 kap Pa-na2-pa chiu7 koh-khah ho2-taN2 kong2: 몮Siong7-chu2 e5 chin-to7 pun2-lai5 si7 eng-kai tai7-seng thoan5 hou7 lin2, tan7-si7 ki3-jian5 lin2 khi3-choat8 chit e5 chin-to7, siuN7-cho3 lin2 ka-ti7 be7-kham-tit tit-tioh8 eng2-seng, sou2-i2 goan2 chiu7 choan2-hiong3 tui3 Goa7-pang-lang5 khi3.  47) In-ui7 Chu2 beng7-leng7 goan2 kong2:
몬goa2 siat-lip8 li2 cho3 Goa7-pang-lang5 e5 kng, Thang hou7 li2 chiong Goa2 e5 chin2-kiu3 toa3 khi3-kau3 thiN-piN hai2-kak.몭몯
	48) goa7-pang-lang5 thiaN-kiN3 an2-ne chin hoaN-hi2, chan3-bi2 Chu2 e5 chin-to7. Hiah-e5 chu3-teng7 boeh hou7 in tit-tioh8 eng2-seng e5 lang5, long2 piN3-cho3 sin3-tou5.
	49) An2-ne Chu2 e5 chin-to7, chai7 hit e5 te7-hng thoan5 khi3-kau3 tak8 sou2-chai7.  50) Tan7-si7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 sian3-tong7 keng3-pai3 Siong7-chu2 e5 kui3-hu7-jin5 kap chhi7-lai7 e5 leng2-to7 kai-kip e5 lang5 pek-hai7 Po2-lo5 kap Pa-na2-pa, ka7 in khu-tiok8 chhut-keng2.  51) Chit nng7 ui7 Su3-tou5 chiu7 hiong3 cheng3-lang5 poaN7 kha e5 thou5-hun2 piau2-si7 khong3-gi7, jian5-au7 khi3 I2-ko-liam7.  52) Chai7 An-the5-o e5 bun5-tou5 long2 chhiong-moa2 hi2-lok8 kap Seng3 Leng5.

Te7 14 ChiuN

Chai7 I2-ko-liam7:
	1) Po2-lo5 kap Pa-na2-pa chai7 I2-ko-liam7, ia7 chiau3 an2-ne jip8-khi3 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 hoe7-tng5 kang2-lun7 to7-li2, chiu7 u7 chin-che7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 kap Hi-lah8-lang5 lai5 sin3.  2) Tan7-si7 hiah-e5 bo5 boeh sin3 e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5, sian3-tong7 Goa7-pang-lang5, hou7 in tui3 sin3 Chu2 e5 hiaN-ti7 phau7 ok-i3.  3) Chit nng7 ui7 Su3-tou5 toa3 hia toa3 chin ku2, oa2-kho3 Chu2 ho2-taN2 kong2 to7-li2. Chu2 siuN2-su3 in leng5-lek8 hian2 chiong2-chiong2 e5 sin5-chek kap ki5-su7, lai5 cheng3-beng5 in sou2 soan-kang2 e5 in-thiong2 e5 to7-li2 si7 chin-sit8 e5.  4) Chhi7-lai7 e5 lang5 chiu7 hun-cho3 nng7 phai3; u7-e5 oa2 Iu5-thai3-lang5, u7-e5 oa2 Su3-tou5.
	5) Hit e5 si5, Goa7-pang-lang5 kap Iu5-thai3-lang5 kap in e5 koaN-tiuN2 koat-teng7 boeh leng5-jiok8 Su3-tou5, eng7 chioh8-thau5 ka7 in tim3.  6) Su3-tou5 chit8-e7 chai-iaN2 chit hang7 tai7-chi3, chiu7 to5-chau2 khi3 Lu7-ko-ni5 Seng2 e5 Lou7-su7-tek kap Tek8-pi3 hit nng7 e5 siaN5-chhi7 kap chiu-ui5 e5 te7-hng.  7) In toa3 hia ke3-siok8 thoan5 Hok-im.

Chai7 Lou7-su7-tek kap Tek8-pi3:
	8) Ti7 Lou7-su7-tek u7 chit8 e5 pai2-kha-e5. I chu7 chhut-si3 chiu7 poan3-sui7, tiaN7-tiaN7 che7-le7, kau3 taN long2 be7 kiaN5-lou7.  9) I thiaN Po2-lo5 kong2 to7-li2. Po2-lo5 liah8 i kim-kim khoaN3, khoaN3 kiN3 i u7 sin3-sim, e7 i tit,  10) chiu7 toa7-siaN kong2, 몮Khia7 khi2-lai5, siang-kha khia7 tit8-tit8!몯 Hit e5 lang5 chiu7 thiau3 khi2-lai5 khai-si2 kiaN5.  11) Cheng3-lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 Po2-lo5 sou2 cho3 e5 tai7-chi3, chiu7 eng7 in Lu7-ko-ni5 e5 oe7, toa7-siaN kong2, 몮Sin5-beng5 chioh lang5 e5 heng5-the2 kang3-lim5 lai5 lan2 chia!몯  12) In ka7 Pa-na2-pa  chheng-hou cho3 Tiu-su7, ka7 Po2-lo5 chheng-hou cho3 Hi-ni2-bi2, in-ui7 Po2-lo5 si7 chu2-kang2-chia2.  13) Ti7 siaN5-chhi7 e5 goa7-bin7 e5 Tiu-su7-bio7 e5 che3-si, khan kui2-na7 chiah koa3 hoe-khoan5 e5 gu5-kang2 lai5-kau3 toa7-mng5-khau2. I kap cheng3-lang5 boeh hian3 seng-le2 hou7 Su3-tou5.  14) Pa-na2-pa kap Po2-lo5 chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 an2-ne, chiu7 thiah-phoa3 in ka-ti7 e5 saN, chong5 jip8-khi3 kun5-chiong3 e5 tiong-kan, hoah kong2:  15) 몮Lin2 chiah-e5 lang5, an3-choaN2 boeh cho3 chit khoan2 tai7-chi3? Goan2 ia7 kap lin2 kang7-khoan2, put-ko3 si7 lang5 nia7-nia7! Goan2 lai5 chia thoan5 Hok-im hou7 lin2, si7 boeh hou7 lin2 li7-khui chiah-e5 khang-hi bu5-ek e5, lai5 kui-hiong3 Hit-ui7 chhong3-cho7 thiN, te7, hai2 i2-kip8 u2-tiu7 ban7-but8 e5 eng2-seng e5 Siong7-chu2.  16) Chai7 koe3-khi3 e5 se3-tai7, Siong7-chu2 iong5-un2 ban7-bin5 khi3 kiaN5 in ka-ti7 e5 lou7.  17) Tan7-si7 I si5-siong5 eng7 I sou2 cho3 e5 ho2-su7 lai5 hian2-si7 I e5 pun2-seng3: chiu7-si7 tui3 thiN-teng2 kang3-hou7, an3-si5 hou7 lang5 siu-seng5; siuN2-su3 lin2 chiah8-niu5, hou7 lin2 e5 sim chhiong-moa2 hi2-lok8.몯  18) Su3-tou5 sui-jian5 u7 kong2 chiah-e5 oe7, iau2-ku2 bo5 hoat-tou7 thang chou2-chi2 kun5-chiong3 hian3 seng-le2 hou7 in.
	19) Hit e5 si5, u7 chit8-koa2 Iu5-thai3-lang5 tui3 An-the5-o kap I2-ko-liam7 lai5, sian3-tong7 kun5-chiong3 eng7 chioh8-thau5 tim3 Po2-lo5, siuN7 kong2 i si2-khi3 a3, chiu7 ka7 i thoa chhut-khi3 siaN5-goa7.  20) Tan7-si7 bun5-tou5 long2 ui5 oa2-lai5 i hia e5 si5, i chiu7 khi2-lai5, to3 tng2-khi3 siaN5-lai7. Keh-tng2-jit8, i kap Pa-na2-pa cho3-hoe2 khi3 Tek8-pi3.

Tng2-khi3 Su7-li7-a Seng2 e5 An-the5-o:
	21) Po2-lo5 kap Pa-na2-pa ti7 Tek8-pi3 thoan5 Hok-im, hou7 chin-che7 lang5 lai5 cho3 bun5-tou5. Jian5-au7 in chiu7 to3 tng2-khi3 Lou7-su7-tek, khi3 I2-ko-liam7, iu7-koh khi3 An-the5-o.  22) In kian-kou3 bun5-tou5 e5 sim, kou2-le7 in kian-chhi5 sin3-sim, kong2: 몮Lan2 tioh8 keng-koe3 chin-che7 khou2-lan7 chiah e7-tang3 chin3-jip8 Siong7-chu2 e5 kok.몯  23) Chai7 kok kau3-hoe7-tiong ka7 in jim7-beng7 tiuN2-lo2, kim3-chiah8 ki5-to2 liau2-au7, chiu7 chiong in kau-thok hou7 in sou2 sin3-kho3 e5 Chu2.
	24) In nng7 ui7 keng-koe3 Pi2-se-ti2, jian5-au7 lai5-kau3 Pong5-hui-li7-a.  25) Toa3 Piat8-ka kong2 to7-li2 liau2-au7, chiu7 loh8-khi3 A-tai7-li7.  26) In tui3 hia che7-chun5 tng2-khi3 An-the5-o, in khah-cha2 tit-tioh8 Siong7-chu2 e5 in-hui7, siu7 cheng3-lang5 e5 kau-thok, khi3 cho3 hian7-chai7 i2-keng oan5-seng5 e5 kang-chok, chiu7-si7 ti7 chit e5 sou2-chai7.
	27) In lai5-kau3 An-the5-o, chiu7 chu7-chip8 kau3-hoe7 e5 cheng3-lang5, ka7 in kong2 Siong7-chu2 kap in cho3-hoe2 sou2 cho3 it-chhe3 e5 tai7-chi3, i2-kip8 Siong7-chu2 an3-choaN2 ka7 Goa7-pang-lang5 khui-lou7 hou7 in lai5 sin3.  28) In chiu7 ti7 hia kap bun5-tou5 cho3-hoe2 toa3 chin-ku2.

Te7 15 ChiuN

Chai7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 khai-hoe7:
	1) U7 kui2-na7 e5 lang5 tui3 Iu5-thai3 loh8-khi3 An-the5-o, kau3-hun3 hiaN-ti7 kong2: 몮Lin2 na7 bo5 chiau3 Mou5-se e5 Lut8-hoat e5 kui-ki2 siu7 kat-le2, lin2 be7-tang3 tit-tioh8 kiu3.몯  2) Po2-lo5 i2-kip8 Pa-na2-pa kap in kek-liat8 pian7-lun7, ui7 chit hang7 tai7-chi3 khi2 hun-cheng; sou2-i2 cheng3-lang5 chiu7 koat-teng7 chi2-phai3 Po2-lo5 kap Pa-na2-pa i2-kip8 ti7 An-the5-o e5 i2-goa7 kui2-na7 e5 lang5, chiuN7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, ui7 chit hang7 bun7-te5 khi3 kiN3 Su3-tou5 kap tiuN2-lo2.
	3) Kau3-hoe7 sang3 in chhut-hoat, in keng-koe3 Hui-ni5-ki kap Sat-ma2-li7-a, po3-ko3 kong2 goa7-pang-lang5 an3-choaN2 lai5 kui Chu2; chit e5 siau-sit hou7 cheng3 hiaN-ti7 toa7 hoaN-hi2.  4) In kau3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 si5, siu7 kau3-hoe7 Su3-tou5 kap tiuN2-lo2 e5 hoan-geng5, chiu7 po3-ko3 Siong7-chu2 kap in sou2 cho3 it-chhe3 e5 tai7-chi3 hou7 in thiaN.  5) Tan7-si7 u7 kui2-na7 e5 siok8 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 sin3-tou5, khia7 khi2-lai5 kong2, 몮Goa7-pang-lang5 tioh8 siu7 kat-le2, kio3 in tioh8 chun-siu2 Mou5-se e5 Lut8-hoat.
	6) Hiah-e5 Su3-tou5 kap tiuN2-lo2 chiu7 chu7-chip8 lai5 tho2-lun7 chit e5 bun7-te5.  7) Pian7-lun7 chin ku2 liau2-au7, Pi2-tek chiu7 khia7 khi2-lai5, kong2: 몮Chu-ui7 hiaN-ti7, lin2 chai-iaN2 Siong7-chu2 cha2-cha2 chiu7 tui3 lin2 tiong-kan keng2-soan2 goa2 lai5 Goa7-pang-lang5 thoan5-pou3 Hok-im e5 to7-li2 hou7 in thiaN, lai5 sin3.  8) Chai-iaN2 lang5 e5 lai7-sim e5 Siong7-chu2, chhin-chhiuN7 tui3-thai7 lan2 an2-ne, ia7 siuN2-su3 Seng3 Leng5 hou7 Goa7-pang-lang5 lai5 piau2-si7 I u7 ka7 in chiap-lap8.  9) I khoaN3 lan2 kap in long2 bo5 chha-piat8. I kiat-cheng7 in e5 sim si7 in-ui7 in u7 sin3.  10) An2-ne lin2 si7 an3-choaN2 boeh chiong lan2 e5 chou2-sian kap lan2 long2 be7-tang3 gia5 e5 ke5, khoa3 toa3 goa7-pang e5 bun5-tou5 e5 keng-thau5, lai5 chhi3-tham3 Siong7-chu2?  11) Tan7-si7 lan2 siong-sin3 kong2 oa2-kho3 Chu2 Ia5-sou e5 in-hui7 e7-tang3 tit-tioh8 kiu3, in ia7-si7 an2-ne.몯
	12) ThiaN-tioh8 an2-ne, cheng3-lang5 long2 tiam7-khi3. In chiu7 koh thiaN Pa-na2-pa kap Po2-lo5 po3-ko3 Siong7-chu2 thong-koe3 in nng7 lang5, chai7 Goa7-pang-lang5 e5 tiong-kan sou2 cho3 it-chhe3 e5 ki5-su7 kap sin5-chek.  13) In kong2 soah e5 si5, Nga2-kok chiu7 kong2: 몮Chu-ui7 hiaN-ti7! ChhiaN2 thiaN goa2 kong2.  14) Se-bun5 Pi2-tek tu2-chiah u7 soat-beng5 Siong7-chu2 khi2-thau5 an2-choaN2 khoaN3-kou3 Goa7-pang-lang5, tui3 in e5 tiong-kan soan2-chhut chit8-e5 jin5-bin5, lai5 kui-siok8 I pun2-sin.  15) Tai7-gian5-jin5 e5 oe7 ia7 kap che oan5-choan5 it-ti3. Tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 Seng3-keng ki3-chai3 kong2:
16) 몬Jian5-au7 Goa2 boeh koh tng2-lai5, Goa2 boeh tiong7-kian3 Tai5-pit8 to2 loh8-khi3 e5 chhu3; Goa2 boeh tiong7-siu hong-hoe3 khi3 e5 sou2-chai7, Tiong7-sin kian3-cho7 khi2-lai5.  17) Hou7 ki5-tha e5 jin5-bin5, Kap it-chhe3 Goa2 tiau3-lai5 kui-siok8 Goa2 e5 Goa7-pang-lang5, Long2 e7 lai5 chhoe7 Chu2.  18) Chiah-e5 oe7 si7 chu7 thai3-kou2 i2-lai5 hian2-beng5 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 e5 Chu2 kong2 e5.몭몯
	19) Nga2-kok ke3-siok8 kong2: 몮Chiau3 goa2 e5 i3-kian3, lan2 m7-thang ui5-lan5 hiah-e5 kui-hiong3 Siong7-chu2 e5 Goa7-pang-lang5.  20) Tan7-si7 tioh8 sia2-phe kio3 in m7-thang chiah8 u7 pai3-koe3 ngou2-siong7 bo5 chheng-khi3 e5 chiah8-mih8; siam2-pi7 hoan7 sia5-im5; m7-thang chiah8 teN7-si2 e5 cheng-seN a2-si7 hoeh.  21) In-ui7 chu7 kou2-cha2, chai7 kok siaN5-chhi7, to7(NNtoh8) u7 lang5 thoan5-kang2 Mou5-se e5 Lut8-hoat, mui2 An-hioh-jit8 chai7 hoe7-tng5 u7 teh thak8.몯

Sia2 hou7 Goa7-pang-lang5 e5 sin3-tou5 e5 phe:
	22) An2-ne hiah-e5 Su3-tou5 kap tiuN2-lo2 i2-kip8 choan5 kau3-hoe7, chiu7 koat-teng7 boeh tui3 in e5 tiong-kan soan2 kui2-e5-a2 lang5, chhe-phai3 in kap Po2-lo5, Pa-na2-pa cho3-hoe2 khi3 An-the5-o. In chiu7 soan2 chheng-hou cho3 Pa-sat-pa e5 Iu5-tai7 kap Se-lah, chit nng7 e5 lang5 chai7 hiaN-ti7 tiong si7 tiong7-iau3 e5 jin5-but8,  23) kau-tai3 in theh8 phe khi3, sia2 kong2: 
	몮Lin2 e5 hiaN-ti7, goan2 chiah-e5 Su3-tou5 kap cho3 tiuN2-lo2 e5, sia2-phe ka7 toa3 ti7 An-the5-o, Su7-li7-a, Ki-li7-ka e5 Goa7-pang e5 cheng3 hiaN-ti7 chheng2-an.  24) Goan2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 u7 chit8-koa2 goan2 chit tin7 e5 lang5, khi3 lin2 hia kong2-oe7 ka7 lin2 ui5-lan5, jiau2-loan7 lin2 e5 sim; ki5-sit8 goan2 peng7 bo5 chi2-si7 in an2-ne cho3.  25) Sou2-i2 goan2 chiah chu7-chip8 cho3-hoe2, tai7-ke tong5-i3 lai5 soan2-chhut kui2-e5-a2 lang5, boeh chhe-phai3 in kap goan2 chhin-ai3 e5 peng5-iu2 Pa-na2-pa kap Po2-lo5 khi3 lin2 hia.  26) Chit nng7 ui7 koe3-khi3 ui7 su7-hong7 lan2 e5 Chu2 Ia5-sou Ki-tok, bo5 sioh-tioh8 in e5 seN3-mia7.  27) TaN goan2 chhe-phai3 Iu5-tai7 kap Se-lah khi3, in ia7 e7 chhin-sin ka7 lin2 kong2 goan2 sou2 sia2 e5 tai7-chi3.  28) In-ui7 Seng3 Leng5 kap goan2 koat-teng7 ti5-liau2 chiah-e5 iau3-kin2 su7-hang7 i2-goa7; bo5 ai3 koh hou7 lin2 hu7-tam sim2-mih tang7-taN3:  29) chiu7-si7 m7-thang chiah8 u7 pai3-koe3 ngou2-siong7 e5 mih8; m7-thang chiah8 hoeh; m7-thang chiah8 teN7-si2 e5 cheng-seN; tioh8 siam2-pi7 sia5-im5. Chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 lin2 na7 long2 siam2-pi7, an2-ne chiu7 ho2. Goan7 lin2 peng5-an.몯
	30) In hong7-phai3 chiu7 loh8-khi3 An-the5-o, toa3 hia chu7-chip8 hoe7-chiong3, chiong hit tiuN phe kau hou7 in.  31) Cheng3-lang5 thak8 liau2-au7, siu7-tioh8 kou2-le7 chiu7 chin hoaN-hi2.  32) Iu5-tai7 kap Se-lah pun2-sin ia7 si7 tai7-gian5-jin5, chiu7 eng7 chin-che7 oe7 kou2-le7 hiaN-ti7, kian-kiong5 in e5 sim.  33) In nng7 lang5 toa3 hia u7 chit8-cham8-a2, hiaN-ti7 chiu7 peng5-peng5-an-an sang3 in tng2-khi3 chhe-phai3 in lai5 e5 lang5 hia.  34) (Tan7-si7 Se-lah koat-i3 boeh koh lau5 toa3 hia.)
	35) Po2-lo5 kap Pa-na2-pa ke3-siok8 toa3 An-the5-o, kap leng7-goa7 chin-che7 lang5 cho3-hoe2 ka3-si7 lang5, thoan5 Chu2 e5 chin-to7.

Po2-lo5 kap Pa-na2-pa hun-khui:
	36) Koe3 kui2-na7-jit8, Po2-lo5 ka7 Pa-na2-pa kong2, 몮Lan2 koh lai5-khi3 khah-cha2 thoan5 Chu2 e5 chin-to7 e5 kok siaN5-chhi7 hong2-bun7 hiah-e5 hiaN-ti7, khoaN3 in an3-choaN2 teh seng-oah8.몯  37) Pa-na2-pa ai3 boeh chhoa7 seN3 Ma2-kho2 e5 Iok-han7 kap in cho3-hoe2 khi3,  38) tan7-si7 Po2-lo5 siuN7 kong2 chhoa7 i khi3 bo5 hap8-sek, in-ui7 Ma2-kho2 khah-cha2 ti7 Pong5-hui-li7-a li7-khui in, m7-kheng2 kap in cho3-hoe2 khi3 kang-chok kau3 lou7-boe2.  39) An2-ne in nng7 e5 chiu7 hoat-seng kek-liat8 e5 cheng-lun7, soah hou7-siong hun-khui khi3. Pa-na2-pa chiu7 chhoa7 Ma2-kho2 cho3-hoe2 che7-chun5 khi3 Ku-pi2-lou7.  40) Po2-lo5 boeh chhut-hoat e5 si5 soan2 Se-lah, kap i cho3-hoe2 khi3, hiaN-ti7 ki5-kiu5 Siong7-chu2 siuN2-su3 in-hui7 ka7 in chiau3-kou3.  41) I chiu7 kiaN5 thau3 Su7-li7-a kap Ki-li7-ka, kian-kou3 hiah-e5 kau3-hoe7.

Te7 16 ChiuN

The5-mou5-thai3 toe3 Po2-lo5 kap Se-lah khi3 thoan5-kau3:
	1) Po2-lo5 khi3-kau3 Tek8-pi3 kap Lou7-su7-tek. U7 chit8 e5 bun5-tou5 kio3-cho3 The5-mou5-thai3 toa3 ti7 hia; i e5 lau7-bo2 si7 Iu5-thai3-lang5, ia7-si7 sin3-tou5, tan7-si7 i e5 lau7-pe7 si7 Hi-lah8-lang5.  2) I chai7 Lou7-su7-tek kap I2-ko-liam7 e5 hiaN-ti7-tiong, chin u7 seng-bong7.  3) Po2-lo5 ai3 boeh chhoa7 The5-mou5-thai3 kap i khi3, chiu7 ka7 i si-heng5 kat-le2. Che si7 in-ui7 toa3 ti7 hit te7-hng e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5, long2 chai-iaN2 The5-mou5-thai3 e5 lau7-pe7 si7 Hi-lah8-lang5.  4) In keng-koe3 kok siaN5-chhi7 e5 si5, chiong Su3-tou5 kap tiuN2-lo2 chai7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 sou2 gi7-koat e5 su7-hang7, kau hou7 sin3-tou5 chun-siu2.  5) Kiat-ko2 kok kau3-hoe7 chai7 sin3-giong2-siong7 lu2 kian-kiong5, jin5-sou3 ia7 jit8-jit8 cheng-ka.

Po2-lo5 chai7 Tek7-lo5-a khoaN3-kiN3 i7-siong7:
	6) In-ui7 Seng3 Leng5 kim3-chi2 in chai7 A-se-a Seng2 kong2 to7-li2, in chiu7 tui3 Hut-lu7-ka kap Ka-liap8-thai3 te7-hng keng-koe3.  7) In lai5-khi3 Pi2-chhui-ni5 Seng2; tan7-si7 Ia5-sou e5 Leng5 m7 in2-chun2 in.  8) an2-ne in chiu7 keng-koe3 Mui2-se-a, loh8-khi3 kau3 Tek8-lo5-a.  9) Po2-lo5 hit am3 khoaN3-kiN3 i7-siong7, khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 e5 Ma2-ki5-tun3-lang5 khia7 teh kiu5 i kong2, 몮ChhiaN2 koe3-lai5 Ma2-ki5-tun3 pang-chou7 goan2!몯  10) Po2-lo5 chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit e5 i7-siong7, goan2 chiu7 sui5-si5 siuN7-boeh chhut-hoat khi3 Ma2-ki5-tun3, in-ui7 goan2 khak-sin3 si7 Siong7-chu2 tiau3 goan2 khi3 thoan5 Hok-im hou7 hia e5 lang5 thiaN.

Lu7-ti2-a kui Chu2:
	11) Goan2 tui3 Tek8-lo5-a che7-chun5 tit8-tit8 koe3-khi3 Sat-mou5-tek8-lat, keh-tng2 jit8 ti7 Ni5-a-pho-li7 loh8-chun5.  12) Tui3 hia koh khi3-kau3 Hui-lip8-pi2, chiu7-si7 Ma2-ki5-tun3 te7-hng e5 tiong7-iau3 siaN5-chhi7; ia7-si7 Lo5-ma2 sit8-bin5-te7. Goan2 chiu7 toa3 hit e5 siaN5-chhi7 toa3 kui2-na7 jit8.  13) An-hioh-jit8, goan2 chhut-khi3 chhi7-goa7, khi3-kau3 ho5-piN, goan2 siuN7-kong2 ti7 hia it-teng7 u7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 teh ki5-to2 e5 sou2-chai7. Goan2 chiu7 che7 loh8-khi3, tui3 chu7-chip8 ti7 hia e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 kong2 to7-li2.  14) ThiaN goan2 kong2 to7-li2 e5, u7 chit8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 kio3-cho3 Lu7-ti2-a. I si7 Chhui-nga2-chhui-lat-lang5, teh be7 chi2-sek e5 pou3-phit. I si7 chit8 e5 keng3-pai3 Siong7-chu2 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5. Chu2 khui i e5 sim, hou7 i chu3-sin5 thiaN Po2-lo5 sou2 teh kong2 e5 oe7.  15) I kap i chit8 ke e5 lang5 siu7 se2-le2 liau2-au7, i chiu7 chhiaN2 goan2, kong2: 몮Lin2 na7 jim7-teng7 kong2 goa2 sit8-chai7 si7 sin3 Chu2 e5, chhiaN2 lin2 lai5-khi3 toa3 goan2 chhu3.몯 I chiu7 kiong5-kiong5 chhiaN2 goan2 khi3.

Chai7 Hui-lip8-pi2 che7-kaN:
	16) U7 chit8 jit8, goan2 boeh khi3 hit e5 ki5-to2 e5 sou2-chai7 e5 si5, tu2-tioh8 chit8 e5 hou7 pok-koa3 e5 sin5 hu7-sin e5 cha-bou2 lou5-le7. I ka7 lang5 siong3-mia7, the3 i hiah-e5 chu2-lang5 than3 chin-che7 chiN5.  17) I toe3 Po2-lo5 kap goan2 lai5, hoah kong2, 몮Chiah-e5 lang5 si7 chi3-ko Siong7-chu2 e5 lou5-pok8! In tui3 lin2 soan-pou3 chin2-kiu3 e5 to7-lou7!몯  18) I an2-ne hoah chin-che7 jit8, hoah kah Po2-lo5 chin tho2-ia3, chiu7 oat8 koe3-lai5 ka7 hit e5 sia5-sin5 kong2, 몮Goa2 hong7 Ia5-sou Ki-tok e5 mia5, beng7-leng7 li2 tui3 chit e5 cha-bou2-lang5 chhut-lai5!몯 Hit e5 sia5-sin5 chek-si5 chiu7 tui3 i chhut-lai5.  19) Tan7-si7 hiah-e5 chu2-lang5, chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 in than3-chiN5 e5 hi-bong7 i2-keng bo5-khi3 a3, chiu7 liah8 Po2-lo5 kap Se-lah, thoa in khi3 chhi7-tiong-sim e5 kong2-tiuN5 kiN3 koaN-oan5.  20) Toa3 Lo5-ma2 e5 koaN-tiuN2 bin7-cheng5 khong3-ko3 kong2: 몮Chiah-el5ang si7 Iu5-thai3-lang5, lai5 teh jiau2-loan7 lan2 e5 siaN5-chhi7.  21) In tui3 lan2 Lo5-ma2-lang5 soan-thoan5 sou2 m7 eng-kai chiap-siu7, m7 eng-kai sit8-heng5 e5 koan3-le7.몯  22) Kun5-chiong3 ia7 cho3-hoe2 lai5 kong-kek in; koaN-tiuN2 pak Po2-lo5 kap Se-lah e5 saN khi2-lai5, beng7-leng7 eng7 kun3-na2 ka7 in phah.  23) In hou7 lang5 phah kah chin li7-hai7 liau2-au7, chiu7 hou7 lang5 koaiN-loh8 kaN-gak8; koaN-tiuN2 beng7-leng7 kou3-kaN-e5 giam5-bit8 ka7 in khan3-siu2.  24) Kou3-kaN-e5 chiap-tioh8 chit e5 beng7-leng7, chiu7 ka7 in koaiN jip8-khi3 lai7-kaN, chiong in e5 siang-kha ka7 in pak8 toa3 chha5-kong5.
	25) Chha-put-to poaN3-me5, Po2-lo5 kap Se-lah ki5-to2 gim5-si teh chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2; ki5-tha e5 hoan7-lang5 long2 chu3-i3 teh thiaN.  26) Hut-jian5-kan hoat-seng toa7 te7-tang7, lian5 kaN-gak8 e5 te7-ki ia7 khi2 tong7-iau5; kaN-gak8 e5 mng5 chek-si5 long2 khui-khi3, hoan7-lang5 e5 kha-khau3 ia7 long2 lak-khi3.  27) Kou3-kaN-e5 chheN2 khi2-lai5, chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 kaN-gak8 e5 mng5 long2 khui-khui, siuN7-cho3 siu5-hoan7 long2 to5-chau2 khi3 a3, chiu7 poeh8 kiam3 khi2-lai5, siuN7-boeh chu7-sat.  28) Tan7-si7 Po2-lo5 toa7-siaN hoah kong2, 몮M7-thang siong-hai7 li2 ka-ti7! goan2 long2 ti7 chia.몯  29) Kou3-kaN-e5 kio3 lang5 giah8 hoe2 lai5, chong5 jip8-khi3 phih8-phih8-chhoah, phak loh8-khi3 Po2-lo5 kap Se-lah e5 bin7-cheng5.  30) Jian5-au7 chhoa7 in chhut-lai5, kong2, 몮Sin-seN a3, goa2 tioh8 an3-choaN2 cho3 chiah e7 tit-tioh8 kiu3?몯  31) In kong2, 몮Tioh8 sin3 Chu2 Ia5-sou, li2 kap li2 choan5-ke e5 lang5 chiu7 e7 tit-tioh8 kiu3.몯  32) In chiu7 chiong Chu2 e5 to7-li2, kong2 hou7 i kap i choan5-ke e5 lang5 thiaN.  33) Hit e5 si5 sui-jian5 hiah-nih8 am3 a3, kou3-kaN-e5 ia7 chhoa7 in khi3 ka7 in se2 khang-chhui3; i kap choan5-ke e5 lang5 long2 chek-si5 siu7 se2-le2.  34) I chiu7 chhoa7 Po2-lo5 kap Se-lah jip8-khi3 i e5 chhu3, pi7-pan7 hou7 in chiah8. I kap choan5-ke e5 lang5, in-ui7 in sin3 Siong7-chu2 a3, long2 chhiong-moa2 hi2-lok8.
	35) Keh-tng2 chai2-khi2, Lo5-ma2 e5 koaN-tiuN2 chhe-phai3 keng2-koaN lai5 kong2, 몮Pang3 hit nng7 e5 lang5 chhut-khi3.몯  36) Kou3-kaN-e5 chiu7 ka7 Po2-lo5 kong2: 몮KoaN-tiuN2 chhe-phai3 lang5 lai5 kong2 tioh8 pang3 lin2 chhut-khi3; taN lin2 thang chhut-khi3, an-sim tng2-khi3.몯  37) Tan7-si7 Po2-lo5 ka7 in kong2: 몮Goan2 si7 Lo5-ma2 e5 kong-bin5. In bo5 ka7 goan2 sim2-phoaN3 chiu7 chai7 cheng3-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 ka7 goan2 phah, iu7-koh ka7 goan2 koaiN-loh8 kaN-gak8; taN in boeh tiam7-tiam7-a2 ka7 goan2 koaN2 chhut-khi3 si7 bo5? An2-ne be7-eng7-tit! Kio3 Lo5-ma2 e5 koaN-tiuN2 chhin-sin lai5 chhoa7 goan2 chhut-khi3.몯  38) Keng2-koaN chiong chiah-e5 oe7 khi3 ka7 Lo5-ma2 e5 koaN-tiuN2 po3-ko3; koaN-tiuN2 thiaN-kiN3 Po2-lo5 kap Se-lah si7 Lo5-ma2 e5 kong-bin5, chiu7 khi2 kiaN-hiaN5.  39) Sou2-i2 in chiu7 lai5 ka7 Po2-lo5 kap Se-lah to7-khiam2; chhoa7 in chhut-lai5, chhiaN2 in li7-khui hit e5 siaN5-chhi7.  40) In chhut kaN, chiu7 khi3 Lu7-ti2-a e5 chhu3, kiN3 in e5 hiaN-ti7, ka7 in kou2-le7 liau2-au7 chiu7 koh chhut-hoat.

Te7 17 ChiuN

Chai7 Thiap-sat-lo5-ni5-ka:
	Po2-lo5 kap Se-lah keng-koe3 Am3-hui-pho-li2 i2-kip8 A-pho-lo5-ni5-a, lai5-kau3 Thiap-sat-lo5-ni5-ka. Ti7 hia u7 chit8 keng Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 hoe7-tng5.  2) Po2-lo5 chiau3 i peng5-siong5 e5 sip8-koan3 jip8-khi3 hoe7-tng5. I ti7 hia lian5-soa3 saN e5 An-hioh-jit8, in2-iong7 Seng3-keng kap in pian7-lun7.  3) I kai2-sek Seng3-keng, in2-iong7 keng-chat lai5 cheng3-beng5 kong2 Bi2-sai3-a it-teng7 tioh8 siu7 khou2-lan7, ia7 e7 tui3 si2-lang5 tiong koh-oah8 khi2-lai5. Po2-lo5 koh kong2, 몮Goa2 sou2 thoan5 hou7 lin2 chit ui7 Ia5-sou chiu7-si7 Hit-ui7 Bi2-sai3-a.몯  4) In e5 tiong-kan u7 chit8-koa2 lang5 siong-sin3, chiu7 lai5 tui-sui5 Po2-lo5 kap Se-lah; ki5-tiong ia7 u7 chit8 toa7 tin7 keng3-khian5 e5 Hi-lah8-lang5 i2-kip8 chin-che7 chun kui3 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5.
	5) Tan7-si7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 khi2 chit-tou3, chio chit8-koa2 put-hoat e5 liu5-bang5, seng5-kun5 kiat-tong2, jiau2-loan7 siaN5-chhi7, kong-kek Ia5-sun e5 chhu3, siuN7 boeh chhoe7 Po2-lo5 kap Se-lah, liah8 in chhut-lai5 kau hou7 kun5-chiong3.  6) Tan7-si7 chit8-e7 chhoe7 in bo5, chiu7 chiong Ia5-sun kap i2-goa7 kui2-a7(**na7) e5 hiaN-ti7, thoa lai5 siaN5-chhi7 e5 koaN-oan5 hia, hoah kong2: 몮Chiah-e5 jiau2-loan7 thian-ha7 e5 lang5, ia7 lai5-kau3 lan2 e5 siaN5-chhi7 a7.  7) Ia5-sun chiau-thai7 in khi3 toa3 in hia. Chiah-e5 lang5 long2 ui5-poe7 hong5-te3 Kai-sat e5 hoat-leng7, soan-gian5 kong2 leng7-goa7 iau2 u7 chit8 e5 ong5, kio3-cho3 Ia5-sou.몯  8) Kun5-chiong3 kap siaN5-chhi7 e5 koaN-oan5 thiaN-kiN3 chiah-e5 oe7 chiu7 khi2 khiong2-hong5.  9) Chiah-e5 koaN-oan5 hou7 Ia5-sun kap i2-goa7 e5 lang5 eng7 chiN5 kau-po2, chiu7 pang3 in khi3.

Chai7 Pi3-li2-a:
	10) Jit8-thau5 chit8-e7 am3, hiaN-ti7 chiu7 chek-si5 hou7 Po2-lo5 kap Se-lah chhut-hoat khi3 Pi3-li2-a. In kau3 hia chiu7 jip8-khi3 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 hoe7-tng5.  11) Chit te7-hng e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5 pi2 Thiap-sat-lo5-ni5-ka e5 lang5 khah khai-beng5. In chin jiat8-sim thiaN to7-li2, tak8-jit8 gian2-kiu3 Seng3-keng, khoaN3 Po2-lo5 kong2 e5 u7 su7-sit8 a2 bo5.  12) Sou2-i2 in e5 tiong-kan u7 chin-che7 lang5 sin3; ia7 u7 chin-che7 Hi-lah8 chun-kui3 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 lai5 sin3, cha-pou-lang5 ia7 be7 chio2.  13) Tan7-si7 Thiap-sat-lo5-ni5-ka e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5, chit8-e7 chai-iaN2 Po2-lo5 ia7 ti7 Pi3-li2-a thoan5 Siong7-chu2 e5 to7-li2, in chiu7 toe3 khi3-kau3 hia, khai-si2 sian3-tong7 kun5-chiong3, in2-khi2 jiau2-loan7.  14) HiaN-ti7 chiu7 chek-si5 sang3 Po2-lo5 khi3 hai2-piN; tan7-si7 Se-lah kap The5-mou5-thai3 iau2 toa3 Pi3-li2-a.  15) Hou7-sang3 Po2-lo5 e5 lang5 chhoa7 i khi3-kau3 Nga2-tian2. Po2-lo5 hoan-hu3 in kio3 Se-lah kap The5-mou5-thai3 chin7-liong7 koaN2-kin2 lai5 kap i hoe7-hap8, hiah-e5 lang5 chiu7 tng2-khi3 Pi3-li2-a.

Chai7 Nga2-tian2:
	16) Po2-lo5 ti7 Nga2-tian2 teh theng3-hau7 Se-lah kap The5-mou5-thai3 e5 tiong-kan, i khoaN3-kiN3 moa2-chhi7 long2 si7 ngou2-siong7, sim-lai7 chin hun3-khai3.  17) An2-ne i chiu7 chai7 hoe7-tng5-lai7 kap Iu5-thai3-lang5 i2-kip8 keng3-ui3 Siong7-chu2 e5 Goa7-pang-lang5 pian7-lun7 to7-li2, ia7 tak8-jit8 toa3 chhi7-tiong-sim e5 kong2-tiuN5 kap i sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 lang5 tho2-lun7.  18) Ia7 u7 chit8-koa2 I2-pi2-kou2-lo5 i2-kip8 Su7-to-a hak8-phai3 e5 tiat-hak8-ka ia7 kap i cheng-lun7. U7-e5 kong2, 몮Chit e5 kau7-oe7-e5 si7 siuN7-boeh kong2 sim2-mih?몯 U7-e5 kong2, 몮I chhin-chhiuN7 teh thoan5 goa7-kok e5 kui2-sin5.몯 In an2-ne kong2 si7 in-ui7 Po2-lo5 thoan5 koan-he7 Ia5-sou kap hok8-hoat8 e5 hok-im.  19) In chiu7 chhoa7 Po2-lo5 khi3-kau3 A-liok8-soaN e5 hoe7-tiuN5, tui3 i kong2: 몮Li2 sou2 thoan5 chit e5 sin e5 kau3 si7 sim2-mih khoan2 e5, goan2 e7-tang3 chai-iaN2 be7?  20) In-ui7 li2 sou2 kong2 e5, u7 chit8-koa2 tai7-chi3 goan2 thiaN-liau2 chin ki5-koai3, goan2 chin ai3 chai-iaN2 si7 sim2-mih i3-su3.몯  21) (In-ui7 Nga2-tian2-lang5 kap toa3 ti7 hia e5 goa7-kok-lang5, long2 ai3 kong2, ia7 ai3 thiaN sin5-ki5 e5 tai7-chi3 lai5 teh tou7 jit8-chi2.)
	22) Po2-lo5 khia7 toa3 A-liok8-soaN hoe7-tiuN5 e5 tiong-ng, kong2: 몮Kok-ui7 Nga2-tian2-lang5 a3! Goa2 khoaN3 lin2 chai7 kok hong-bin7 chin u7 keng3-ui3 sin5 e5 sim.  23) In-ui7 goa2 tui3 lin2 e5 siaN5-chhi7 keng-koe3 e5 si5, u7 khoaN3-kiN3 lin2 sou2 teh keng3-pai3 e5 sou2-chai7, goa2 ia7 u7 hoat-kian3 tioh8 chit8 cho7 che3-toaN5, teng2-bin7 sia2 kong2, 몬Hian3 hou7 m7-bat e5 sin5.몭 Sui-jian5 lin2 m7-bat ia7 lai5 teh keng3-pai3 e5 si7 sim2-mih sin5, goa2 hian7-chai7 boeh kong2 hou7 lin2 chai-iaN2.  24) Chhong3-cho7 u2-tiu7 kap ki5-tiong ban7-but8 e5 Siong7-chu2, ki3-jian5 si7 thiN-te7 e5 Chu2-chaiN2, chiu7 bo5 toa3 lang5 kian3-cho7 e5 sin5-tian7;  25) I ia7 bo5 khiam3-eng7 lang5 eng7 in e5 chhiu2 ui7 I sou2 cho3 e5 mih8-kiaN7. I pun2-sin tian-to3 chiong seN3-mia7, hou-khip i2-kip8 ban7-but8 siuN2-su3 hou7 ban7-bin5.  26) I tui3 chit8 e5 lang5 chhong3-cho7 kok chiong2-chok8 e5 lang5, hou7 in toa3 ti7 choan5 se3-kai3. I i7-sian ka7 in koat-teng7 heng-bong5 e5 ki5-han7 kap ki-chu7 e5 kai3-han7.  27) Siong7-chu2 an2-ne cho3 si7 boeh hou7 in lai5 chhoe7-kiu5 I, ng3-bang7 in chai7 am3-tiong bong-so lai5 chhoe7-tioh8 I. Ki5-sit8 Siong7-chu2 li7 lan2 mui2 chit8 e5 lang5 bo5 loa7 hng7;  28) in-ui7
몬Lan2 kap I kiat-hap8 lai5 teh seng-chun5, lai5 teh heng5-tong7, lai5 teh chun5-chai7.몭
Chhin-chhiuN7 lin2 e5 si-jin5 ia7 u7 lang5 kong2,
몬Lan2 ia7 si7 I e5 kiaN2-sun.몭
29) Lan2 ki3-jian5 si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 kiaN2-sun, chiu7 m7-thang siuN7-cho3 Siong7-chu2 e5 pun2-seng3 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 eng7 lang5 e5 chhiu2-ge7 kap chiau3 lang5 e5 khong-siong2 sou2 tiau-khek e5 kim, gin5 a2-si7 chioh8 e5 siong7.  30) Se3-kan-lang5 iau2 bo5 ti3-sek e5 si5-tai7, Siong7-chu2 bo5 tui-kiu3, tan7-si7 hian7-chai7 I beng7-leng7 tak8 sou2-chai7 e5 lang5 long2 tioh8 hoe2-kai2 in e5 choe7-ko3.  31) In-ui7 I i2-keng koat-teng7 chit8 e5 jit8-chi2, boeh eng7 I i2-keng soan2-teng7 e5 lang5 eng7 kong-gi7 lai5 sim2-phoaN3 choan5 se3-kai3. I i2-keng hou7 Hit-ui7 tui3 si2-lang5-tiong koh-oah8 khi2-lai5, lai5 hou7 ban7-bin5 cho3 sin3-kho3 e5 pin5-ki3.몯
	32) In chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 Po2-lo5 kong2 si2-lang5 hok8-hoat8 e5 tai7-chi3, u7-e5 ka7 i thi2-chhio3, tan7-si7 u7-e5 kong2, 몮Goan2 na7 u7 ki-hoe7, ai3-boeh koh thiaN li2 kong2 chit e5 tai7-chi3.몯  33) Po2-lo5 chiu7 li7-khui in.  34) Tan7-si7 u7 kui2-na7 e5 lang5 sui5-chiong5 i, lai5 cho3 sin3-tou5, ki5-tiong u7 A-liok8-soaN hoe7-tiuN5 e5 koaN-oan5 Tiu-ni5-siu, kap chit8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, mia5 kio3-cho3 Tai7-ma2-li2, i2-goa7 iau2 u7 kui2-na7 e5 lang5.

Te7 18 ChiuN

Chai7 Ko-lim5-to:
	1) Jian5-au7 Po2-lo5 li7-khui Nga2-tian2 khi3-kau3 Ko-lim5-to.  2) Ti7 hia tu2-tioh8 chit8 e5 ti7 Pun2-tou chhut-si3 e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5, mia5 kio3-cho3 A-ku-lah. I kap in thai3-thai3 Pek-ki-lah tui3 I3-tai7-li7 lai5 bo5 loa7 ku2, in-ui7 hong5-te3 Kek-lo2-tiu beng7-leng7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 long2 tioh8 li7-khui Lo5-ma2. Po2-lo5 chiu7 khi3 chhoe7 in.  3) In e5 chit-giap8 si7 teh cho3 pou3-phang5, in-ui7 Po2-lo5 kap in si7 tong5-giap8, i chiu7 kap in cho3-hoe2 toa3, cho3-hoe2 kang-chok.  4) Tak8 An-hioh-jit8, Po2-lo5 toa3 hoe7-tng5 pian7-lun7, siuN7-boeh soat-hok8 Iu5-thai3-lang5 kap Hi-lah8-lang5.
	5) Se-lah kap The5-mou5-thai3 tui3 Ma2-ki5-tun3 lai5 liau2-au7, Po2-lo5 chiu7 choan-sim thoan5-kau3, tui3 Iu5-thai3-lang5 cheng3-beng5 Ia5-sou chiu7-si7 Hit-ui7 Bi2-sai3-a.  6) In ka7 i hoan2-tui3, ka7 i bu2-jiok8 e5 si5, Po2-lo5 chiu7 poaN7 i e5 saN e5 thou5-hun2 khong3-gi7, tui3 in kong2: 몮Lin2 na7 biat8-bong5, lin2 ka-ti7 tioh8-ai3 hu7-chek! Bo5 goa2 e5 chek-jim7. Tui3 chim2-ma2 khi2, goa2 boeh khi3 Goa7-pang-lang5 hia.몯  7) I chiu7 li7-khui in, khi3 toa3 chit8 e5 Goa7-pang-lang5 mia5 kio3-cho3 The5-to Iu5-su7-to e5 lang5 in chhu3. I si7 keng3-pai3 Siong7-chu2 e5 lang5; i e5 chhu3 ti7 hoe7-tng5 e5 keh-piah.  8) Hoe7-tng5-tiuN2 Kek-li7-su7-pou3 kap i choan5-ke e5 lang5 long2 sin3 Chu2, ia7 u7 chin-che7 Ko-lim5-to-lang5 thiaN-tioh8 Po2-lo5 e5 to7-li2 chiu7 sin3, siu7 se2-le2.
	9) U7 chit8 am3 chai7 i7-siong7-tiong, Chu2 tui3 Po2-lo5 kong2: 몮M7-thang kiaN, tioh8 ke3-siok8 kong2, m7-thang tiam7-khi3,  10) in-ui7 Goa2 kap li2 tong5-chai7. Bo5 lang5 kaN2 siong-hai7 li2, in-ui7 ti7 chit e5 siaN5-chhi7 u7 chin-che7 Goa2 e5 chu2-bin5.몯  11) Po2-lo5 chiu7 toa3 hia toa3 ni5-poaN3, tui3 hiah-e5 lang5 ka3-si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 chin-to7.
	12) Ka-liu5 cho3 A-kai-a chong2-tok e5 si5, Iu5-thai3-lang5 lian5-hap8 lai5 kong-kek Po2-lo5, liah8 i khi3 sim2-phoaN3-teng5.  13) In kong2, 몮Chit e5 lang5 khoan3-iu2 lang5 ui5-poe7 lut8-hoat lai5 keng3-pai3 Siong7-chu2.몯  14) Po2-lo5 tu2 boeh khui-chhui3 e5 si5, Ka-liu5 chiu7 tui3 Iu5-thai3-lang5 kong2: 몮Iu5-thai3-lang5 a3, i sou2 cho3 e5 tai7-chi3 na7-si7 u7 sim2-mih put-cheng3 a2-si7 put-hoat, goa2 tong-jian5 tioh8 jim2-nai7 lai5 thiaN lin2 e5 khong3-sou3.  15) Tan7-si7 kah-si7 ui7-tioh8 gian5-gi2, beng5-chheng i2-kip8 lin2 ka-ti7 e5 lut8-hoat e5 bun7-te5 e5 pian7-lun7, lin2 tioh8 ka-ti7 khi3 kai2-koat. Goa2 bo5 boeh sim2-phoaN3 chit khoan2 tai7-chi3!몯  16) I chiu7 ka7 in koaN2-chhut sim2-phoaN3-teng5.  17) Cheng3-lang5 chiu7 liah8 hoe7-tng5-tiuN2 Sou2-the5-ni5, toa3 sim2-phoaN3-teng5 cheng5 ka7 i phah. Tan7-si7 tui3 chit hang7 tai7-chi3 Ka-liu5 long2 bo5 khi3 chhap i.

Po2-lo5 tng2-lai5 An-the5-o:
	18) Po2-lo5 kap hiaN-ti7 toa3 Ko-lim5-to chin-che7 jit8, kap hiaN-ti7 li7-piat8 chiu7 kap Pek-ki-lah i2-kip8 A-ku-lah cho3-hoe2 che7-chun5 khi3 Su7-li7-a. In-ui7 i he7-goan7 e5 ki5 i2-keng moa2 a3, chiu7 toa3 Kian-kek-li2 chian2 thau5-mng5.  19) In lai5-kau3 I2-hut-sou2, Po2-lo5 chiu7 chiong Pek-ki-lah kap A-ku-lah pang3-le3; ka-ti7 jip8-khi3 hoe7-tng5, kap Iu5-thai3-lang5 pian7-lun7.  20) In lau5 i kap in toa3 khah ku2 le3, m7-ku2 i ka7 in sia7-choat8,  21) tan7-si7 boeh si5-piat8 e5 si5 ka7 in kong2, 몮Siong7-chu2 na7 goan7-i3, goa2 e7 koh tng2-lai5 lin2 chia.몯 I chiu7 che7-chun5 li7-khui I2-hut-sou2.
	22) Toa3 Kai-sat-li7-a loh8-chun5, chiu7 chiuN7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 ka7 kau3-hoe7 chheng2-an, jian5-au7 chiah loh8-khi3 An-the5-o.  23) Toa3 hia toa3 u7 chit8 toaN7 si5-kan, i koh li7-khui hia, keng-koe3 Ka-liap8-thai3 kap Hut-lu7-ka te7-khu e5 kok te7-hng, kou2-le7 chiong3 bun5-tou5.

A-pho-lo5 chai7 I2-hut-sou2 kap Ko-lim5-to:
	24) U7 chit8 e5 ti7 A-lek8-san-thai3 chhut-si3 e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5, mia5 kio3-cho3 A-pho-lo5, lai5-kau3 I2-hut-sou2. I chin u7 khau2-chai5, ia7 chin cheng-thong Seng3-keng.  25) I i2-keng hak8-sip8 Chu2 e5 To7, chin jiat8-sim chiong koan-he7 Ia5-sou e5 tai7-chi3 cheng3-khak kang2-kai2 ka3-si7 lang5. Sui-jian5 si7 an2-ne, i chi2-u7 chai-iaN2 Iok-han7 e5 se2-le2 e5 tai7-chi3 nia7-nia7.  26) I chai7 hoe7-tng5-lai7 ho2-taN2 khai-si2 kang2-to7. Pek-ki-lah kap A-ku-lah chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3, chiu7 chhoa7 i khi3 in chhu3, koh-khah cheng3-khak ka7 i soat-beng5 Siong7-chu2 e5 To7.  27) A-pho-lo5 siuN7-boeh khi3 A-kai-a e5 si5, hiaN-ti7 chiu7 ka7 i kou2-le7, iu7-koh sia2 phe khi3 hou7 bun5-tou5, chhiaN2 in ka7 i chiap-thai7. I kau3 hia e5 si5, to-to pang-chou7 hiah-e5 oa2-kho3 Siong7-chu2 e5 in-hui7 lai5 cho3 sin3-tou5 e5.  28) In-ui7 i chai7 kong-chiong3 e5 bin7-cheng5, chin u7 leng5-lek8, pian7 iaN5 Iu5-thai3-lang5, in2-iong7 Seng3-keng lai5 cheng3-beng5 Ia5-sou chiu7-si7 Bi2-sai3-a.

Te7 19 ChiuN

Po2-lo5 chai7 I2-hut-sou2:
	1) A-pho-lo5 ti7 Ko-lim5-to e5 tiong-kan, Po2-lo5 keng-koe3 A-se-a Seng2 e5 pak-pou7 te7-hng, lai5-kau3 I2-hut-sou2. I ti7 hia tu2-tioh8 kui2-na7-e5 bun5-tou5,  2) mng7 in kong2, 몮Lin2 lai5 cho3 sin3-tou5 hit e5 si5, u7 nia2-siu7 Seng3 Leng5 bo5?몯 In in3-tap kong2, 몮Bo5, goan2 kin-pun2 m7-bat thiaN-kiN3 kong2 u7 Seng3 Leng5.몯  3) Po2-lo5 mng7 kong2, 몮An2-ne, lin2 nia2-siu7 sim2-mih khoan2 e5 se2-le2?몯 In in3-tap kong2, 몮Si7 Iok-han7 e5 se2-le2.몯  4) Po2-lo5 kong2: 몮Iok-han7 sou2 si-heng5 e5 si7 hoe2-kai2 e5 se2-le2, tan7-si7 ka7 I2-sek-liat8-lang5 kong2 tioh8 sin3 Hit-ui7 toe3 i au7-bin7 teh-boeh lai5 e5 Ia5-sou.몯  5) In thiaN-kiN3 an2-ne, chiu7 hong7 Chu2 Ia5-sou e5 mia5 siu7 se2-le2.  6) Po2-lo5 chit8-e7 ka7 in an3-chhiu2, Seng3 Leng5 chiu7 kang3-lim5 lai5 ti7 in lai7-bin7; in chiu7 jip8-sin5 kong2 chhut ki5-biau7 e5 oe7-gi2, ia7 the3 Siong7-chu2 kong2-oe7.  7) Hiah-e5 lang5 long2-chong2 tai7-iok u7 chap8-ji7 e5.
	8) Po2-lo5 jip8-khi3 hoe7-tng5, saN goeh8-jit8 ku2 ho2-taN2 thoan5-to7, chiong koan-he7 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok e5 tai7-chi3 kap in pian7-lun7, ia7 khoan3-bian2 in chiap-siu7.  9) Tan7-si7 u7 chit8-koa2 lang5 chin kou3-chip m7 sin3, chai7 cheng3-lang5 bin7-cheng5 hui2-pong3 Chu2 e5 To7. Po2-lo5 chiu7 li7-khui in, ia7 chhoa7 bun5-tou5 kap i cho3-hoe2 khi3; tak8-jit8 toa3 Chhui-lat8-lou5 e5 kang2-tng5 kap in tho2-lun7.  10) An2-ne ke3-siok8 u7 nng7 ni5 ku2, sou2-i2 toa3 ti7 A-se-a Seng2 e5 lang5, bo5-lun7 si7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 a2-si7 Hi-lah8-lang5, long2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 Chu2 e5 to7-li2.

Su7-ki-oa2 e5 kiaN2-ji5:
	11) Siong7-chu2 chioh Po2-lo5 e5 chhiu2 ke3-siok8 cho3 hui-siong5 hi-han2 e5 sin5-chek.  12) Sim7-chi3 Po2-lo5 u7 eng7-koe3 e5 chhiu2-kin a2-si7 ui5-su-kun5, na7 theh8-khi3 peN7-lang5 hia, in e5 peN7-cheng3 chiu7 ho2-khi3, sia5-sin5 chiu7 tui3 in chau2 chhut-khi3.  13) Hit e5 si5, u7 kui2-na7 e5 si3-ke3 iu5-lek8 liam7-chiu3 koaN2-kui2 e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5, tui3 hiah-e5 hou7 sia5-sin5 hu7-sin e5 lang5, loan7-iong7 Chu2 Ia5-sou e5 mia5 kong2, 몮Goa2 hong7 Po2-lo5 sou2 soan-iong5 e5 Ia5-sou, beng7-leng7 lin2 chhut-lai5.몯  14) Iu5-thai3 e5 che3-si-tiuN2 Su7-ki-oa2 e5 chhit e5 kiaN2 ia7 teh cho3 chit khoan2 tai7-chi3.  15) Tan7-si7 sia5-sin5 in3 in kong2, 몮Na7-si7 Ia5-sou, goa2 bat I, Po2-lo5 goa2 ia7 bat i(**I); tan7-si7 lin2 si7 sim2-mih lang5?몯  16) Hit e5 hou7 sia5-sin5 hu7-sin e5 lang5 chiu7 thiau3 lai5 ka7 in kong-kek, phah-iaN5 in, ka7 in che3-hok8, hou7 in siu7-siong, chhiah-sin lou7-the2, tui3 hit keng chhu3 chau2 chhut-khi3.  17) Toa3 ti7 I2-hut-sou2 e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5 kap Hi-lah8-lang5 chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 chit hang7 tai7-chi3; chiu7 long2 khi2 toa7 tioh8-kiaN, Chu2 Ia5-sou e5 mia5 ia7 chiu7 toa7-toa7 siu7 chun-tiong7.  18) U7 chin-che7 i2-keng sin3 e5 lang5 lai5, kong-khai jin7-choe7, thou3-lou7 chin-che7 bat li7-iong7 sia5-sut8 e5 lang5, theh8 in e5 chheh lai5 khng3 cho3-hoe2, toa3 cheng3-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 pang3-hoe2 sio. Hiah-e5 chheh e5 ke3-chiN5 in chong2-ke3 khi2-lai5, chiu7 chai-iaN2 ke3-tat8 gin5-oan5 gou7-ban7 khou.  20) An2-ne Chu2 e5 to7-li2 chiam7-chiam7 khong3-tian2, kian-kou3 khi2-lai5.

Chai7 I2-hut-sou2 hoat-seng po7-tong7:
	21) Chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 hoat-seng liau2-au7, Po2-lo5 chiu7 siu7 Seng3 Leng5 e5 chi2-si7, koat-sim boeh keng-koe3 Ma2-ki5-tun3 kap A-kai-a, ke3-siok8 khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2. I kong2, 몮Goa2 khi3 hia liau2-au7, ia7 tioh8 khi3 Lo5-ma2 khoaN3-khoaN3 le3.몯  22) I chiu7 tui3 i e5 chou7-chhiu2 e5 tiong-kan chhe-phai3 nng7 e5, chiu7-si7 The5-mou5-thai3 kap I2-lah-tou tai7-seng khi3 Ma2-ki5-tun3. I pun2-sin chiam7-si5 lau5 toa3 A-se-a Seng2.
	23) Tu2-tu2 hit e5 si5 koan-he7 Chu2 e5 To7, hoat-seng giam5-tiong7 e5 jiau2-loan7.  24) U7 chit8 e5 phah-gin5 sai-hu7, kio3-cho3 Ti2-bi2-tiu. I eng7 gin5 cho3 A-ti2-bi2 sin5-tian7 e5 bou5-heng5, hou7 i hiah-e5 sai-hu7 than3 be7 chio2 chiN5.  25) I chiu7 tiau3-chip8 hiah-e5 sai-hu7 kap i2-goa7 e5 tong5-giap8-chia2 lai5, ka7 in kong2: 몮Kok-ui7, lin2 chai-iaN2 lan2 si7 oa2-kho3 chit e5 seng-li2 lai5 teh than3-chiN5 e5.  26) Hian7-chai7 chit e5 Po2-lo5, put-tan7 chai7 I2-hut-sou2, ia7 chha-put-to chai7 choan5 A-se-a Seng2 in2-iu2 be5-hek8 chin-che7 lang5, kong2 eng7 lang5 e5 chhiu2 cho3 e5 m7-si7 sin5. Che si7 lin2 sou2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3, sou2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 e5.  27) An2-ne put-tan7 lan2 chit e5 su7-giap8 e7 tu2-tioh8 siu7 lang5 khoaN3-khin e5 gui5-hiam2, lian5 ui2-tai7 e5 li2-sin5 A-ti2-bi2 e5 bio7 ia7 e7 hou7 lang5 khoaN3 be7 khi2. Choan5 A-se-a Seng2 kap choan5 se3-kai3 sou2 teh keng3-pai3 chit e5 li2-sin5 e5 chun-giam5, ia7 e7 siau-biat8 khi3.몯
	28) ThiaN-kiN3 chiah-e5 oe7 e5 lang5 hui-siong5 siu7-khi3, chiu7 it-tit8 hoah kong2: 몮Ui2-tai7 a3! I2-hut-sou2-lang5 e5 A-ti2-bi2!몯  29) Choan5 siaN5-chhi7 long2 jiau2-loan7 khi2-lai5. Cheng3-lang5 chiong hit nng7 e5 kap Po2-lo5 tong5-heng5 e5 Ma2-ki5-tun3-lang5 Kai-iu5 kap A-li2-tat8-kou2 liah8 khi2-lai5, cho3 chit8-e7 chhih8 jip8-khi3 hi3-iN7 lai7.  30) Po2-lo5 siuN7-boeh chiN3 jip8-khi3 bin5-chiong3 e5 bin7-cheng5, tan7-si7 bun5-tou5 m7 hou7 i khi3.  31) U7 kui2-na7 ui7 A-se-a Seng2 e5 koaN-tiuN2, si7 Po2-lo5 e5 peng5-iu2, in ia7 chhe-phai3 lang5 lai5 khng3 i m7-thang mou7-hiam2 jip8-khi3 hi3-iN7.  32) Hit e5 si5 chu7-hoe7 e5 tiat8-su7 toa7 hun7-loan7, chit8 lang5 hoah chit8 khoan2, toa7 pou7-hun7 e5 lang5 m7-chai in si7 ui7-tioh8 sim2-mih bok8-tek lai5 chu7-chip8.  33) Kun5-chiong3 e5 tiong-kan u7 lang5 chiong chit e5 jiau2-loan7 e5 chek-jim7 the hou7 A-lek8-san-tai7, in-ui7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 ka7 i sak chhut-khi3 thau5-cheng5. A-lek8-san-tai7 chiu7 io5-chhiu2, siuN7-boeh toa3 bin5-chiong3 e5 bin7-cheng5 pian7-beng5.  34) Tan7-si7 in chit8-e7 jin7-chhut i si7 Iu5-thai3-lang5, chiu7 tai7-ke tang5-che5 toa7-siaN hoah kong2: 몮Ui2-tai7 a3! I2-hut-sou2-lang5 e5 A-ti2-bi2!몯 An2-ne hoah nng7 tiam2-cheng ku2.
	35) choe3-au7 siaN5-chhi7 e5 su-ki3-koaN tin3-ap kun5-chiong3 hou7 in leng2-cheng7, chiu7 tui3 in kong2: 몮I2-hut-sou2-lang5 a3! Sim2-mih lang5 m7 chai-iaN2 I2-hut-sou2 e5 siaN5-chhi7 si7 ui2-tai7 e5 A-ti2-bi2 e5 sin5-tian7 i2-kip8 tui3 thiN-teng2 sou2 lak(NNlak8) loh8-lai5 i e5 siong7 e5 siu2-hou7-chia2.  36) Chit e5 tai7-chi3 bo5 pian7-pok e5 i5-te7, sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 tin3-cheng7, m7-thang chhiong-tong7.  37) Lin2 chhoa7 chiah-e5 lang5 lai5 chia, in peng7 bo5 siat-tok8 ia7 bo5 hui2-pong3 lan2 e5 li2-sin5.  38) Ti2-bi2-tiu kap i e5 sai-hu7 na7 boeh khong3-ko3 sim2-mih lang5, u7 khai-teng5 e5 jit8-ki5, ia7 u7 chong2-tok; in e7-tang3 toa3 hia sio-ko3.  39) Tan7-si7 lin2 na7 iau2 u7 sim2-mih tai7-chi3 ai3-boeh tiau-cha, chiu7 tioh8 chai7 cheng3-sek e5 gi7-hoe7 lai5 kai2-koat.  40) In-ui7 kin-na2-jit8 chai7 chit e5 chu7-hoe7 sou2 hoat-seng e5 tai7-chi3, bo5 pian7-kai2 e5 i5-te7, sou2-i2 lan2 lan5-bian2 e7 hou7 lang5 ko3 jiau2-loan7 ti7-an.몯  41) Kong2 chiah-e5 oe7 liau2-au7, chiu7 kio3 in san3-hoe7.

Te7 20 ChiuN

Po2-lo5 khi3 Ma2-ki5-tun3 kap Hi-lah8:
	1) Jiau2-loan7 peng5-cheng7 liau2-au7, Po2-lo5 tiau3-chip8 bun5-tou5, ka7 in khoan3-bian2, chiu7 kap in si5-piat8, chhut-hoat khi3 Ma2-ki5-tun3.  2) I keng-koe3 hiah-e5 te7-hng, kong2 chin-che7 to7-li2 khoan3-bian2 cheng3-lang5, jian5-au7 lai5-kau3 Hi-lah8,  3) ti7 hia toa3 saN kou2(NNko3)-goeh8. I tu2 boeh che7-chun5 khi3 Su7-li7-a e5 si5, chai-iaN2 Iu5-thai3-lang5 ke3-oe7 boeh hai7 i; sou2-i2 i chiu7 koat-teng7 boeh keng-koe3 Ma2-ki5-tun3 tng2-khi3.  4) Pi3-li2-a-lang5 Pit-lou7 e5 kiaN2 Sou2-pa2-tek, Thiap-sat-lo5-ni5-ka-lang5 A-li2-tat8-kou2 kap Se-kong-tou, Tek8-pi3-lang5 Ka-iu5, kap The5-mou5-thai3, A-se-a Seng2 e5 lang5 Chhui-ki-kou2 kap Tek8-lo5-hui-mou5 chiah-e5 lang5 kap Po2-lo5 cho3-hoe2 khi3.  5) In chiah-e5 lang5 tai7-seng chhut-hoat, toa3 Tek8-lo5-a theng3-hau7 goan2.  6) Bo5-kaN3-cheh au7, goan2 khi3-kau3 Tek8-lo5-a kap in siong-hoe7, ti7 hia toa3 chit8 le2-pai3.

Po2-lo5 choe3-au7 chit8 pai2 hong2-bun7 Tek8-lo5-a:
	7) Pai3-lak8 am3 goan2 tai7-ke chu7-chip8 boehpeh mi7-pau. Po2-lo5 in-ui7 keh-tng2 jit8 boeh chhut-hoat, chiu7 tui3 in kong2 to7-li2, it-tit8 kong2 kau3 poaN3-me5.  8) Goan2 teh chu7-chip8 e5 lau5-teng2 hit keng pang5 u7 tiam2 chin-che7 pha teng-hoe2.  9) U7 chit8 e5 siau3-lian5-lang5 kio3-cho3 Iu5-chhui-kou2, che7 ti7 thang-a2-mng5-kheng; in-ui7 Po2-lo5 ke3-siok8 kong2 to7-li2 kong2 chin ku2, i it-tit8 khi2 ai3-khun3, soah khun3 loh8-bin5, soah tui3 saN lau5 poah8 loh8-khi3 thou5-kha. In ka7 i hu5 khi2-lai5 e5 si5, i i2-keng si2-khi3 a3.  10) Po2-lo5 chiu7 loh8-khi3, phak loh8-khi3 i e5 seng-khu ka7 i lam2-le3, kong2, 몮M7-bian2 hoan5-lo2, i iau2 teh oah8!몯  11) Po2-lo5 chiu7 koh khit-khi3 lau5-teng2, peh mi7-pau lai5 chiah8. Kap in tam5-lun7 chin ku2, tam5-lun7 kau3 thiN-kng, i chiah chhut-hoat.  12) In chiong hit e5 koh-oah8 khi2-lai5 e5 siau3-lian5-lang5 chhoa7 tng2-khi3, tit-tioh8 chin toa7 e5 an-ui3.

Tui3 Tek8-lo5-a khi3 Bi2-li7-tou:
	13) Goan2 tai7-seng che7-chun5, khui-chun5 khi3 A-sok, siuN7-boeh toa3 hia chih Po2-lo5 chiuN7-chun5; Po2-lo5 u7 hoan-hu3 goan2 an2-ne cho3, in-ui7 i boeh kiaN5-lou7 khi3 hia.  14) I lai5-kau3 A-sok kap goan2 siong-hoe7, goan2 chiu7 chih i chiuN7-chun5, khi3-kau3 Bi2-thui-li7-ni5.  15) Goan2 tui3 hia khui-chun5, keh-tng2 jit8 khi3-kau3 Ki-o e5 goa7-hai2. Chit8 jit8 au7 khi3-kau3 Sat-mou5 kho3-hoaN7, keh tng2 jit8 goan2 chiu7 khi3-kau3 Bi2-li7-tou.  16) Po2-lo5 kiaN-liau2 chai7 A-se-a Seng2 tam-gou7 si5-kan, chiu7 koat-i3 bo5 boeh chai7 I2-hut-sou2 theng5-liu5; in-ui7 kau3 Gou7-sun5-cheh hit jit8, siuN7-boeh chin7-liong7 koaN2 khi3-kau3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.

Po2-lo5 tui3 I2-hut-sou2 e5 tiuN2-lo2 to7-piat8:
	17) Po2-lo5 tui3 Bi2-li7-tou chhe lang5 khi3 I2-hut-sou2, chhiaN2 kau3-hoe7 e5 tiuN2-lo2 lai5.  18) In lai5 e5 si5, i chiu7 tui3 in kong2: 몮Lin2 chai-iaN2 chu7 goa2 tah8-jip8 A-se-a Seng2 hit jit8 i2-lai5, si2-chiong kap lin2 cho3-hoe2 an2-choaN2 teh seng-oah8.  19) Lin2 ia7 chai-iaN2 in-ui7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 ke3-bou5, goa2 an3-choaN2 lek8-chin7 chhi3-lian7, eng7 it-chhe3 e5 khiam-pi kap bak8-sai2 lai5 su7-hong7 Chu2.  20) Lin2 ia7 chai-iaN2 bo5-lun7 sim2-mih tui3 lin2 u7 li7-ek e5 tai7-chi3, goa2 ti7 kong-chiong3 e5 bin7-cheng5, a2-si7 ti7 lin2 ke-ke hou7-hou7, long2 m7-bat iu5-i7 put-koat bo5 ka7 lin2 kong2, bo5 ka7 lin2 ka3.  21) Bo5-lun7 tui3 Iu5-thai3-lang5 a2-si7 tui3 Hi-lah8-lang5 long2 kang7-khoan2, goa2 giam5-siok tui3 in soan-gian5 kong2 tioh8 hoe2-kai2 lai5 kui-hiong3 Siong7-chu2, ia7 tioh8 sin3 lan2 e5 Chu2 Ia5-sou.  22) Hian7-chai7 goa2 siu7 Seng3 Leng5 e5 chhui-pek, boeh khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2. Ti7 hia e7 tu2-tioh8 sim2-mih tai7-chi3 goa2 long2 m7-chai.  23) Put-ko3 goa2 chai-iaN2 Seng3 Leng5 chai7 kok siaN5-chhi7, keng2-ko3 goa2 kong2 u7 kaN-gak8 kap hoan7-lan7 teh theng3-hau7 goa2.  24) Na7-si7 ui7-tioh8 boeh oan5-seng5 goa2 e5 lou7-theng5, seng5-chiu7 goa2 tui3 Chu2 Ia5-sou nia2-siu7 e5 jim7-bu7, chiu7-si7 ui7 Siong7-chu2 in-hui7 e5 Hok-im cho3 kian3-cheng3, goa2 chit8-sut-la2 to bo5 po2-sioh goa2 e5 seN3-mia7.몯
	25) 몮Goa2 peng5-siong5 ti7 lin2 e5 tiong-kan lai5-ong2, soan-iong5 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok e5 to7-li2. TaN goa2 chai-iaN2 i2-au7 lin2 be7-tang3 koh kiN3-tioh8 goa2 e5 bin7 a7.  26) Sou2-i2 goa2 kin-na2-jit8 tui3 lin2 soan-gian5: lin2 e5 tiong-kan na7 u7 lang5 biat8-bong5, bo5 goa2 e5 chek-jim7.  27) In-ui7 Siong7-chu2 cheng2-ko5 e5 chi2-i3, goa2 long2 bo5 po2-liu5 poaN3-hang7, tak8 hang7 to thoan5 hou7 lin2.  28) Lin2 ka-ti7 tioh8 kin2-sin7, ia7 tioh8 koan2(NN3)-kou3 Seng3 Leng5 sou2 kau-thok hou7 lin2 kam3-tok e5 long2-chong2 e5 iuN5-kun5. Tioh8 bok8-iong2 Siong7-chu2 e5 kau3-hoe7, chiu7-si7 I eng7 I ka-ti7 e5 KiaN2 e5 si2-bong5 lai5 siok8-hoe5 e5.  29) Goa2 chai-iaN2 goa2 li7-khui liau2-au7, hiong-ok e5 chhai5-long5 e7 chin3 jip8-lai5 lin2 e5 tiong-kan. In e7 chan5-jim2 lai5 tui3-thai7 iuN5-kun5.  30) Lin2 ka-ti7 e5 tiong-kan, ia7 e7 u7 lang5 chhut-lai5 khiok-kai2 chin-li2, in2-iu2 bun5-tou5 khi3 kin-toe3 in.  31) Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 keng2-seng2, e7-ki3-tit goa2 saN ni5 ku2 me5-jit8 bak8-sai2 lau5 bo5 theng5, lai5 khoan3-kai2 lin2 mui2 chit8 e5 lang5.몯
	32) 몮TaN goa2 chiong lin2 kau-thok hou7 Siong7-chu2 i2-kip8 kau-thok hou7 I e5 in-hui7 e5 to7-li2. Chit e5 to7-li2 e7 ka7 lin2 kian3-lip8 tek-heng7, ia7 e7 hou7 lin2 seng5-siu7 ui7 it-chhe3 Siong7-chu2 e5 chu2-bin5 sou2 po2-chun5 e5 chiok-hok.  33) Goa2 m7-bat tham lang5 e5 kim-gin5 a2-si7 saN-khou3.  34) Lin2 ka-ti7 ia7 chai-iaN2 goa2 eng7 goa2 chit nng7 ki chhiu2 kang-chok, lai5 kiong3-kip goa2 kap goa2 e5 tang5-phoaN7 sou2 su-iau3 e5.  35) Goa2 ban7-su7 i2-sin chok-chek, chi2-si7 lin2 tioh8 an2-ne lo5-khou2 lai5 pang-chou7 loan2-jiok8 e5 lang5, ia7 tioh8 e7-ki3-tit Chu2 Ia5-sou e5 oe7 kong2, 몬Hou7 lang5 e5 , pi2 nia2-siu7 e5, khah u7 hok-khi3.몭몯
	36) Chiah-e5 oe7 kong2 soah, Po2-lo5 chiu7 kap in tai7-ke kui7 loh8-khi3 ki5-to2.  37) Tai7-ke long2 toa7-siaN khau3, lam2 i e5 am7-kun2, ka7 i chim.  38) Hou7 in choe3 siong-sim e5, chiu7-si7 in u7 thiaN-kiN3 i kong2 i2-au7 in be7-tang3 koh kiN3-tioh8 i e5 bin7. In chiu7 sang3 i khi3 che7-chun5.

Te7 21 ChiuN

Po2-lo5 khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2:
	1) Goan2 kap cheng3-lang5 li7-piatli8au-au7, chiu7 khui-chun5 it-tit8 khi3-kau3 Ko-su7; keh-tng2 jit8 khi3 Lo5-ti2, tui3 hia koh khi3 PhaN3-tai7-lah.  2) Ti7 hia tu2-tioh8 u7 chit8 chiah chun5 boeh koe3-khi3 Hui-ni5-ki, goan2 chiu7 chiuN7-chun5 chhut-hoat.  3) Goan2 lai5-kau3 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 Ku-pi2-lou7 e5 si5, chiu7 sai2 tui3 i e5 chiaN3-peng5 koe3-khi3, khi3 Su7-li7-a. Goan2 chiu7 toa3 Chhui-lo5 loh8-chun5, in-ui7 chun5 boeh toa3 hia loh8-hoe3.  4) Ti7 hia chhoe7 tioh8 chit8-koa2 bun5-tou5, chiu7 kap in toa3 chhit jit8. In siu7 Seng3 Leng5 bek8-si7, ka7 Po2-lo5 kong2 m7-thang khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.  5) Tan7-si7 goan2 kap in cho3-hoe2 toa3 chit kui2 jit8 liau2-au7, goan2 chiu7 chhut-hoat koh ke3-siok8 li2-heng5. cheng3-lang5 chhoa7 in e5 bou2-kiaN2 sang3 goan2 khi3-kau3 siaN5-goa7, tai7-ke chiu7 kui7 loh8-khi3 toa3 hai2-phiaN5 ki5-to2.  6) Hou7-siong si5-piat8 liau2-au7, goan2 chiu7 chiuN7-chun5 in chiah tng2-khi3 chhu3-nih8.
	7) Goan2 ke3-siok8 che7-chun5 tui3 Chhui-lo5 it-tit8 khi3-kau3 To-li7-mai2, ka7 hiaN-ti7 chheng2-an, kap in cho3-hoe2 toa3 chit8 jit8.  8) Keh-tng2 jit8 chhut-hoat, khi3-kau3 Kai-sat-li7-a. Goan2 chiu7 jip8-khi3 thoan5 Hok-im e5 lang5 Hui-lek8 e5 chhu3, kap i cho3-hoe2 toa3. I si7 chhit e5 chip-su7-tiong e5 chit8 e5.  9) I u7 si3 e5 bo5 kiat-hun e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, teh cho3 Siong7-chu2 e5 tai7-gian5-jin5.  10) Goan2 toa3 hia toa3 kui2-na7 jit8 e5 tiong-kan, u7 chit8 e5 Siong7-chu2 e5 tai7-gian5-jin5, kio3-cho3 A-ka-pou3, tui3 Iu5-thai3 lai5.  11) I lai5 goan2 chia, chiu7 theh8 Po2-lo5 e5 khou3-toa3, pak8 i ka-ti7 e5 kha-chhiu2, kong2: 몮Seng3 Leng5 u7 kong2, 몬Chit tiau5 khou3-toa3 e5 chu2-lang5, e7 hou7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5 an2-ne pak8 khi2-lai5, e7 hou7 in kau hou7 Goa7-pang-lang5.몭몯  12) Goan2 chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 chiah-e5 oe7, chiu7 kap hit sou2-chai7 e5 lang5 khun2-kiu5 Po2-lo5 m7-thang khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.  13) Tan7-si7 Po2-lo5 in3 kong2: 몮Lin2 an3-choaN2 an2-ne khau3, lai5 hou7 goa2 siong-sim? Goa2 ui7-tioh8 Chu2 Ia5-sou, put-tan7 hou7 lang5 pak8, lian5 si2 toa3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, goa2 ia7 kam-goan7.몯  14) Po2-lo5 ki3-jian5 m7 thiaN goan2 khou2-khng3, goan2 ia7 chiu7 bo5 oe7 thang koh kong2, chi2-u7 tui3 i kong2, 몮Goan7 Chu2 e5 chi2-i3 seng5-chiu7.몯
	15) Kui2-na7 jit8 au7, goan2 heng5-li2 khoan2 ho2, chiu7 chiuN7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.  16) U7 chit8-koa2 tui3 Kai-sat-li7-a lai5 e5 bun5-tou5 ia7 kap goan2 khi3, chhoa7 goan2 boeh khi3 chit8 e5 Ku-pi2-lou7-lang5 Na2-sun e5 chhu3. I si7 chin cha2 chiu7 cho3 bun5-tou5 e5.

Po2-lo5 hong2-bun7 Nga2-kok:
	17) Goan2 kau3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 si5, chai7-te7 e5 hiaN-ti7 jiat8-liat8 ka7 goan2 hoan-geng5.  18) Keh-tng2 jit8, Po2-lo5 kap goan2 khi3 hong2-bun7 Nga2-kok; kau3-hoe7 e5 tiuN2-lo2 ia7 long2 ti7 hia.  19) Po2-lo5 ka7 in chheng2-an liau2-au7, chiu7 siong5-se3 ka7 in po3-ko3 Siong7-chu2 thong-koe3 i e5 thoan5-kau3 kang-chok, chai7 Goa7-pang-lang5 e5 tiong-kan sou2 cho3 it-chhe3 e5 tai7-chi3.  20) In thiaN-kiN3 liau2-au7, long2 chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2, chiu7 tui3 Po2-lo5 kong2: 몮HiaN-ti7 a3, li2 khoaN3, chia u7 seng5-chhian seng5-ban7 e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5 lai5 cho3 Ki-tok-tou5 a7, in ia7 long2 chin jiat8-sim siu2 Lut8-hoat.  21) In thiaN-kiN3 lang5 kong2 li2 ka3-si7 toa3 ti7 Goa7-pang it-chhe3 e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5, tioh8 hong3-khi3 Mou5-se e5 Lut8-hoat, ka7 in kong2 m7-thang ka7 in e5 gin2-na2 si-heng5 kat-le2, ia7 m7-bian2 siu2 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 koan3-le7.  22) In long2 tek-khak e7 thiaN-kiN3 li2 lai5 a7. TaN boeh an3-choaN2 pan7?  23) Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 chiau3 goan2 ka7 li2 kong2 e5 an2-ne khi3 cho3. Goan2 chia u7 si3 e5 lang5 he7-goan7.  24) Li2 chhoa7 in khi3 cho3-hoe2 chham-ka kiat-cheng7-le2, ka7 in chhut sou2-hui3 hou7 in thi3-thau5. An2-ne cheng3-lang5 chiu7 e7 chai-iaN2 in sou2 thiaN-kiN3 koan-he7 li2 e5 tai7-chi3, long2 m7-si7 su7-sit8 e5, tian-to3 e7 chai-iaN2 li2 u7 chun-siu2 Mou5-se e5 Lut8-hoat teh seng-oah8.  25) Tan7-si7 tui3 i2-keng cho3 Ki-tok-tou5 e5 Goa7-pang-lang5, goan2 i2-keng u7 sia2-phe ka7 in kong2 goan2 u7 koat-gi7 kio3 in m7-thang chiah8 u7 pai3-koe3 ngou2-siong7 e5 chiah8-mih8, a2-si7 hoeh, a2-si7 teN7-si2 e5 cheng-seN, ia7 tioh8 kim3-kai3 sia5-im5.몯  26) Po2-lo5 chiu7 chhoa7 hit si3 e5 lang5, keh-tng2 jit8 kap in cho3-hoe2 chham-ka kiat-cheng7-le2. Jian5-au7 jip8-khi3 seng3-tian7, po3-ko3 kiat-cheng7-le2 e5 jit8-ki5 kau3 sim2-mih si5 e7 moa2, hit e5 si5 thang ui7 in kok lang5 hian3 che3-phin2.

Po2-lo5 ti7 seng3-tian7-lai7 hou7 lang5 liah8-khi3:
	27) Hit chhit jit8 teh-boeh moa2 e5 si5, u7 chit8-koa2 tui3 A-se-a Seng2 lai5 e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5, khoaN3-kiN3 Po2-lo5 ti7 Seng3-tian7-lai7, chiu7 sian3-tong7 kun5-chiong3, he7-chhiu2 liah8 Po2-lo5,  28) hoah kong2: 몮I2-sek-liat-lang5 a3, lai5 pang-chou7 le3! To3-chhu3 kau3-hun3 cheng3-lang5 lai5 hoan2-tui3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 jin5-bin5 kap Mou5-se e5 Lut8-hoat i2-kip8 chit e5 Seng3-tian7 e5, chiu7-si7 chit e5 lang5. TaN, i siong7-chhiaN2 chhoa7 chit8-koa2 Hi-lah8-lang5 jip8-lai5 Seng3-tian7, siat-tok8 chit e5 sin5-seng3 e5 tiuN5-sou2!몯  29) (In an2-ne kong2, si7 in-ui7 in bat khoaN3-kiN3 I2-hut-sou2-lang5 Tek8-lo5-hui-mou5 kap Po2-lo5 ti7 chhi7-lai7, sou2-i2 in siuN7 kong2 si7 Po2-lo5 chhoa7 i jip8-lai5 Seng3-tian7 e5.)  30) Choan5 siaN5-chhi7 long2 khi2 hun7-loan7, bin5-chiong3 long2 chau2 oa2-lai5, liah8 Po2-lo5, thoa i chhut-khi3 Seng3-tian7 e5 goa7-bin7. Seng3-tian7 e5 mng5 chiu7 chek-si5 koaiN khi2-lai5.  31) Kun5-chiong3 tu2 teh siuN7-boeh thai5-si2 Po2-lo5 e5 si5, u7 lang5 po3-ko3 Lo5-ma2 kun-tui7 e5 iaN5-tiuN2 kong2 choan5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 teh khi2 po7-tong7.  32) IaN5-tiuN2 chiu7 chek-si5 toa3 peng kap kui2-na7 e5 kun-koaN chhiong jip8-khi3 kun5-chiong3 e5 lai7-bin7. Kun5-chiong3 chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 iaN5-tiuN2 kap peng-tui7 lai5, chiu7 m7-kaN2 koh phah Po2-lo5.  33) IaN5-tiuN2 oa2-khi3 liah8 Po2-lo5, kio3 lang5 eng7 nng7 tiau5 lian7-a2 ka7 i lian7 khi2-lai5, mng7 kong2, 몮Chit e5 lang5 si7 sim2-mih lang5, u7 cho3 sim2-mih tai7-chi3?몯  34) Kun5-chiong3 chit8 e5 hoah chit8 khoan2; in-ui7 loan7-chhau-chhau, iaN5-tiuN2 be7-tang3 chai-iaN2 sit8-cheng5, chiu7 beng7-leng7 pou7-ha7 khan Po2-lo5 jip8-khi3 iaN5-pang5.  35) In chhoa7 i lai5-kau3 gim5-a2-kha e5 si5, in-ui7 kun5-chiong3 chin hiong-beng2, sou2-i2 peng-su7 soah tioh8 ka7 i chhah khit-khi3.  36) Chit8 toa7 tin7 lang5 long2 toe3 toa3 i e5 au7-bin7, hoah kong2, 몮Ka7 i thai5-si2!몯

Po2-lo5 ui5 chu7-ki2 pian7-hou7:
	37) In tu2 boeh thoa Po2-lo5 jip8-khi3 iaN5-pang5 e5 si5, i tui3 iaN5-tiuN2 kong2, 몮Goa2 e7-eng7-tit ka7 li2 kong2 kui2-ku3-a2 oe7 be7?몯 IaN5-tiuN2 mng7 i kong2: 몮Li2 e7-hiauk2ong Hi-lah8-oe7 be7?  38) Li2 kam2 m7-si7 khah-cha2 cho7-hoan2 chhoa7 si3-chheng e5 hiong-siu2 chau2 jip8-khi3 khong3-ia2 hit e5 Ai-kip8-lang5?몯  39) Po2-lo5 in3 kong2: 몮GOa2 si7 Iu5-thai3-lang5, ti7 Ki-li7-ka e5 Tai7-sou3 chhut-si3, si7 chit8 e5 chhut-mia5 e5 siaN5-chhi7 e5 chhi7-bin5. ChhiaN2 li2 chun2 goa2 tui3 bin5-chiong3 kong2-oe7.몯  40) IaN5-tiuN2 chun2 i, Po2-lo5 chiu7 khia7 toa3 gim5-a2-teng2, tui3 bin5-chiong3 io5-chhiu2. Cheng3-lang5 long2 tiam7-khi3, Po2-lo5 chiu7 eng7 Hi-pek-lai5-oe7 ka7 in kong2:

Te7 22 ChiuN

	1) 몮Chu-ui7 hu7-lo2 hiaN-ti7, goa2 taN toa3 lin2  bin7-cheng5 boeh ka-ti7 pian7-beng5, chhiaN2 lin2 ka7 goa2 thiaN!몯  2) Cheng3-lang5 thiaN-kiN3 i eng7 Hi-pek-lai5-oe7 ka7 in kong2, in chiu7 koh-khah siok-cheng7. Po2-lo5 ke3-siok8 kong2:
3) 몮Goa2 si7 Iu5-thai3-lang5, ti7 Ki-li7-ka e5 Tai7-sou3 chhut-si3, ti7 chit e5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2-siaN5 tiong2-seng5, cho3 Ka-ma2-liat8 e5 hak8-seng, chiau3 lan2 e5 chou2-sian e5 Lut8-hoat giam5-keh siu7 kau3-iok8, kap kin-na2-jit8 ti7 chia e5 lin2 tai7-ke kang7-khoan2, jiat8-sim su7-hong7 Siong7-chu2.  4) Goa2 ia7 bat pek-hai7 sin3-hong7 chit e5 To7 e5 lang5 pek-hai7 kau3 si2, bo5-lun7 cha-pou cha-bou2, liah8 in koaiN-loh8 kaN-gak8.  5) Che3-si-tiuN2 kap chiong3 tiuN2-lo2 to e7-tang3 ka7 goa2 cheng3-beng5 che si7 su7-sit8 e5, in-ui7 in u7 sia2 boeh hou7 toa3 ti7 Tai7-ma2-sek Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 hiaN-ti7 e5 phe hou7 goa2 toa3 khi3. Goa2 khi3 hia e5 bok8-tek si7 boeh liah8 toa3 ti7 hia e5 Ki-tok-tou5 tng2-lai5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 chhu2-hoat8.몯

Po2-lo5 tam5-lun7 i an3-choaN2 lai5 kui Chu2: (Heng5-toan7 9:1-19; 26:12-18)
	6) 몮Goa2 khi3 teh-boeh kau3 Tai7-ma2-sek e5 si5, chha-put-to tiong-tau3. Hut-jian5-kan tui3 thiN-teng2 u7 chit8 e5 chin kiong5 e5 kng, chio3-sia7 loh8-lai5 goa2 e5 chiu-ui5.  7) Goa2 chiu7 poah8 loh8-khi3 thou5-kha, thiaN-kiN3 chit8 e5 siaN ka7 goa2 kong2, 몬So3-lo5, So3-lo5, li2 an3-choaN2 pek-hai7 Goa2?몭  8) Goa2 in3 kong2, 몬Chu2 a3, Li2 si7 sim2-mih lang5?몭 I in3 goa2 kong2, 몬Goa2 chiu7-si7 li2 sou2 pek-hai7 e5 Na2-sat-lek8-lang5 Ia5-sou.몭  9) Kap goa2 cho3-hoe2 kiaN5 e5 lang5, u7 khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 kng, m7-ku2 bo5 thiaN-kiN3 tui3 goa2 kong2-oe7 Hit-ui7 e5 siaN.  10) Goa2 kong2, 몬chu2 a3, taN goa2 tioh8 an3-choaN2 cho3 chiah ho2?몭 Chu2 ka7 goa2 kong2, 몬Khi2-lai5 jip8-khi3 Tai7-ma2-sek, ti7 hia Siong7-chu2 sou2 chi2-teng7 boeh hou7 li2 cho3 it-chhe3 e5 tai7-chi3, long2 e7 ka7 li2 kong2.몭  11) In-ui7 hit e5 kng-soaN3 siuN kiong5, goa2 e5 bak8-chiu soah bo5 khoaN3-kiN3, chiu7 hou7 goa2 e5 tang5-phoaN7 khan goa2 e5 chhiu2 jip8-khi3 Tai7-ma2-sek.몯
	12) 몮Ti7 hia u7 chit8 e5 lang5 kio3-cho3 A-na2-ni5-a, si7 chit8 e5 chin khian5-seng5 chun-siu2 Lut8-hoat e5 lang5, chin siu7 toa3 ti7 Tai7-ma2-sek e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5 chun-keng3.  13) I lai5 chhoe7 goa2, khia7 toa3 goa2 e5 sin-piN, kong2, 몬HiaN-ti7 So3-lo5, hou7 li2 koh u7 khoaN3-kiN3!몭 goa2 e5 bak8-chiu chek-si5 chiu7 koh kim khi2-lai5, u7 khoaN3-kiN3 i.  14) I chiu7 kong2: 몬Lan2 chou2-sian e5 Siong7-chu2 i2-keng keng2-soan2 li2, hou7 li2 chai-iaN2 I e5 chi2-i3, lai5 kiN3 I kong-gi7 e5 Pok8-jin5, thiaN I e5 chhui3 sou2 kong2 e5 siaN.  15) In-ui7 li2 e7 chiong li2 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3, sou2 thiaN-kiN3 e5, tui3 ban7-bin5 lai5 ka7 I cho3 kian3-cheng3.  16) TaN, li2 si7 an3-choaN2 iau2 teh tiu5-ti5? Khi2-lai5, hou-kiu5 I e5 mia5 siu7 se2-le2, lai5 se2-chheng li2 e5 choe7.몭몯

Po2-lo5 khi3 tui3 Goa7-pang-lang5 thoan5-kau3:
	17) 몮Goa2 chiu7 tng2-lai5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, ti7 Seng3-tian7 teh ki5-to2 e5 si5, goa2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 i7-siong7.  18) Chai7 i7-siong7 tiong, Chu2 ka7 goa2 kong2, 몬Li2 tioh8 koaN2-kin2 li7-khui Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, in-ui7 ti7 chia e5 lang5 bo5 boeh chiap-siu7 li2 ui7 Goa2 boeh cho3 e5 kian3-cheng3.몭  19) Goa2 in3 kong2, 몬chu2 a3, in chai-iaN2 goa2 i2-cheng5 khi3 kok hoe7-tng5, chiong sin3 Li2 e5 lang5 liah8 khi2-lai5 koaiN, ka7 in phah.  20) Iu7-koh Li2 e5 kian3-cheng3-jin5 Su7-the5-hoan2 hou7 lang5 thai5-si2 e5 si5, goa2 pun2-sin ia7 ti7 hia, chan3-tong5 i e5 hiong-sat, sim7-chi3 khoaN3-kou3 hiah-e5 hiong-siu2 e5 goa7-saN.몭  21) Chu2 tui3 goa2 kong2, 몬Li2 khi3. goa2 boeh chhe-phai3 li2 khi3 hng7-hng7 e5 Goa7-pang-lang5 hia.몭몯
	22) Cheng3-lang5 thiaN Po2-lo5 kong2 kau3 chit ku3 oe7, chiu7 toa7 siaN hoah kong2: 몮Chit khoan2 e5 lang5, tioh8 tui3 te7-siong7 ka7 i siau-biat8! M7-thang hou7 i oah8!몯  23) In toa7 siaN jiong2, thng3 saN khi2-lai5 iaN7, hiong3 khong-tiong ia7 thou5-soa.  24) Lo5-ma2 e5 iaN5-tiuN2 beng7-leng7 lang5 chiong Po2-lo5 chhoa7 jip8-khi3 iaN5-pang5, kio3 in eng7 piN ka7 i phah, boeh chai-iaN2 Iu5-thai3-lang5 si7 an3-choaN2 tui3 i an2-ne teh jiong2.  25) Tan7-si7 in eng7 phoe5-toa3 ka7 i pak8 khi2-lai5 boeh phah e5 si5, Po2-lo5 ka7 khia7 ti7 piN-a e5 kun-koaN kong2, 몮Tui3 chit8 e5 Lo5-ma2 e5 kong-bin5, ia7 bo5 ka7 i sim2-phoaN3, lin2 chiu7 boeh eng7 piN phah i, kam2 u7 hap8-hoat?몯  26) Kun-koaN thiaN-kiN3 an2-ne, chiu7 khi3 kiN3 iaN5-tiuN2, ka7 i kong2, 몮TaN li2 boeh an3-choaN2 pan7? Hit e5 lang5 si7 Lo5-ma2 e5 kong-bin5!몯  27) IaN5-tiuN2 chiu7 khi3 chhoe7 Po2-lo5, mng7 i kong2, 몮Li2 ka7 goa2 kong2, li2 si7 Lo5-ma2 e5 kong-bin5 a2 m7-si7?몯 Po2-lo5 kong2, 몮Si7.몯  28) IaN5-tiuN2 kong2, 몮Goa2 eng7 chin-che7 chiN5 chiah be2 tioh8 Lo5-ma2 e5 kong-bin5-koan5.몯 Po2-lo5 kong2, 몮Tan7-si7 goa2 chhut-si3 chiu7-si7 Lo5-ma2 e5 kong-bin5.몯  29) Boeh sim2-mng7 Po2-lo5 hiah-e5 lang5, chiu7 chek-si5 kiu-khi3; iaN5-tiuN2 chit8-e7 chai-iaN2 i si7 Lo5-ma2 e5 kong-bin5, ia7 in-ui7 u7 ka7 i pak8, chiu7 chin kiaN.

Po2-lo5 chai7 kong-gi7-hoe7 siu7-sim2:
	30) Keh-tng2 jit8, iaN5-tiuN2 ai3-boeh chai-iaN2 Iu5-thai3-lang5 ko3 Po2-lo5 e5 sit8-cheng5, chiu7 thau2-khui Po2-lo5 e5 lian7-a2, beng7-leng7 hiah-e5 che3-si-tiuN2 kap choan5 kong-gi7-hoe7 e5 gi7-oan5 long2 chu7-chip8, chhoa7 Po2-lo5 lai5, hou7 i khia7 toa3 in e5 bin7-cheng5.

Te7 23 ChiuN

	Po2-lo5 chu3-sin5 khoaN3 kong-gi7-hoe7 e5 gi7-oan5, kong2, 몮Chu-ui7 hiaN-ti7 a3! goa2 kau3 kin-na2-jit8, chai7 Siong7-chu2 e5 bin7-cheng5, to si7 oan5-choan5 chiau3 chheng-pek8 e5 liong5-sim seng-oah8.몯  2) Che3-si-tiuN2  A-na2-ni5-a chiu7 beng7-leng7 khia7 ti7 Po2-lo5 e5 piN-a e5 lang5 phah i e5 chhui3.  3) Po2-lo5 chiu7 tui3 i kong2: 몮Li2 chit e5 gui7-sian7 e5 lang5 a3, Siong7-chu2 it-teng7 e7 ka7 li2 phah! Li2 che7-tng5 si7 an3-chiau3 Lut8-hoat boeh ka7 goa2 sim2-phoaN3, tan7-si7 li2 soah ui5-poe7 Lut8-hoat; beng7-leng7 lang5 phah goa2!몯  4) Khia7 ti7 Po2-lo5 e5 piN-a e5 lang5 kong2, 몮Li2 kaN2 bu2-jiok8 Siong7-chu2 e5 che3-si-tiuN2!몯  5) Po2-lo5 in3 kong2, 몮HiaN-ti7 a3, goa2 m7 chai-iaN2 i si7 che3-si-tiuN2. In-ui7 Seng3-keng u7 ki3-chai3 kong2, 몬M7-thang tui3 lin2 peh-seN3 e5 thau5-lang5 kong2 phaiN2-oe7.몭몯
	6) Tan7-si7 Po2-lo5 khoaN3-chhut in chit8 peng5 si7 Sat-thou2-kai-tong2 e5 lang5, chit8 peng5 si7 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5, i chiu7 chai7 kong-gi7-hoe7 toa7-siaN kong2: 몮Chu-ui7 hiaN-ti7 a3, goa2 si7 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5, si7 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 e5 kiaN2. Goa2 ti7 chia siu7 sim2-phoaN3, si7 in-ui7 goa2 ng3-bang7 si2-lang5 e7 koh-oah8 khi2-lai5!몯  7) I chit8-e7 an2-ne kong2, Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 kap Sat-thou2-kai-tong2 e5 lang5 chiu7 khai-si2 hun-cheng, hoe7-chiong3 chiu7 hun cho3 nng7 phai3.  8) In-ui7 Sat-thou2-kai-tong2 e5 lang5 kong2 si2-lang5 be7 koh-oah8 khi2-lai5, bo5 thian-sai3 ia7 bo5 leng5-hun5 --- tan7-si7 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 chu2-tiuN chit saN hang7 long2 u7.  9) Hit e5 si5 lu2 jiong2 lu2 toa7 siaN, u7 kui2-na7 e5 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 keng-hak8-chia2 khia7 khi2-lai5, toan3-gian5 kong2: 몮Goan2 be7-tang3 tui3 chit e5 lang5 chhoe7-chhut sim2-mih chho3-gou7! Bo5-tiaN7-tioh8 u7 leng5-hun5 a2-si7 thian-sai3 ka7 i chi2-tiam2!몯
	10) Gi7-lun7 lu2 lai5 lu2 kek-liat8, iaN5-tiuN2 kiaN-liau2 Po2-lo5 hou7 in thiah kah chhui3-kut-hun-sin, chiu7 beng7-leng7 peng-a2 loh8-khi3 tui3 cheng3-lang5 e5 tiong-kan chiong i chhiuN2 chhut-lai5, chhoa7 i jip8-khi3 peng-iaN5.
	11) Keh-tng2 am3, Chu2 lai5 khia7 toa3 Po2-lo5 e5 sin-piN, kong2: 몮Tioh8 iong2-kam2 chong3-taN2! Li2 i2-keng ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 ui7 Goa2 cho3 kian3-cheng3 a3; li2 ia7 tioh8 toa3 Lo5-ma2 chiau3 an2-ne ui7 Goa2 cho3 kian3-cheng3.몯

Ke3-bou5 sat-hai7 Po2-lo5:
	12) Keh-tng2 chai2-khi2, Iu5-thai3-lang5 cho3-hoe2 ke3-bou5, chiu3-choa7 kong2 na7 bo5 theng3-hau7 kau3 thai5-si2 Po2-lo5, in ia7 m7 chiah8, ia7 m7 lim.  13) Cho3-hoe2 an2-ne ke3-bou5 e5 lang5 u7 si3-chap8 e5 i2-siong7.  14) In chiu7 khi3 kiN3 che3-si-tiuN2 kap tiuN2-lo2, kong2: 몮Goan2 hou7-siong kian-koat chiu3-choa7 kong2 na7 bo5 theng3-hau7 kau3 thai5-si2 Po2-lo5, poaN3 hang7 mih8 to m7 chiah8.  15) Hian7-chai7 lin2 kap kong-gi7-hoe7 e5 gi7-oan5 tioh8 kio3 Lo5-ma2 e5 koaN-tiuN2 sang3 Po2-lo5 lai5 chia, ke2 cho3 lin2 boeh koh-khah siong5-se3 tiau-cha i e5 an3-kiaN7. Tan7-si7 goan2 chun2-pi7 i iau2-boe7 kau3 chia i2-cheng5, chiu7 boeh ka7 i thai5-si2.몯
	16) Tan7-si7 Po2-lo5 e5 goe7-seng chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 chit e5 im-bou5, chiu7 jip8-khi3 peng-iaN5 po3-ko3 Po2-lo5.  17) Po2-lo5 chhiaN2 chit8 e5 lian5-tiuN2 lai5, ka7 i kong2, 몮Li2 chhoa7 chit e5 siau3-lian5-lang5 khi3 kiN3 iaN5-tiuN2, in-ui7 i u7 tai7-chi3 boeh ka7 iaN5-tiuN2 po3-ko3.몯  18) Lian5-tiuN2 chiu7 chhoa7 i lai5 kiN3 iaN5-tiuN2 kong2, 몮Hit e5 siu5-hoan7 Po2-lo5 kio3 goa2 khi3, kiu5 goa2 chhoa7 chit e5 siau3-lian5-lang5 lai5 kiN3 li2, in-ui7 i u7 tai7-chi3 boeh ka7 li2 po3-ko3.몯  19) IaN5-tiuN2 chiu7 khan i e5 chhiu2, khi3 piN-a mng7 i kong2, 몮Li2 u7 sim2-mih tai7-chi3 boeh ka7 goa2 po3-ko3?몯  20) I kong2: 몮Iu5-thai3-lang5 u7 ke3-ek8 boeh chhiaN2 li2 bin5-na2-chai3 sang3 Po2-lo5 loh8-khi3 kong-gi7-hoe7, ke2 cho3 boeh koh siong5-se3 tiau-cha i e5 an3-kiaN7.  21) Kiu5 li2 m7-thang thiaN in e5 oe7, in-ui7 in u7 si3-chap8 goa7 e5 lang5 bai5-hok8 teh tng-tan2 i. In u7 chiu3-choa7 kong2 na7 bo5 theng3-hau7 kau3 ka7 i thai5-si2, ia7 m7 chiah8, ia7 m7 lim. TaN in long2 chun2-pi7 pian7-pian7, teh theng3-hau7 li2 e5 in2-chun2.몯  22) IaN5-tiuN2 ka7 i kong2, 몮M7-thang ka7 lang5 kong2 li2 u7 lai5 ka7 goa2 po3-ko3 chit hang7 tai7-chi3.몯 I chiu7 kio3 chit e5 siau3-lian5-lang5 tng2-khi3.

Hou7-sang3 Po2-lo5 khi3 hou7 chong2-tok Hui-lek8-su7:
	23) IaN5-tiuN2 chiu7 kio3 nng7 e5 lian5-tiuN2 lai5, ka7 in kong2: 몮Eng-am3 kau2 tiam2 i2-cheng5, tioh8 chun2-pi7 nng7-pah e5 pou7-peng, chhit-chap8 e5 be2-peng, nng7-pah e5 giah8 chhiuN e5 peng thang khi3 Kai-sat-li7-a.  24) Ia7 tioh8 chun2-pi7 be2 thang hou7 Po2-lo5 khia5, hou7-sang3 i an-choan5 khi3-kau3 chong2-tok Hui-lek8-su7 hia.몯  25) IaN5-tiuN2 iu7-koh sia2 chit8 tiuN phe kong2:
	26) 몮Kek-lo2-tiu Lu7-se-a ka7 chong2-tok Hui-lek8-su7 kok-ha7 chheng2-an.  27) Chit e5 Po2-lo5 hou7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 liah8-khi3, teh boeh hou7 in thai5-si2. Goa2 chit8-e7 chai-iaN2 i si7 Lo5-ma2 e5 kong-bin5, chiu7 chhoa7 peng khi3 ka7 i kiu3 chhut-lai5.  28) Goa2 ai3-boeh chai-iaN2 in ko3 i e5 li2-iu5, sou2-i2 goa2 sang3 i loh8-khi3 in e5 kong-gi7-hoe7.  29) Goa2 chiah chai-iaN2 i hou7 in ko3 si7 ui7-tioh8 tui3 in e5 lut8-hoat e5 kian3-kai2 bo5 kang7-khoan2, peng7 m7-si7 u7 hoan7-tioh8 sim2-mih eng-kai siu7 si2-heng5 a2-si7 tou5-heng5 e5 choe7-chng7.  30) U7 lang5 ka7 goa2 po3-ko3 IU5-thai3-lang5 teh ke3-bou5 boeh ham7-hai7 i, sou2-i2 goa2 chiu7 sui5-si5 sang3 i khi3-kau3 li2 hia, beng7-leng7 ko3 i e5 lang5 toa3 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 khong3-ko3 i.몯
	31) Pou7-peng chiu7 chiau3 iaN5-tiuN2 e5 beng7-leng7, thau3-me5 chiong Po2-lo5 chhoa7 khi3-kau3 An-the5-phaN3-ti2.  32) Keh-tng2 jit8 hou7 be2-peng sang3 i khi3, in chiu7 tng2-khi3 peng-iaN5.  33) Hiah-e5 be2-peng sang3 i khi3-kau3 Kai-sat-li7-a, chiong hit tiuN phe kau hou7 chong2-tok, chiu7 chhoa7 Po2-lo5 lai5 i e5 bin7-cheng5.  34) Chong2-tok thak8 hit tiuN phe liau2-au7, mng7 Po2-lo5 khoaN3 i si7 tah chit8 seng2 e5 lang5. Chit8-e7 chai-iaN2 i si7 Ki-li7-ka-lang5,  35) chiu7 kong2, 몮Theng3-hau7 ko3 li2 e5 lang5 lai5 e5 si5, goa2 chiah lai5 chhu2-li2 li2 e5 an3-kiaN7.몯 I chiu7 beng7-leng7 lang5 toa3 Hi-lut8 e5 hong5-kiong-lai7 kou3-siu2 Po2-lo5.

Te7 24 ChiuN

Iu5-thai3-lang5 khong3-ko3 Po2-lo5:
	1) Gou7 jit8 au7, che3-si-tiuN2 A-na2-ni5-a, kap kui2-na7 e5 tiuN2-lo2, i2-kip8 chit8 e5 lut8-su kio3-cho3 Thiap-thou2-lo5 loh8-lai5 Kai-sat-li7-a. In lai5 chong2-tok e5 bin7-cheng5 ko3 Po2-lo5.  2) Po2-lo5 chit8-e7 hou7 lang5 tiau3 chhut-tng5, Thiap-thou2-lo5 chiu7 khai-si2 khong3-ko3 i kong2: 
	몮Hui-lek8-su7 kok-ha7! goan2 chai7 li2 e5 leng2-to7 ha7 toa7-toa7 hiong2-siu7 thai3-peng5. In-ui7 li2 u7 sian-kian3 chi beng5, chit e5 kok-ka tit-tioh8 toa7-toa7 e5 kek-sin.  3) Chit hang7 tai7-chi3 hou7 goan2 si5-si5 chhu3-chhu3 hoan-geng5, chhim-chhim kam2-sia7.  4) TaN goa2 m7-kaN2 ian5-chhian5 li2 siuN ku2, kiu5 li2 khoan-iong5 lai5 thiaN goan2 kan2-tan e5 sin-ko3.  5) Goan2 chha5-chhut chit e5 lang5 chhin-chhiuN7 thoan5-jiam2-peN7, chai7 choan5 se3-kai3 Iu5-thai3-lang5-tiong sian3-tong7 lang5 chok-loan7. I si7 Na2-sat-lek8 tong2-phai3 e5 siu2-leng2.  6) I sim7-chi2 siuN7-boeh siat-tok8 Seng3-tian7, goan2 chiu7 ka7 i liah8 khi2-lai5. (Goan2 boeh chiau3 goan2 e5 Lut8-hoat ka7 i sim2-mng7,  7) tan7-si7 iaN5-tiuN2 Lu7-se-a jip8-lai5, chiong i tui3 goan2 e5 chhiu2 kiong5-kiong5 chhiuN2-khi3.  8) Lu7-se-a beng7-leng7 ko3 i e5 lang5 tioh8 lai5 li2 chia.) Li2 na7 sim2-mng7 chit e5 lang5, li2 chiu7 e7 chai-iaN2 goan2 sou2 khong3-ko3 i it-chhe3 e5 tai7-chi3 .몯  9) Iu5-thai3-lang5 ia7 long2 chham loh8-khi3 khong3-ko3 i, kheng2-teng7 kong2 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 long2 si7 su7-sit8 e5.

Po2-lo5 chai7 Hui-lek8-su7 bin7-cheng5 pian7-beng5:
	10) Chong2-tok chiu7 tui3 Po2-lo5 tim3-thau5 kio3 i hoat-gian5, Po2-lo5 chiu7 tap-pian7 kong2:
	몮Goa2 chai-iaN2 li2 tui3 chit e5 jin5-bin5 eng7 kong-gi7 lai5 chip-cheng3 chin-che7 ni5 a7, sou2-i2 goa2 e7-tang3 hong3-sim toa3 li2 bin7-cheng5 ui7 ka-ti7 pian7-hou7.  11) Li2 ka-ti7 tiau-cha chiu7 e7 chai-iaN2, goa2 chiuN7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 khi3 keng3-pai3 kau3 taN put-ko3 u7 chap8-ji7 jit8.  12) Iu5-thai3-lang5 bo5 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 goa2 ti7 Seng3-tian7, a2-si7 ti7 hoe7-tng5, a2-si7 ti7 siaN5-chhi7-lai7 kap lang5 pian7-lun7, a2-si7 sian3-tong7 kun5-chiong3.  13) In hian7-chai7 sou2 khong3-ko3 goa2 e5 tai7-chi3, ia7 be7-tang3 theh8-chhut sim2-mih cheng3-ki3 lai5 hou7 li2.  14) Tan7-si7 goa2 tioh8 tui3 li2 seng5-jin7 chit8 hang7 tai7-chi3: chiu7-si7 goa2 u7 an3-chiau3 in sou2 kio3-cho3 i7-toan e5 To7, lai5 keng3-pai3 lan2 chou2-sian e5 Siong7-chu2. Tan7-si7 goa2 ia7 u7 sin3 ti7 Mou5-se Lut8-hoat e5 chheh i2-kip8 tai7-gian5-jin5 e5 chheh sou2 ki3-chai3 it-chhe3 e5 tai7-chi3.  15) Goa2 tui3 Siong7-chu2 u7 phau7 hi-bong7, chiu7-si7 ho2-lang5 kap phaiN2-lang5 long2 e7 tui3 si2-lang5 tiong koh-oah8 khi2-lai5; che ia7 si7 in ka-ti7 sou2 teh ki5-thai7 e5.  16) In-ui7 an2-ne, goa2 siong5-siong5 ka-ti7 chin7-lek8, bo5-lun7 si7 tui3 Siong7-chu2 a2-si7 tui3 lang5, long2 po2-chhi5 chheng-pek8 e5 liong5-sim.
	17) 몮Goa2 li7-khui Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 kui2-na7 ni5 au7, goa2 koh tng2-khi3, u7 theh8 chit8-koa2 chiN5 khi3 chin2-che3 tong5-pau kap hong7-hian3 che3-phin2.  18) Ti7 seng3-tian7 teh hian3 che3-phin2 e5 si5, in khoaN3-tioh8 goa2. Goa2 chham-ka kiat-cheng7-le2 liau2-au7, hit e5 si5 bo5 kun5-chiong3 ti7 hia, ia7 bo5 jiau2-loan7.  19) Tan7-si7 u7 kui2-na7 e5 tui3 A-se-a lai5 e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5 ti7 hia. Ka2-su2 in na7 u7 sim2-mih boeh khong3-ko3 goa2, in eng-kai tioh8 ka-ti7 lai5 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 ko3 goa2 chiah tioh8.  20) A2-si7 ti7 chia chiah-e5 lang5, na7 u7 hoat-kian3 goa2 khia7 ti7 kong-gi7-hoe7 cheng5 e5 si5 u7 hoan7-tioh8 sim2-mih choe7, in tioh8 ka-ti7 kongchhut2-lai5.  21) Goa2 khia7 ti7 in tiong-kan e5 si5, goa2 put-ko3 u7 toa7-siaN kong2 chit8 ku3 oe7 nia7-nia7; chiu7-si7 kong2: 몬In-ui7 goa2 sin3 si2-lang5 e7 koh-oah8 khi2-lai5, goa2 kin-na2-jit8 chiah lai5 siu7 lin2 e5 sim2-phoaN3.몭몯
	22) In-ui7 Hui-lek8-su7 siong5-se3 chai-iaN2 chit e5 To7 e5 tai7-chi3, chiu7 soan-pou3 hiu-hoe7, kong2, 몮Theng3-hau7 kau3 iaN5-tiuN2 Lu7-se-a lai5 e5 si5, goa2 chiah lai5 phoaN3-koat lin2 e5 an3-kiaN7.몯  23) I chiu7 beng7-leng7 lian5-tiuN2 siu-ah Po2-lo5, thang chou2-chi2 i e5 peng5-iu2 toa3 i khiam3-eng7 e5 mih8 lai5 khoaN3 i.

Po2-lo5 chai7 Hui-lek8-su7 kap Thou2-se-lah e5 bin7-cheng5:
	24) Kui2-na7 jit8 au7, Hui-lek8-su7 kap i e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 thai3-thai3 Thou2-se-lah lai5. I kio3 Po2-lo5 chhut-lai5, thiaN i kang2-lun7 koan-he7 sin3 Ki-tok Ia5-sou e5 to7-li2.  25) Tan7-si7 Po2-lo5 lun7 kau3 kong-cheng3, chiat-che3 kap chiong-lai5 e5 sim2-phoaN3 e5 si5, Hui-lek8-su7 soah khi2 kiaN-hiaN5, kong2, 몮TaN li2 ho2 chhut-khi3 a3. Goa2 na7 u7 ki-hoe7 chiah koh kio3 li2 lai5.몯  26) Leng7-goa7 chit8 hong-bin7 i ia7 ki5-thai7 Po2-lo5 e7 siap chit8-koa2 chiN5 hou7 i, sou2-i2 i chaip8-chiap8 kio3 Po2-lo5 chhut-lai5, kap i tam5-lun7.
	27) Keng-koe3 nng7 ni5, Pho-kiu5 Hui-su7-tou chiap Hui-lek8-su7 e5 jim7 cho3 Chong2-tok. Hui-lek8-su7 ai3-boeh be2 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 hoan-sim, chiu7 ka7 Po2-lo5 ke3-siok8 kam3-kim3 toa3 kaN-gak8.

Te7 25 ChiuN

Po2-lo5 tui3 hong5-te3 siong7-sou3:
	1) Hui-su7-tou lai5-kau3 hit Seng2 chiu7-jim7 saN jit8 au7, chiu7 tui3 Kai-sat-li7-a chiuN7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.  2) Che3-si-tiuN2 kap Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 thau5-lang5, chiu7 khi3 i hia khong3-ko3 Po2-lo5.  3) In khun2-kiu5 Hui-su7-tou, pai3-thok i chiong Po2-lo5 sang3 lai5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, in-ui7 in i2-keng ke3-bou5 boeh bai5-hok8 toa3 poaN3-lou7 sat-hai7 i.  4) Hui-su7-tou in3 kong2: 몮Po2-lo5 pi7 kam3-kim3 ti7 Kai-sat-li7-a, goa2 ka-ti7 ia7 liam5-piN boeh tng2-khi3 hia.  5) Lin2 tiong-kan cho3 thau5-lang5 e5, kap goa2 cho3-hoe2 loh8-khi3 Kai-sat-li7-a. Hit e5 lang5 na7 u7 cho3 sim2-mih m7-tioh8, chiu7 thang ka7 i ko3.몯
	6) Hui-su7-tou toa3 in hia, put-ko3 toa3 chap8 jit8 peh jit8, chiu7 loh8-khi3 Kai-sat-li7-a. Keh-tng2 jit8 che7-tng5, beng7-leng7 lang5 chhoa7 Po2-lo5 jip8-lai5.  7) Po2-lo5 jip8-lai5 e5 si5, tui3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 loh8-lai5 e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5, chiu7 lai5 khia7 toa3 i e5 chiu-ui5, khai-si2 eng7 chin-che7 giam5-tiong7 e5 choe7-mia5 khong3-ko3 i, tan7-si7 long2 be7-tang3 theh8-chhut cheng3-ki3.  8) Po2-lo5 ui7 ka-ti7 pian7-hou7 kong2: 몮Tui3 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 Lut8-hoat, a2-si7 Seng3-tian7, a2-si7 Lo5-ma2 hong5-te3, goa2 long2 bo5 hoan7-tioh8 sim2-mih choe7.몯  9) Hui-su7-tou siuN7-boeh be2 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 hoan-sim, chiu7 mng7 Po2-lo5 kong2, 몮Li2 goan7-i3 chiuN7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, toa3 hia ui7-tioh8 chiah-e5 choe7-mia5 chai7 goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 siu7 sim2-phoaN3 bo5?몯  10) Po2-lo5 kong2: 몮Goa2 hian7-chai7 khia7 ti7 Kok-ha7 e5 sim2-phoaN3-teng5. Chia si7 goa2 eng-kai siu7 sim2-phoaN3 e5 sou2-chai7. Goa2 tui3 Iu5-thai3-lang5 peng7 bo5 cho3 sim2-mih m7-tioh8 e5 tai7-chi3. Che li2 ia7 beng5-beng5 chai-iaN2.  11) Goa2 na7 u7 cho3 sim2-mih m7-tioh8, u7 cho3 sim2-mih eng-kai siu7 si2-choe7 e5 tai7-chi3, goa2 si2 ia7 bo5 the-si5. Tan7-si7 chiah-e5 lang5 sou2 khong3-ko3 goa2 e5 tai7-chi3 na7 bo5 su7-sit8, chiu7 bo5 lang5 e7-tang3 chiong goa2 kau hou7 in. Goa2 boeh tui3 Hong5-te3 siong7-sou3.몯  12) Hui-su7-tou kap i e5 kou3-bun7 chham-siong5 liau2-au7, chiu7 in3 kong2, 몮Li2 ki3-jian5 tui3 Hong5-te3 siong7-sou3, chiu7 tioh8 khi3 Hong5-te3 hia.몯

Po2-lo5 chai7 A-ki-phaN3 kap Pek-ni5-ki e5 bin7-cheng5:
	13) Koe3 kui2-na7 jit8, A-ki-phaN3-ong5 kap Pek-ni5-ki lai5 Kai-sat-li7-a, ka7 Hui-su7-tou piau2 keng3-i3.  14) In toa3 hia toa3 chin-che7 jit8, chai7 chit e5 tiong-kan Hui-su7-tou chiu7 chiong Po2-lo5 e5 an3-kiaN7 ka7 kok-ong5 po3-ko3, kong2: 몮Ti7 chia u7 chit8 e5 Hui-lek8-su7 iau2-ku2 khau3-liu5 le3 e5 lang5;  15) goa2 khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 si5, Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 che3-si-tiuN2 kap tiuN2-lo2 ka7 i khong3-ko3, iau-kiu5 goa2 ka7 i teng7-choe7.  16) Tan7-si7 goa2 ka7 in kong2 pi7-ko3 kap goan5-ko3 na7 iau2-boe7 tng-bin7 tui3-chit, bo5 hou7 pi7-ko3 u7 pian7-hou7 e5 ki-hoe7 chiu7 ka7 i kau chhut-khi3 hou7 lang5 koaiN, che m7-si7 Lo5-ma2 lang5 e5 koan3-le7.  17) Sou2-i2 in chu7-chip8 lai5 chia e5 si5, goa2 chiu7 bo5 ian5-chhian5, keh-tng2 jit8 che7-tng5, beng7-leng7 lang5 chhoa7 hit e5 lang5 jip8-lai5.  18) Goan5-ko3 khia7 khi2-lai5 ka7 i ko3, tan7-si7 in sou2 ko3 e5 an3-kiaN7, bo5 chit8 hang7 chiau3 goa2 sou2 siuN7 e5 hiah-nih8 phaiN2.  19) In chi2-u7 kap i pian7-lun7 chit8-koa2 koan-he7 in ka-ti7 e5 chong-kau3 e5 bun7-te5, i2-kip8 koan-he7 Hit-ui7 Ia5-sou e5 tai7-chi3. In kong2 I i2-keng si2-khi3 a3, tan7-si7 Po2-lo5 chu2-tiuN kong2 I iau2 teh oah8.  20) Chiah-e5 bun5-te5 m7-chai tioh8 an3-choaN2 chhu2-li2, sou2-i2 goa2 mng7 Po2-lo5 khoaN3 i goan7-i3 chiuN7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, toa3 hia ui7-tioh8 chiah-e5 choe7-mia5 siu7 sim2-phoaN3 a2 m7.  21) Tan7-si7 Po2-lo5 siong7-sou3, chheng2-kiu5 goa2 lau5 i kau3 i e5 an3-kiaN7 hou7 Hong5-te3 chhai5-koat, goa2 chiu7 beng7-leng7 chiong i khau3-liu5 kau3 sang3 hou7 Hong5-te3.몯  22) A-ki-phaN3 ka7 Hui-su7-tou kong2, 몮Goa2 ka-ti7 ia7 chin ai3 thiaN chit e5 lang5 e5 pian7-hou7.몯 Hui-su7-tou in3 i kong2, 몮Li2 bin5-na2-chai3 chiu7 e7-tang3 thiaN i kong2.몯
	23) Keh-tng2 jit8, A-ki-phaN3 kap Pek-ni5-ki ui-hong lim2-lim2 kap lian5-tiuN2 i2-kip8 chhi7-lai7 e5 iau3-jin5 jip8-lai5 kong-hoe7-tng5. Hui-su7-tou ha7-leng7, Po2-lo5 chiu7 hou7 lang5 chhoa7 jip8-lai5.  24) Hui-su7-tou kong2: 몮A-ki-phaN3-ong5 i2-kip8 kap goan2 chai7-tiuN5 e5 chu-ui7. Lin2 khoaN3 chit e5 lang5: it-chhe3 e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5, bo5-lun7 si7 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 a2-si7 ti7 chia e5, long2 khun2-kiu5 goa2, hoah kong2 m7-thang koh hou7 i oah8.  25) Tan7-si7 goa2 be7-tang3 chhoe7-chhut i sou2 cho3 e5, u7 chit8 hang7 eng-kai siu7 si2-choe7 e5 tai7-chi3. Peng7-chhiaN2 i ka-ti7 tui3 Hong5-te3 siong7-sou3, sou2-i2 goa2 koat-teng7 boeh ka7 i sang3 khi3 hia.  26) Tan7-si7 koan-he7 chit e5 lang5, goa2 bo5 chit8 hang7 khak-teng7 e5 su7-sit8 thang chau3 Hong5-te3. Sou2-i2 goa2 chhoa7 i lai5 lin2 bin7-cheng5, --- Tek8-piat8 si7 chai7 A-ki-phaN3-ong5, li2 e5 bin7-cheng5, --- thang chai7 sim2-mng7 liau2-au7, goa2 e7-tang3 tit-tioh8 chit8-koa2 theng5-bun5 e5 chai5-liau7.  27) In-ui7 chiau3 goa2 khoaN3, ah-sang3 siu5-hoan7, na7 bo5 chi2-beng5 i e5 choe7-mia5, si7 bo5 hap8-li2 e5.

Te7 26 ChiuN

Po2-lo5 chai7 A-ki-phaN3 e5 bin7-cheng5 ui7 chu7-ki2 pian7-hou7:
	1) A-ki-phaN3 ka7 Po2-lo5 kong2, 몮In2-chun2 li2 ui7 ka-ti7 pian7-beng5.몯 Po2-lo5 chiu7 chhun-chhiu2 chhut-khi3, khai-si2 pian7-beng5, kong2:
	2) 몮A-ki-phaN3-ong5! Iu5-thai3-lang5 sou2 khong3-ko3 goa2 it-chhe3 e5 tai7-chi3, kin-na2-jit8 goa2 e7-tang3 toa3 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 pian7-beng5, kam2-kak chineng5-heng7.  3) Kai-chai3 in-ui7 li2 tui3 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 koan2-le7 kap in e5 bun7-te5, tek8-piat8 cheng-thong; sou2-i2 goa2 kiu5 li2 jim2-nai7 ka7 goa2 thiaN.몯
	4) 몮Goa2 chu7 siau3-lian5 i2-lai5, tui3 khi2-thau5 chai7 goa2 ka-ti7 e5 bin5-chok8 tiong i2-kip8 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, goa2 e5 chhu2(NN3)-se3 ui5-jin5 si7 sim2-mih khoan2 e5, sou2 u7 e5 Iu5-thai3-lang5 long2 chai-iaN2.  5) In chin cha2 chiu7 bat goa2. Ka2-su2 in na7 kheng2 cho3-cheng3, e7-tang3 ka7 goa2 cheng3-beng5 kong2 goa2 u7 chiau3 lan2 chong-kau3-tiong  choe3 giam5-keh e5 chit8 phai3, cho3 chit8 e5 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 teh seng-oah8.  6) Hian7-chai7 goa2 khia7 ti7 chia siu7 sim2-phoaN3, si7 in-ui7 goa2 u7 teh ki5-thai7 Siong7-chu2 tui3 lan2 e5 chou2-sian sou2 eng3-un2 e5 ---  7) chiu7-si7 lan2 chap8-ji7 chi-phai3 me5-jit8 jiat8-sim keng3-pai3 Siong7-chu2, ki5-thai7 e7-tang3 tit-tioh8 e5 eng3-un2. Ong5 a3, goa2 chiaN3-chiaN3 si7 ui7-tioh8 chit e5 ki5-thai7, chiah siu7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 khong3-ko3.  8) Siong7-chu2 hou7 si2-lang5 koh-oah8, lin2 IU5-thai3-lang5 an3-choaN2 khoaN3-cho3 si7 be7-tang3 siong-sin3 e5 tai7-chi3?몯
	9) 몮Goa2 i2-cheng5 ia7 bat siuN7-kong2 chin7 goa2 e5 lek8-liong7 lai5 hoan2-tui3 Na2-sat-lek8-lang5 Ia5-sou.  10) Goa2 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 chin-chiaN3 u7 an2-ne cho3. Goa2 tui3 che3-si-tiuN2 nia2-siu7 koan5-peng3, chiong chin-che7 Siong7-chu2 e5 chu2-bin5 koaiN-loh8 kaN-gak8; in pi7 teng7 si2-heng5 e5 si5, goa2 ia7 piau2-si7 chan3-tong5.  11) Goa2 ti7 kok hoe7-tng5 tiaN7-tiaN7 ka7 in chhu2-hoat8, kiong5-pek in kong2 siat-tok8 e5 oe7, hiong-beng2 ka7 in kong-kek, sim7-chi2 khi3-kau3 goa7-kok e5 siaN5-chhi7 ka7 in pek-hai7.몯

Po2-lo5 kong2-khi2 i an3-choaN2 lai5 kui Chu2: (Heng5-toan7 9:1-19; 22:6-16)
	12) 몮Ui7-tioh8 chit e5 bok8-tek, goa2 nia2-siu7 che3-si-tiuN2 e5 koan5-peng3 kap beng7-leng7 khi3 Tai7-ma2-sek.  13) Ong5 a3! Goa2 ti7 lou7-nih8, tu2 tiong-tau3 hit e5 si5, u7 khoaN3-kiN3 pi2 thai3-iong5 koh-khah kiong5 e5 kng tui3 thiN-teng2 hoat-sia7 loh8-lai5 chio3 goa2, i2-kip8 chio3 goa2 e5 tang5-phoaN7 e5 chiu-ui5.  14) Goan2 long2 poah8 loh8-khi3 thou5-kha e5 si5, goa2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 chit8 e5 siaN, eng7 Hi-pek-lai5-oe7 ka7 goa2 kong2, 몬So3-lo5, So3-lo5! Li2 an3-choaN2 ka7 Goa2 pek-hai7? Li2 an2-ne cho3 tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 gu5 khi3 that chu2-lang5 u7 chhi3 e5 kun3-na2, si7 ka-ti7 teh siong-hai7 ka-ti7.몭  15) Goa2 mng7 kong2, 몬Chu2 a3! Li2 si7 sim2-mih lang5?몭 chu2 in3 kong2: 몬goa2 chiu7-si7 li2 sou2 pek-hai7 e5 Ia5-sou.  16) TaN li2 tioh8 khi2-lai5 khia7 le7; Goa2 hian2-hian7 hou7 li2 khoaN3, si7 ui7-tioh8 boeh soan2-phai3 li2 lai5 hong7-su7, lai5 ui7-tioh8 li2 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5, i2-kip8 goa2 chiong-lai5 boeh hian2-si7 hou7 li2 khoaN3 e5 i7-siong7 lai5 cho3 kian3-cheng3.  17) Goa2 e7 tui3 I2-sek-liat8-lang5 kap Goa7-pang-lang5 e5 tiong-kan ka7 li2 kiu3 chhut-lai5. TaN Goa2 boeh chhe-phai3 li2 khi3 Goa7-pang-lang5 hia.  18) Li2 tioh8 khui in e5 bak8-chiu, hou7 in tui3 ou-am3 choan2-jip8 kong-beng5, tui3 Sat-tan3 e5 koan5-se3 lai5 kui-hiong3 Siong7-chu2, thong-koe3 tui3 Goa2 e5 sin3-giong2, in e7 tit-tioh8 sia3-choe7, ia7 e7 kap Siong7-chu2 sou2 keng2-soan2 e5 chu2-bin5, hun-hiong2 Siong7-chu2 soan2-bin5 e5 tek8-koan5.몭몯

Po2-lo5 tin5-sut8 i e5 kang-chok:
	19) 몮A-ki-phaN3-ong5 a3, sou2-i2 goa2 bo5 ui5-poe7 tui3 thiN-teng2 lai5 e5 i7-siong7.  20) Tai7-seng ti7 Tai7-ma2-sek, au7-lai5 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, jian5-au7 ti7 Iu5-thai3 choan5-te7, i2-kip8 ti7 Goa7-pang-lang5 e5 tiong-kan tui3 lang5 thoan5-to7, kio3 in tioh8 hoe2-kai2 lai5 kui hiong3 Siong7-chu2, tioh8 eng7 heng5-tong7 lai5 cheng3-beng5 in chin-chiaN3 u7 hoe2-kai2.  21) Ui7-tioh8 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3, Iu5-thai3-lang5 ti7 seng3-tian7 lai7 ka7 goa2 liah8-khi3, siuN7-boeh ka7 goa2 thai5-si2.  22) Tan7-si7 kau3 kin-na2-jit8, goa2 ke3-siok8 siu7 Siong7-chu2 e5 po2-hou7, sou2-i2 goa2 khia7 ti7 chia, tui3 chun-kui3-e5 kap pi-bi5-e5 cho3 kian3-cheng3. Goa2 sou2 kong2 e5, to si7 kap tai7-gian5-jin5 i2-kip8 Mou5-se kong2 e7 hoat-seng e5 tai7-chi3 oan5-choan5 kang7-khoan2:  23) chiu7-si7 kong2 Bi2-sai3-a it-teng7 tioh8 siu7 khou2-lan7, peng7-chhiaN2 I si7 tui3 si2-lang5 tiong koh-oah8 khi2-lai5 e5 thau5 chit8 e5, I e7 thoan5 kong-beng5 e5 sin3-sek hou7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 kap Goa7-pang-lang5.몯
	24) Po2-lo5 an2-ne ui7 ka-ti7 pian7-hou7 e5 si5, Hui-su7-tou toa7-siaN kong2, 몮Po2-lo5, li2 teh khi2-siau2! Hak8-bun7 siuN koan5 soah hou7 li2 piN3-cho3 khi2-siau2-e5!몯  25) Po2-lo5 in3 kong2: 몮Hui-su7-tou Kok-ha7, goa2 m7-si7 khi2-siau2-e5! Goa2 sou2 kong2 e5 si7 chin-sit8 koh cheng3-siong5 e5 oe7.  26) A-ki-phaN3-ong5 a3, in-ui7 Pe3-ha7 chai-iaN2 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3, sou2-i2 goa2 chiah kaN2 tui3 Pe3-ha7 ho2-taN2 siong7-sou3. Goa2 khak-sin3 Ong5 tui3 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 tak8-hang7 to chin beng5-pek8, in-ui7 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 m7-si7 ti7 phian-phiah e5 sou2-chai7 cho3 e5.  27) A-ki-phaN3-ong5 a3, li2 u7 sin3 Siong7-chu2 e5 tai7-gian5-jin5 bo5? Goa2 chai-iaN2 li2 u7 sin3!몯  28) A-ki-phaN3 tuiP3o-lo5 kong2, 몮Li2 hiah-nih8 kan2-tan chiu7 siuN7-boeh khoan3-hok8 goa2 cho3 Ki-tok-tou5!몯  29) Po2-lo5 in3 kong2, 몮Bo5-lun7 kan2-tan a2-si7 bo5 kan2-tan, goa2 ki5-kiu5 Siong7-chu2 put-tan7 hou7 Pe3-ha7 pun2-sin, ia7 hou7 kin-na2-jit8 it-chhe3 thiaN goa2 kong2 e5 lang5, ti5-liau2 hou7 lang5 eng7 lian7-a2 lian7 i2-goa7, long2 e7 kap goa2 kang7-khoan2.몯
	30) Chit e5 si5, Ong5 kap Chong2-tok kap Pek-ni5-ki, i2-kip8 chai7-cho7 e5 lang5 long2 khia7 khi2-lai5,  31) the3 chhut-khi3 liau2-au7, hou7-siong tam5-lun7 kong2, 몮Chit e5 lang5 peng7 bo5 hoan7-tioh8 sim2-mih eng-kai siu7 si2-heng5 a2-si7 tou7-heng5 e5 choe7.몯  32) A-ki-phaN3 ka7 Hui-su7-tou kong2, 몮Chit e5 lang5 na7 bo5 tui3 Hong5-te3 siong7-sou3, cha2-cha2 chiu7 e7-tang3 ka7 i sek-hong3 a3.몯

Te7 27 ChiuN

Po2-lo5 che7-chun5 khi3 Lo5-ma2:
	1) Chit8-e7 koat-teng7 kong2 goan2 tioh8 che7-chun5 khi3 I3-tai7-li7 e5 si5, Po2-lo5 kap leng7-goa7 kui2-na7 e5 siu5-hoan7, chiu7 hou7 lang5 kau hou7 Hong5-ka-kun Se-pa-su7-tok-iaN5 e5 lian5-tiuN2, mia5 kio3-cho3 Iu5-liu5.  2) U7 chit8 chiah tui3 A-tai7-bi2-tian5 lai5 e5 chun5, boeh sun7 A-se-a ian5-hai2 e5 kang2-khau2 kiaN5, goan2 chiu7 che7 hit chiah chun5 chhut-phang5. Tui3 Thiap-sat-lo5-ni5-ka lai5 e5 Ma2-ki5-tun3-lang5 A-li2-tat8-kou2 ia7 kap goan2 cho3-hoe2 khi3.  3) Keh-tng2 jit8, goan2 chiu7 kau3 Se-tun3. Iu5-liu5 chin chhin-chhiat tui3-thai7 Po2-lo5, chun2 i khi3 kiN3 i e5 peng5-iu2, siu7 in e5 ho2 khoan2-thai7.  4) Goan2 tui3 hia koh khui-chun5, in-ui7 chiN3-hong, goan2 chiu7 sun7 Ku-pi2-lou7-tou2(NNto2) siam2-hong e5 sou2-chai7 kiaN5.  5) Jian5-au7 goan2 keng-koe3 Ki-li7-ka kap Pong5-hui-li7-a e5 goa7-hai2, lai5 kau3 Lu7-ka e5 Mui2-lah.  6) Ti7 hia lian5-tiuN2 chhoe7 tioh8 chit8 chiah tui3 A-lek8-san-tai7 lai5 e5 chun5, boeh khi3 I3-tai7-li7, i chiu7 kio3 goan2 che7 hit chiah chun5.
	7) Chun5 kiaN5 chin ban7, kiaN5 kui2-na7 jit8 chiah lai5-kau3 Kek-ni5-thou2 e5 kang2-goa7. In-ui7 hou7 hong chou2-tong3, goan2 chiu7 sun7 Kek-li2-ti2-tou2(NNto2) siam2-hong e5 sou2-chai7 kiaN5, tui3 Sat-mou5-ni5 keng-koe3.  8) Goan2 sun7 hai2-kiN5 kiaN5, bian2-kiong2 lai5-kau3 chit8 e5 sou2-chai7 kio3-cho3 몮An-choan5-kang2,몯 li7 Lah-se-a-siaN5 bo5 loa7 hng7.
	9) Ti7 hia tam-gou7 chin-che7 jit8, lian5 Kim3-chiah8 e5 cheh-ki5 ia7 koe3-khi3 a3, boeh koh kiaN5-chun5 i2-keng chin gui5-hiam2 a3, Po2-lo5 chiu7 khng3 in kong2:  10) 몮Kok-ui7, goa2 khoaN3 lan2 na7 boeh ke3-siok8 kiaN5-chun5 e7 chin gui5-hiam2; m7-na7 hoe3-but8 kap chun5 e7 siu7 toa7 sun2-hai7, lian5 lan2 e5 seN3-mia7 ia7 e7 sit-loh8 khi3.몯  11) Tan7-si7 lian5-tiuN2 siong-sin3 chun5-tiuN2 kap chun5-chu2 e5 oe7, m7 siong-sin3 Po2-lo5 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7.  12) Iu7-koh in-ui7 chai7 chit e5 kang2-khau2 koe3 tang-thiN bo5 sek-hap8; toa7 pou7-hun7 e5 lang5 to siuN7 ai3 khui-chun5 li7-khui chit e5 sou2-chai7, khoaN3 e7-tang3 khi3-kau3 Hui-ni5-ki koe3 tang-thiN be7. Hui-ni5-ki si7 Kek-li2-ti2-tou2 e5 chit8 e5 kang2-khau2, chit8 bin7 ng3 sai-pak, chit8 bin7 ng3 sai-lam5.

Tu2-tioh8 toa7 hong-eng2:
