	13) Hit e5 si5 lam5-hong bi5-bi5-a2 chhoe-lai5, in chiu7 siuN7-kong2 in e7-tang3 tat8-tioh8 bok8-tek chiu7 khi2-tiaN3, chin7-liong7 sun7 Kek-li2-ti2-tou2 e5 hai2-kiN5 kiaN5.  14) Tan7-si7 liam5-piN u7 chit8 chun7 toa7-hong --- kio3-cho3 몮Tang-pak e5 hong-thai몯 --- tui3 hit e5 tou2(NNto2) sau3 loh8-lai5.  15) Chun5 hou7 hong chit8-e7 phah, chiu7 be7-tang3 ng3 hong-thau5 sai2, goan2 chiu7 pang3 i phiau-liu5.  16) KiaN5 lai5-kau3 chit8 e5 sio2 tou2(NNto2), kio3-cho3 Ko-tai7 e5 lam5-peng5 siam2 hong e5 sou2-chai7, goan2 kiong5-kiong5 siu sam-pan2 khi2-lai5.  17) In chiong sam-pan2 thoa khi2-lai5 liau2-au7, chiu7 eng7 toa7-soh khun2 hit chiah chun5, ia7 kiaN-liau2 ti7 Sai3-ni5-ti2 e5 hai2-phiaN5 kho3-chhian2; chiu7 loh8 phang5, chhut-chai7 i khi3 phiau-liu5.  18) Goan2 hou7 hong-eng2 phah kah chin li7-hai7, sou2-i2 keh-tng2 jit8, cheng3-lang5 chiu7 khai-si2 chiong chai3 ti7 chun5-nih8 e5 hoe3-but8 hiat loh8-khi3 hai2-nih8.  19) Te7 saN jit8, in koh chhin-chhiu2 chiong chun5 e5 khi3-ku7 hiat-tiau7.  20) Kui2-na7 jit8 ku2, goan2 ia7 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 jit8-thau5, ia7 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 chheN; hong-eng2 ke3-siok8 phah kah chin li7-hai7. choe3-au7 goan2 tit-kiu3 e5 hi-bong7 to siau-sit khi3.
	21) Cheng3-lang5 chin ku2 long2 bo5 chiah8, Po2-lo5 chiu7 khia7 toa3 in e5 bin7-cheng5 kong2: 몮Kok-ui7, lin2 hit e5 si5 na7 thiaN goa2 e5 oe7, na7 mai2 khui-chun5 li7-khui Kek-li2-ti2-tou2(NNto2), chiu7 be7 tu2-tioh8 chit khoan2 e5 siong-hai7 kap sun2-sit.  22) Tan7-si7 taN goa2 khng3 lin2 theh8-chhut iong2-khi3! Lin2 bo5 lang5 e7 sit-loh8 seN3-mia7; chi2-u7 e7 sit-loh8 chit chiah-chun5.  23) In-ui7 chang-am3, u7 chit8 ui7 goa2 sou2 siok8 sou2 keng3-pai3 e5 Siong7-chu2 e5 thian-sai3, lai5 khia7 toa3 goa2 e5 piN-a,  24) kong2, 몬Po2-lo5, m7-bian2 kiaN, li2 tioh8 khi3 khia7 toa3 Hong5-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5; peng7-chhiaN2 Siong7-chu2 ia7 i2-keng siuN2-su3 li2 i2-kip8 kap li2 che7-chun5 chiah-e5 lang5 e7-tang3 tit-tioh8 an-choan5.몭  25) Sou2-i2 chhiaN2 lin2 tai7-ke theh8-chhut iong2-khi3! In-ui7 goa2 sin3-kho3 Siong7-chu2, it-chhe3 e5 tai7-chi3 e7 chiau3 I sou2 kong2 e5 an2-ne sit8-hian7.  26) Tan7-si7 lan2 it-teng7 e7 hou7 hong phah khit-khi3 chit8 e5 tou2(NNto2).몯
	27) Kau3 te7 chap8-si3 jit8 e5 am3-si5, goan2 ti7 A-ti2-a-hai2 hou7 hong-thai phah-lai5 phah-khi3. Chha-put-to poaN3-me5, kiaN5-chun5-e5 siuN7-cho3 si7 oa2-kin7 liok8-te7 a7.  28) In chiu7 tan3 ian5-thui7 loh8-khi3 niu5, chai-iaN2 u7 chap8-ji7 tng7 chhim; koh khi3 khah hng7 koh niu5 chit8-e7 khoaN3-bai7 le3, u7 kau2 tng7 chhim.  29) KiaN-liau2 chun5 e7 le3-tioh8 toa7-chioh8, chiu7 tui3 chun5-boe2 pha si3 e5 tiaN3 loh8-khi3, chiu7 ki5-to2 koaN2-kin2 e7-tang3 thiN-kng.  30) KiaN5-chun5-e5 siuN7-boeh tui3 chun5 to5-chau2; pang3 sam-pan2 loh8-khi3 hai2-nih8, ke2 cho3 boeh tui3 chun5-thau5 pha-tiaN3.  31) Tan7-si7 Po2-lo5 tui3 lian5-tiuN2 kap peng-a2 kong2, 몮Chiah-e5 lang5 na7 bo5 lau5 toa3 chun5-teng2, lin2 be7-tang3 tit-tioh8 kiu3.몯  32) Peng-a2 chiu7 cham7-tng7 pak8 sam-pan2 e5 toa7-soh, pang3 i lau5 khi3.
	33) ThiN teh-boeh kng e5 si5, Po2-lo5 khou2-khng3 cheng3-lang5 tioh8 chiah8, kong2: 몮Lin2 tai7-ke i2-keng tan2 chap8-si3 jit8 ku2 a3. Chit e5 tiong-kan long2 bo5 chiah8 poaN3 hang7.  34) Sou2-i2 goa2 khou2-khng3 lin2 tioh8 chiah8 chit8-koa2 a2; lin2 chiah u7 khui3-lat8 thang oah8. Lin2 bo5 lang5 e7 sit-loh8 kah chit8 ki thau5-mng5.몯  35) Po2-lo5 kong2 chiah-e5 oe7 liau2-au7, chiu7 theh8 mi7-pau, toa3 cheng3-lang5 bin7-cheng5 kam2-sia7 Siong7-chu2, peh-khui chiu7 chiah8.  36) An2-ne cheng3-lang5 chiu7 hoe-hok8 iong2-khi3, khai-si2 chiah8.  37) Goan2 ti7 chun5-nih8 e5 lang5, long2-chong2 u7 nng7-pah chhit-chap8-lak8 e5.  38) In long2 chiah8-pa2 liau2-au7, chiu7 chiong beh8-a2 tan3-loh8 hai2, lai5 hou7 chun5 khah khin.

Chun5 phoa3-khi3:
	39) Kau3 thiN-kng, sai2-chun5-e5 m7 chai-iaN2 si7 ti7 tah chit8 e5 hai2-hoaN7, tan7-si7 in khoaN3-kiN3 chit e5 hai2-oan u7 hai2-phiaN5, chiu7 siuN7-kong2 khoaN3 e7-tang3 sai2-chun5 jip8-khi3 hia kho3-phiaN5 a2-be7.  40) In chiu7 cham7-tng7 tiaN3-soh, chiong tiaN3 pang3 toa3 hai2-te2, kang7-si5 ia7 thau2-khui pak8 chun5-toa7 e5 soh, jian5-au7 tiau3 cheng5-phang5 khi2-lai5, sun7-hong hiong3 hai2-hoaN7 sai2-khi3.  41) Tan7-si7 chun5 long3-tioh8 soaN-phiaN5 soah kho3-chhian2; chun5-thau5 ka7 tiau5-le7, be7 tin2-tang7, chun5-boe2 hou7 toa7-eng2 phah hai7-khi3.
	42) Peng-a2 kiaN-liau2 siu5-hoan7 siu5-chui2 to5-chau2 khi3, siuN7-boeh ka7 in thai5-si2.  43) Tan7-si7 lian5-tiuN2 siuN7-boeh kiu3 Po2-lo5, chiu7 chou2-tong3 in chit e5 ke3-oe7. I beng7-leng7 e7 siu5-chui2 e5 lang5, tai7-seng thiau3 loh8-khi3 chui2-nih8, siu5 khit-khi3 hoaN7-teng2;  44) ki5-tha e5 lang5 khip8 toa3 pang-nih8 a2-si7 chun5-teng2 e7 phu5 e5 mih8-kiaN7 chiuN7-hoaN7. An2-ne goan2 tai7-ke long2 an-choan5 chiuN7-liok8.

Te7 28 ChiuN

Chai7 Bi2-li7-tai7:
	1) Goan2 an-choan5 chiuN7-liok8 liau2-au7, chiah chai-iaN2 hit e5 tou2(NNto2) kio3-cho3 Bi2-li7-tai7.  2) Ti7 hia e5 thou2-lang5 tek8-piat8 ho2-i3 khoan2-thai7 goan2. In-ui7 hit e5 si5 tu2 teh loh8-hou7, ia7 chin koaN5, in chiu7 khi2-hoe2 chiap-thai7 goan2 tai7-ke.  3) Po2-lo5 khioh chit8 khun2 chha5, thiN loh8-khi3 hoe2-nih8 e5 si5, u7 chit8 boe2 tok8-choa5 hou7 hoe2-khi3 hahN(NNhaN8h)-tioh8, so5 chhut-lai5 tiN5 toa3 i e5 chhiu2-nih8.  4) Thou2-lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 hit boe2 tok8-choa5 tiau3 ti7 Po2-lo5 e5 chhiu2-nih8 chiu7 hou7-siong kong2, 몮Chit e5 lang5 it-teng7 si7 hiong-siu2, sui-jian5 tui3 hai2-nih8 to5-seng, thian-li2 ia7 m7 iong5-un2 i oah8.몯  5) Tan7-si7 Po2-lo5 chiong hit boe2 tok8-choa5 hiu3 loh8-khi3 hoe2-nih8, long2 bo5 siu7-siong.  6) Thou2-lang5 teh theng3-hau7 i cheng2 khi2-lai5 a2-si7 hut-jian5-kan to2 loh8-khi3 si2. Tan7-si7 theng3-hau7 chin ku2, bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 hoat-seng sim2-mih koh-iuN7 e5 tai7-chi3, in chiu7 kai2-pian3 siuN7-hoat, kong2, 몮I si7 sin5!몯
	7) Li7 hit e5 sou2-chai7 bo5 loa7 hng7, u7 chit8-koa2 thou2-te7 si7 siok8 ti7 chit e5 tou2(NNto2) e5 thau5-lang5 Pou7-pek-liu5 e5. I hoan-geng5 goan2 khi3 toa3 in hia, chhin-chhiat khoan2-thai7 goan2 saN jit8 ku2.  8) Hit e5 si5 Pou7-pek-liu5 e5 lau7-pe7 tu2-tu2 tioh8 jiat8-cheng3 kap chhiah-li7, to2 ti7 bin5-chhng5. Po2-lo5 jip8-khi3 i e5 pang5-keng the3 i ki5-to2, ka7 i an3-chhiu2, chiu7 ka7 i i-ho2 khi3.  9) U7 chit e5 tai7-chi3 liau2-au7, chai7 chit e5 tou2(NNto2)-siong7 ki5-tha it-chhe3 e5 peN7-lang5, ia7 lai5 i hia hou7 i i-ho2 khi3.  10) In tui3 goan2 piau2-si7 chap8-hun e5 chun-keng3. Goan2 boeh khui-chun5 e5 si5, in chiong goan2 sou2 su-iau3 e5 mih8-kiaN7 ka7 goan2 sang3 lai5-kau3 chun5-nih8.

Tui3 Bi2-li7-tai7 khi3 Lo5-ma2:
	11) SaN kou2(NNko3)-goeh8 au7, goan2 che7 chit8 chiah ti7 chit e5 tou2(NNto2) koe3 tang-thiN, kio3-cho3 몮Siang-seN-a2 Sin5몯 e5 A-lek8-san-tai7 e5 chun5 chhut-phang5.  12) kau3 Su7-lah-kou2, toa3 hia theng5-liu5 saN jit8.  13) Tui3 hia chhut-phang5, seh8 khi3-kau3 Li7-ki5-ong. In-ui7 keh-tng2 jit8 thau3 lam5-hong, goan2 nng7 jit8 kan chiu7 lai5-kau3 Pou7-tiu-li7.  14) Goan2 ti7 hia tu2-tioh8 Ki-tok-tou5 e5 hiaN-ti7. In chhiaN2 goan2 cho3-hoe2 toa3 chhit jit8, jian5-au7 goan2 chiu7 lai5-kau3 Lo5-ma2.  15) Toa3 ti7 Lo5-ma2 e5 Ki-tok-tou5 e5 hiaN-ti7 thiaN-kiN3 goan2 e5 siau-sit, chiu7 lai5-kau3 A-pi2-ou e5 chhi7-tiuN5 kap 몮Sam-koan2몯 e5 sou2-chai7 geng5-chiap goan2. Po2-lo5 kiN3-tioh8 in e5 si5, kam2-sia7 Siong7-chu2, chiu7 chong3-taN2 khi2-lai5.

Chai7 Lo5-ma2:
	16) Goan2 kau3 Lo5-ma2 e5 si5, in in2-chun2 Po2-lo5 kap chit8 e5 khan3-siu2 i e5 peng, leng7-goa7 kap i cho3-hoe2 toa3.
	17) SaN jit8 au7, Po2-lo5 chhiaN2 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 thau5-lang5 lai5. In chu7-chip8 e5 si5, i chiu7 tui3 in kong2: 몮Chu-ui7 hiaN-ti7, goa2 bo5 cho3 sim2-mih tui3-put-khi2 lan2 e5 tong5-pau a2-si7 ui5-poe7 lan2 chou2-sian e5 koan3-le7 e5 tai7-chi3; tan7-si7 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, hou7 lang5 khoaN3-cho3 siu5-hoan7 kau hou7 Lo5-ma2-lang5 e5 chhiu2.  18) In sim2-mng7 goa2 liau2-au7, khoaN3 goa2 bo5 hoan7-tioh8 sim2-mih eng-kai siu7-si2 e5 choe7, siuN7-boeh pang3 goa2 khi3.  19) Tan7-si7 in-ui7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 hoan2-tui3, goa2 put-tek-i2 chiah tui3 Hong5-te3 siong7-sou3. Goa2 peng7 m7-si7 siuN7-boeh khong3-ko3 goa2 e5 tong5-pau.  20) In-ui7 an2-ne, goa2 chiah chhiaN2 lin2 lai5 kiN3-bin7 tam5-lun7; goa2 chiu7-si7 ui7-tioh8 I2-sek-liat8-lang5 sou2 giong2-bong7 Hit-ui7, chiah hou7 chit tiau5 lian7-a2 lian7-le7.몯  21) In tui3 i kong2: 몮Goan2 bo5 chih-tioh8 tui3 Iu5-thai3 lai5 e5 phe kong2-khi2 li2 e5 tai7-chi3, ia7 bo5 poaN3 e5 tui3 hia lai5 e5 hiaN-ti7 ka7 goan2 po3-ko3 sim2-mih siau-sit, a2-si7 kong2 li2 e5 phaiN2-oe7.  22) Tan7-si7 goan2 chin ai3 thiaN khoaN3 li2 e5 kian3-kai2 si7 an3-choaN2, in-ui7 goan2 chai-iaN2 to3-chhu3 lang5 to si7 teh hoan2-tui3 li2 sou2 siok8 chit e5 kau3-phai3.몯
	23) In kap Po2-lo5 iok-teng7 chit8 e5 jit8-chi2. Hit jit8 chiu7 u7 chin-che7 lang5 lai5-kau3 Po2-lo5 teh toa3 e5 sou2-chai7. Tui3 chai2-khi2-si5 kau3 am3-si5, Po2-lo5 ka7 in soat-beng5, ia7 tui3 in kian3-cheng3 koan-he7 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok e5 to7-li2, in2-iong7 Mou5-se e5 Lut8-hoat kap tai7-gian5-jin5 e5 chheh, khoan3-to7 in sin3 Ia5-sou.  24) U7 lang5 sin3 Po2-lo5 sou2 kong2 chiah-e5 oe7, u7 lang5 m7 sin3.  25) In e5 tiong-kan hou7-siong i3-kian3 be7 hah8, boeh li7-khui e5 si5, Po2-lo5 koh kong2 chit8 ku3 oe7, kong2: 몮Seng3 Leng5 thok tai7-gian5-jin5 I2-sai3-a, tui3 lin2 e5 chou2-sian kong2 e5 oe7, kong2 liau2 chin tioh8.  26) I kong2:
몬Li2 khi3 ka7 chit e5 bin5-chok8 kong2: Lin2 thiaN sit8-chai7 u7 teh thiaN, tan7-si7 long2 be7 liau2-kai2; Lin2 khoaN3 u7 chu3-i3 teh khoaN3, tan7-si7 long2 be7 beng5-pek8.  27) In-ui7 chit e5 bin5-chok8 e5 sim piN3-cho3 chin tun7; In e5 hiN7-khang piN3-cho3 chin tang7, In e5 bak8-chiu pang3 kheh-kheh, KiaN-liau2 in e5 bak8-chiu u7 khoaN3-kiN3, In e5 hiN7-khang u7 thiaN-kiN3, In e5 sim e7 li2-kai2, In e7 hoe2-kai2, Lai5 hou7 Goa2 ka7 in i-ho2 khi3.몭몯
28) Po2-lo5 iu7-koh kong2: 몮Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8-ai3 chai-iaN2 chit e5 Siong7-chu2 chin2-kiu3 e5 sin3-sek i2-keng thoan5 kau3 Goa7-pang-lang5 hia khi3 a3. In e7 thiaN-chiong5 chit e5 sin3-sek!몯  ( 29) Po2-lo5 kong2 chiah-e5 oe7 liau2-au7, Iu5-thai3-lang5 gi7-lun7 hun-hun, chiu7 li7-khui khi3.)
	30) Po2-lo5 toa3 i sou2 chou e5 chhu3 toa3 nng7 ni5, it-chhe3 lai5 hong2-bun7 e5 lang5, i long2 ka7 in hoan-geng5.  31) I toa7-taN2 chu7-iu5 chu7-chai7 soan-iong5 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok, ka3-si7 koan-he7 Chu2 Ia5-sou Ki-tok e5 tai7-chi3.
